/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[fn_Strip]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[fn_Strip] 
	(@InString varchar(4000), 
	 @Char varchar(1) = ' ')
RETURNS varchar(4000) 
AS
BEGIN
	SELECT @InString = REPLACE(@InString,@Char,'')
	RETURN (@InString)
END
GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[RemoveHTML]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
Create function [dbo].[RemoveHTML] (@intro varchar(200))
RETURNS varchar(200)
AS
BEGIN
            declare @leftbracket char(1)
            declare @rightbracket char(1)
            declare @resultstring varchar(200)
            declare @remainingString varchar(200)
            declare @openbracketposition tinyint
            declare @closebracketposition tinyint
            set @leftbracket = '<'
            set @rightbracket = '>'
            set @resultstring = ''
            set @remainingString = @intro
            while len(@remainingString) > 0
            begin
                        set @openbracketposition = charindex(@leftbracket, @remainingString)
                        if @openbracketposition > 0
                        begin
                                    set @resultstring = @resultstring + left(@remainingString, @openbracketposition - 1)
                                    set @remainingString = substring(@remainingString, @openbracketposition, 200)
                                    set @closebracketposition = charindex(@rightbracket, @remainingString)
                                    if @closebracketposition > 0
                                                set @remainingString = substring(@remainingString, @closebracketposition + 1, 00)
                                    else
                                                set @remainingString = ''
                        end
                        else
                        begin
                                    set @resultstring = @resultstring + @remainingString
                        	    set @remainingString = ''
                        end
            end
RETURN @resultstring
END
GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[TRIM]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date, ,>
-- Description:	<Description, ,>
-- =============================================

CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[TRIM](@string VARCHAR(MAX))
 RETURNS VARCHAR(MAX)
 BEGIN
 RETURN LTRIM(RTRIM(@string))
 END

/****** Object:  View [dbUser].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_THREAD_COUNT_V]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbUser].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_THREAD_COUNT_V]
AS
SELECT     Q_FORUM_ID, COUNT(Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID) AS THREADCOUNT
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
WHERE     (TOPIC_STARTER = 1) OR
                      (Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = 0)
GROUP BY Q_FORUM_ID
GO

SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V]
AS
SELECT     dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID, COUNT(dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_T.Q_BLOG_ID) AS COMMENT_COUNT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_T LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_T ON dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_T.Q_BLOG_ID
GROUP BY dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID
GO

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[Q_BLOG_MAX_DATE_V]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[Q_BLOG_MAX_DATE_V]
AS
SELECT DISTINCT TOP 100 PERCENT MAX(dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE) AS maxdate, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID, dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.USER_ID
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T ON dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
WHERE     (dbo.Q_BLOG_T.PUBLISH = 1)
GROUP BY dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID, dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.USER_ID
ORDER BY maxdate DESC
GO

 CONSTRAINT [PK_Q_FORUM_T] PRIMARY KEY NONCLUSTERED

	[Q_FORUM_ID] ASC

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_V]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_V]
AS
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_SUBJECT, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_LAST_POST, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_REPLY_COUNT_V.NUMBEROFREPLIES, dbo.Q_FORUM_T.Q_FORUM_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_T.Q_FORUM_NAME
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_T ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_T.Q_FORUM_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_REPLY_COUNT_V ON 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_REPLY_COUNT_V.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID
WHERE     (dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID IS NULL) OR
                      (dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = 0)
ORDER BY dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_LAST_POST DESC
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[Q_FORUM_VIEW_V] AS
SELECT USERS_T.USERNAME, USERS_T.USER_ID, Q_FORUM_T.Q_FORUM_ID, Q_FORUM_T.Q_FORUM_NAME, Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_SUBJECT, Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_DATE, Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID, Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_MESSAGE
FROM USERS_T INNER JOIN (Q_FORUM_T INNER JOIN Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T ON Q_FORUM_T.Q_FORUM_ID = Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_ID) ON USERS_T.USER_ID = Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.USER_ID
GO

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[Q_USER_ARTICLE_COUNT_BY_MONTH_V]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[Q_USER_ARTICLE_COUNT_BY_MONTH_V]
AS
SELECT     COUNT(dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.Q_ARTICLE_ID) AS ARTICLE_COUNT, dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.USER_ID, COUNT(dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.Q_ARTICLE_ID) 
                      * 5 AS ARTICLE_POINTS, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME
FROM         dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID
WHERE     (dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.DISPLAY = 1) AND (MONTH(dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.DATE_CREATED) = MONTH(GETDATE())) AND 
                      (YEAR(dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.DATE_CREATED) = YEAR(GETDATE()))
GROUP BY dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[ALT_MP3_T_UPDATE_SP]
	( @ALT_MP3_ID int = 0
	, @IP varchar(50) = null
	, @CONNECTION varchar(50) = null
	)

			, CONNECTION = @CONNECTION
		where 
			ALT_MP3_ID = @ALT_MP3_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[ARTICLE_T_PAGE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
Create Procedure [dbo].[ARTICLE_T_PAGE_SP]
@PageSize int,  
@CurrentPage int,        
@ItemCount int output     
AS 
Declare @UpperBand int, @LowerBand int
-- Get The Count Of The Rows That They Meet the Criteria 
SET @ItemCount = (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ARTICLE_T)    
-- Calculate the @LowerCount and @UpperCount    
SET @LowerBand  = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize    
SET @UpperBand  = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize) + 1   
-- -- create a temporaty table     
CREATE TABLE #AllRows(             
RowNumber int IDENTITY, 
	ID int,
	thefile nvarchar(50),
	Title nvarchar(50),
	Date_d datetime,
	Source nvarchar(50),
	display int,
	Cat_id int,
	User_id int,
	PUBLICATION_DATE smalldatetime,
	EXACT int)
   -- INSERT ALL THE Rows that meets the Criteria 
	 INSERT INTO #AllRows ( 		[ID],
		[thefile],
		[Title],
		[Date_d],
		[Source],
		[display],
		[Cat_id],
		[User_id],
		[PUBLICATION_DATE],
		[EXACT])
	 select distinct  			[ID],
			[thefile],
			[Title],
			[Date_d],
			[Source],
			[display],
			[Cat_id],
			[User_id],
			[PUBLICATION_DATE],
			[EXACT]
	From ARTICLE_T
	ORDER BY [ID] ASC 
	  -- AND finally select and return desired -Paged- Rows  
	 SELECT RowNumber ,
		[ID],
		[thefile],
		[Title],
		[Date_d],
		[Source],
		[display],
		[Cat_id],
		[User_id],
		[PUBLICATION_DATE],
		[EXACT] FROM #AllRows WHERE RowNumber > @LowerBand AND RowNumber < @UpperBand RETURN
GO

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[AspNet_SqlCacheRegisterTableStoredProcedure]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[AspNet_SqlCacheRegisterTableStoredProcedure] 
             @tableName NVARCHAR(450) 
         AS
         BEGIN

         DECLARE @triggerName AS NVARCHAR(3000) 
         DECLARE @fullTriggerName AS NVARCHAR(3000)
         DECLARE @canonTableName NVARCHAR(3000) 
         DECLARE @quotedTableName NVARCHAR(3000) 

         /* Create the trigger name */ 
         SET @triggerName = REPLACE(@tableName, '[', '__o__') 
         SET @triggerName = REPLACE(@triggerName, ']', '__c__') 
         SET @triggerName = @triggerName + '_AspNet_SqlCacheNotification_Trigger' 
         SET @fullTriggerName = 'dbo.[' + @triggerName + ']' 

         /* Create the cannonicalized table name for trigger creation */ 
         /* Do not touch it if the name contains other delimiters */ 
         IF (CHARINDEX('.', @tableName) <> 0 OR 
             CHARINDEX('[', @tableName) <> 0 OR 
             CHARINDEX(']', @tableName) <> 0) 
             SET @canonTableName = @tableName 
         ELSE 
             SET @canonTableName = '[' + @tableName + ']' 

         /* First make sure the table exists */ 
         IF (SELECT OBJECT_ID(@tableName, 'U')) IS NULL 
         BEGIN 
             RAISERROR ('00000001', 16, 1) 
             RETURN 
         END 

         BEGIN TRAN
         /* Insert the value into the notification table */ 
         IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT tableName FROM dbo.AspNet_SqlCacheTablesForChangeNotification WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE tableName = @tableName) 
             IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT tableName FROM dbo.AspNet_SqlCacheTablesForChangeNotification WITH (TABLOCKX) WHERE tableName = @tableName) 
                 INSERT  dbo.AspNet_SqlCacheTablesForChangeNotification 
                 VALUES (@tableName, GETDATE(), 0)

         /* Create the trigger */ 
         SET @quotedTableName = QUOTENAME(@tableName, '''') 
         IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT name FROM sysobjects WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE name = @triggerName AND type = 'TR') 
             IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT name FROM sysobjects WITH (TABLOCKX) WHERE name = @triggerName AND type = 'TR') 
                 EXEC('CREATE TRIGGER ' + @fullTriggerName + ' ON ' + @canonTableName +'
                       FOR INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE AS BEGIN
                       SET NOCOUNT ON
                       EXEC dbo.AspNet_SqlCacheUpdateChangeIdStoredProcedure N' + @quotedTableName + '
                       END
                       ')
         COMMIT TRAN
         END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[AspNet_SqlCacheUnRegisterTableStoredProcedure]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[AspNet_SqlCacheUnRegisterTableStoredProcedure] 
             @tableName NVARCHAR(450) 
         AS
         BEGIN

         BEGIN TRAN
         DECLARE @triggerName AS NVARCHAR(3000) 
         DECLARE @fullTriggerName AS NVARCHAR(3000)
         SET @triggerName = REPLACE(@tableName, '[', '__o__') 
         SET @triggerName = REPLACE(@triggerName, ']', '__c__') 
         SET @triggerName = @triggerName + '_AspNet_SqlCacheNotification_Trigger' 
         SET @fullTriggerName = 'dbo.[' + @triggerName + ']' 

         /* Remove the table-row from the notification table */ 
         IF EXISTS (SELECT name FROM sysobjects WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE name = 'AspNet_SqlCacheTablesForChangeNotification' AND type = 'U') 
             IF EXISTS (SELECT name FROM sysobjects WITH (TABLOCKX) WHERE name = 'AspNet_SqlCacheTablesForChangeNotification' AND type = 'U') 
             DELETE FROM dbo.AspNet_SqlCacheTablesForChangeNotification WHERE tableName = @tableName 

         /* Remove the trigger */ 
         IF EXISTS (SELECT name FROM sysobjects WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE name = @triggerName AND type = 'TR') 
             IF EXISTS (SELECT name FROM sysobjects WITH (TABLOCKX) WHERE name = @triggerName AND type = 'TR') 
             EXEC('DROP TRIGGER ' + @fullTriggerName) 

         COMMIT TRAN
         END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[AspNet_SqlCacheUpdateChangeIdStoredProcedure]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[AspNet_SqlCacheUpdateChangeIdStoredProcedure] 
             @tableName NVARCHAR(450) 
         AS

         BEGIN 
             UPDATE dbo.AspNet_SqlCacheTablesForChangeNotification WITH (ROWLOCK) SET changeId = changeId + 1 
             WHERE tableName = @tableName
         END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[COMPETITION_T_PAGE_SP]
@CurrentPage As int,
@PageSize As int,
@TotalRecords int OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN

set nocount on

Declare @FirstRec int
Declare @LastRec int

-- Initialize variables.
Set @FirstRec = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize
Set @LastRec = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize + 1)

--Create a temporary table

DECLARE @TempTable Table
(	
ID int IDENTITY,
--- all paramaters
 COMPETITION_ID int
	, COMPETITION_TITLE varchar(150)
	, COMPETITION_DESCRIPTION varchar(2500)
	, COMPETITION_QUESTION varchar(550) 
	, DISPLAY int
	, COMPETITION_ENDS smalldatetime

)


INSERT INTO 
@TempTable
( 

--- all paramaters
		 
			 COMPETITION_ID
			,  COMPETITION_TITLE
			,  COMPETITION_DESCRIPTION
			,  COMPETITION_QUESTION
			,  DISPLAY
			,  COMPETITION_ENDS


)
		select 
			 COMPETITION_ID
			,  COMPETITION_TITLE
			,  COMPETITION_DESCRIPTION
			,  COMPETITION_QUESTION
			,  DISPLAY
			,  COMPETITION_ENDS

from
COMPETITION_T
order by COMPETITION_ID


		select 
			 COMPETITION_ID
			,  COMPETITION_TITLE
			,  COMPETITION_DESCRIPTION
			,  COMPETITION_QUESTION
			,  DISPLAY
			,  COMPETITION_ENDS

-- parameter list
FROM @TempTable
WHERE ID > @FirstRec AND ID < @LastRec
order by COMPETITION_ID  asc

--Return the total number of records available as an output parameter
Select
@TotalRecords = Count(COMPETITION_ID)
From 
COMPETITION_T




END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[COMPETITION_T_UPDATE_SP]
	( @COMPETITION_ID int
	, @COMPETITION_TITLE varchar(150)
	, @COMPETITION_DESCRIPTION varchar(2500)
	, @COMPETITION_QUESTION varchar(550) = null
	, @DISPLAY int
	, @COMPETITION_ENDS smalldatetime
	)
AS
BEGIN

	set nocount on

	declare @ReturnValue int
	set @ReturnValue = @COMPETITION_ID 

	if @COMPETITION_ID = 0 
	begin

		insert into COMPETITION_T
			( COMPETITION_TITLE
			, COMPETITION_DESCRIPTION
			, COMPETITION_QUESTION
			, DISPLAY
			, COMPETITION_ENDS
			)
		values
			( @COMPETITION_TITLE
			, @COMPETITION_DESCRIPTION
			, @COMPETITION_QUESTION
			, @DISPLAY
			, @COMPETITION_ENDS
			)
	
		set @ReturnValue = scope_identity()

	end
	else
	begin
	
		update COMPETITION_T with (rowlock)
			set COMPETITION_TITLE = @COMPETITION_TITLE
			, COMPETITION_DESCRIPTION = @COMPETITION_DESCRIPTION
			, COMPETITION_QUESTION = @COMPETITION_QUESTION
			, DISPLAY = @DISPLAY
			, COMPETITION_ENDS = @COMPETITION_ENDS
		where 
			COMPETITION_ID = @COMPETITION_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[ELMAH_GetErrorsXml]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[ELMAH_GetErrorsXml]
(
    @Application NVARCHAR(60),
    @PageIndex INT = 0,
    @PageSize INT = 15,
    @TotalCount INT OUTPUT
)
AS 

    SET NOCOUNT ON

    DECLARE @FirstTimeUTC DATETIME
    DECLARE @FirstSequence INT
    DECLARE @StartRow INT
    DECLARE @StartRowIndex INT

    SELECT 
        @TotalCount = COUNT(1) 
    FROM 
        [ELMAH_Error]
    WHERE 
        [Application] = @Application

    -- Get the ID of the first error for the requested page

    SET @StartRowIndex = @PageIndex * @PageSize + 1

    IF @StartRowIndex <= @TotalCount
    BEGIN

        SET ROWCOUNT @StartRowIndex

        SELECT  
            @FirstTimeUTC = [TimeUtc],
            @FirstSequence = [Sequence]
        FROM 
            [ELMAH_Error]
        WHERE   
            [Application] = @Application
        ORDER BY 
            [TimeUtc] DESC, 
            [Sequence] DESC

    END
    ELSE
    BEGIN

        SET @PageSize = 0

    END

    -- Now set the row count to the requested page size and get
    -- all records below it for the pertaining application.

    SET ROWCOUNT @PageSize

    SELECT 
        errorId     = [ErrorId], 
        application = [Application],
        host        = [Host], 
        type        = [Type],
        source      = [Source],
        message     = [Message],
        [user]      = [User],
        statusCode  = [StatusCode], 
        time        = CONVERT(VARCHAR(50), [TimeUtc], 126) + 'Z'
    FROM 
        [ELMAH_Error] error
    WHERE
        [Application] = @Application
    AND
        [TimeUtc] <= @FirstTimeUTC
    AND 
        [Sequence] <= @FirstSequence
    ORDER BY
        [TimeUtc] DESC, 
        [Sequence] DESC
    FOR
        XML AUTO
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[ELMAH_GetErrorXml]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[ELMAH_GetErrorXml]
(
    @Application NVARCHAR(60),
    @ErrorId UNIQUEIDENTIFIER
)
AS

    SET NOCOUNT ON

    SELECT 
        [AllXml]
    FROM 
        [ELMAH_Error]
    WHERE
        [ErrorId] = @ErrorId
    AND
        [Application] = @Application
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[ELMAH_LogError]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[ELMAH_LogError]
(
    @ErrorId UNIQUEIDENTIFIER,
    @Application NVARCHAR(60),
    @Host NVARCHAR(30),
    @Type NVARCHAR(100),
    @Source NVARCHAR(60),
    @Message NVARCHAR(500),
    @User NVARCHAR(50),
    @AllXml NTEXT,
    @StatusCode INT,
    @TimeUtc DATETIME
)
AS

    SET NOCOUNT ON

    INSERT
    INTO
        [ELMAH_Error]
        (
            [ErrorId],
            [Application],
            [Host],
            [Type],
            [Source],
            [Message],
            [User],
            [AllXml],
            [StatusCode],
            [TimeUtc]
        )
    VALUES
        (
            @ErrorId,
            @Application,
            @Host,
            @Type,
            @Source,
            @Message,
            @User,
            @AllXml,
            @StatusCode,
            @TimeUtc
        )
GO

Set @LastRec = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize + 1)

 EMAIL_TEMPLATE_ID int 
	, EMAIL_NICKNAME varchar(50)

)

			 EMAIL_TEMPLATE_ID
			,  EMAIL_NICKNAME
			,  EMAIL_SUBJECT
			,  EMAIL_TEXT

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[EMAIL_TEMPLATE_T_UPDATE_SP]
	( @EMAIL_TEMPLATE_ID int = 0
	, @EMAIL_NICKNAME varchar(50) = null
	, @EMAIL_SUBJECT varchar(100) = null
	, @EMAIL_TEXT varchar(2000) = null
	
	, @EMAIL_FROM_ADDRESS_TYPE tinyint
	)
AS
BEGIN

	set nocount on

	declare @ReturnValue int
	set @ReturnValue = @EMAIL_TEMPLATE_ID 

	if @EMAIL_TEMPLATE_ID = 0 
	begin

		insert into EMAIL_TEMPLATE_T
			( EMAIL_NICKNAME
			, EMAIL_SUBJECT
			, EMAIL_TEXT
			, EMAIL_FROM_ADDRESS_TYPE
			)
		values
			( @EMAIL_NICKNAME
			, @EMAIL_SUBJECT
			, @EMAIL_TEXT
			, @EMAIL_FROM_ADDRESS_TYPE
			)
	
		set @ReturnValue = scope_identity()

	end
	else
	begin
	
		update EMAIL_TEMPLATE_T with (rowlock)
			set EMAIL_NICKNAME = @EMAIL_NICKNAME
			, EMAIL_SUBJECT = @EMAIL_SUBJECT
			, EMAIL_TEXT = @EMAIL_TEXT
			, EMAIL_FROM_ADDRESS_TYPE = @EMAIL_FROM_ADDRESS_TYPE
		where 
			EMAIL_TEMPLATE_ID = @EMAIL_TEMPLATE_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue
--	exec C:\webs_richard\components\UnifiedASPCodeGeneratorSourceVB.Net2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASP Code Generator Source VB.Net 2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASPCodeGenerator\outputEMAIL_TEMPLATE_T_Get @ReturnValue

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[FindReplace]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create PROCEDURE [dbo].[FindReplace]
	(
	@TABLE  VARCHAR(200),
	@Field  VARCHAR(200),
	@WHERE VARCHAR(100),
	@Find  VARCHAR(500),
	@REPLACE  VARCHAR(500)
	)
	AS
	DECLARE @query VARCHAR(8000)
	SET @query  = 'UPDATE ' +  @TABLE +
	              ' SET ' +  @Field + '= REPLACE(CONVERT(varchar(8000),'
	              + @Field + '),''' +  @Find + ''',''' + @REPLACE  +''')'
	IF(@WHERE <> '')
	        SET @query = @query + ' WHERE '+@WHERE
	       
	EXECUTE (@query)
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[J_MENU_T_UPDATE_SP]

	, @MENU_TITLE varchar(50) = null
	, @MENU_TEXT varchar(8000) = null
	, @DISPLAY int = null
	, @SORT_ORDER int = null
	)
AS
BEGIN

	set nocount on

	declare @ReturnValue int
	set @ReturnValue = @J_MENU_ID

	begin

		insert into J_MENU_T
			( MENU_TITLE
			, MENU_TEXT
			, DISPLAY
			, SORT_ORDER
			)
		values
			( @MENU_TITLE
			, @MENU_TEXT
			, @DISPLAY
			, @SORT_ORDER
			)
	
		set @ReturnValue = scope_identity()

	end
	else
	begin
	
		update J_MENU_T with (rowlock)
			set MENU_TITLE = @MENU_TITLE
			, MENU_TEXT = @MENU_TEXT
			, DISPLAY = @DISPLAY
			, SORT_ORDER = @SORT_ORDER
		where 
			J_MENU_ID = @J_MENU_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue

SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[LABS_ARTICLE_CAT_FOR_BLOG_LIST_SP]
@Q_BLOG_ID INT
AS


SELECT     TOP 100 dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_SUBJECT
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T ON dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_ID
WHERE     (dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID =
                          (SELECT     dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID
                            FROM          dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T INNER JOIN
                                                   dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T ON dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID
                            WHERE      TAG_TYPE = 1 AND Q_BLOG_ID = @Q_BLOG_ID)) AND PUBLISH = 1
ORDER BY dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[LABS_GRADUATE_POSTS_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[LABS_GRADUATE_POSTS_SP]
 AS
SELECT     TOP 2 dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_SUBJECT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_TEXT, dbo.Q_BLOG_THUMB_T.THUMB_URL, 
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_THUMB_T.THUMB_WIDTH, dbo.Q_BLOG_THUMB_T.THUMB_HEIGHT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE, BYLINE
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_THUMB_T RIGHT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_T ON dbo.Q_BLOG_THUMB_T.Q_BLOG_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID
WHERE     (dbo.Q_BLOG_T.PUBLISH = 1) and q_blog_title_id = 590 AND (LABS_GRADUATE = 1)
ORDER BY dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE DESC
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[LABS_RECENT_POSTS_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[LABS_RECENT_POSTS_SP]
 AS
SELECT     TOP 3  dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_SUBJECT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_TEXT, dbo.Q_BLOG_THUMB_T.THUMB_URL, 
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_THUMB_T.THUMB_WIDTH, dbo.Q_BLOG_THUMB_T.THUMB_HEIGHT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE, BYLINE
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_THUMB_T RIGHT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_T ON dbo.Q_BLOG_THUMB_T.Q_BLOG_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID
WHERE     (dbo.Q_BLOG_T.PUBLISH = 1) and q_blog_title_id = 590 AND (LABS_GRADUATE = 0)
ORDER BY dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE DESC
GO

Create Procedure [dbo].[LABS_TAG_LIST_SP]
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID INT
As
Begin
	Select 
		[Q_BLOG_TAG_ID],
		[TAG_NAME],
		[Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID],
		[TAG_TYPE]
	From Q_BLOG_TAG_T
WHERE Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID and tag_type = 1
ORDER BY TAG_NAME ASC
End

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_ALBUM_LIST_SP]
 AS
SELECT     Q_ALBUM_ID, ALBUM_NAME, year(release_date) as release_year, isnull(THUMB_URL, '') as thumb_url, isnull(THUMB_HEIGHT, '') as thumb_height, isnull(THUMB_WIDTH, '') as thumb_width
FROM         Q_ALBUM_T
WHERE     (ACTIVE = 1)
ORDER BY year(RELEASE_DATE), month(release_date) asc
GO

-- Description:	<Description,,>

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_ALBUM_SONG_LIST_SITEMAP_SP] 
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT     Q_ALBUM_T.ALBUM_NAME + '/' + Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.SONG_TITLE as song_title, Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID
FROM         Q_ALBUM_T WITH (nolock) INNER JOIN
                      Q_ALBUM_SONG_T ON Q_ALBUM_T.Q_ALBUM_ID = Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ALBUM_ID
ORDER BY Q_ALBUM_T.Q_ALBUM_ID
END

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_ALBUM_SONG_RANDOM_SP] 
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT     TOP (1) Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID, Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.SONG_TITLE, Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.SONG_LYRICS, Q_ALBUM_T.ALBUM_NAME, 
                      Q_ALBUM_T.Q_ALBUM_ID, Q_ALBUM_T.THUMB_URL, Q_ALBUM_T.THUMB_HEIGHT, Q_ALBUM_T.THUMB_WIDTH
FROM         Q_ALBUM_SONG_T INNER JOIN
                      Q_ALBUM_T ON Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ALBUM_ID = Q_ALBUM_T.Q_ALBUM_ID
          where SONG_LYRICS <> '' 
                      ORDER BY NEWID()
END

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_ALBUM_SONG_T_DISPLAY_SP]
	( @Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID int )
AS
BEGIN

set nocount on

		SELECT     Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID, Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.SONG_TITLE, Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.SONG_LYRICS, Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ALBUM_ID, 
                      Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.SONG_NOTES, Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ARTIST_ID, Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.IS_SINGLE, Q_ALBUM_T.ALBUM_NAME, 
                      Q_ARTIST_T.ARTIST_NAME
FROM         Q_ALBUM_SONG_T INNER JOIN
                      Q_ALBUM_T ON Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ALBUM_ID = Q_ALBUM_T.Q_ALBUM_ID INNER JOIN
                      Q_ARTIST_T ON Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ARTIST_ID = Q_ARTIST_T.Q_ARTIST_ID 
		where Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID = @Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID

BEGIN

set nocount on

SELECT     Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.SONG_TITLE, Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID, Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.SONG_LYRICS, Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ALBUM_ID, 
                      Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.SONG_NOTES, Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ARTIST_ID, Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.IS_SINGLE, Q_ALBUM_T.ALBUM_NAME
FROM         Q_ALBUM_SONG_T INNER JOIN
                      Q_ALBUM_T ON Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ALBUM_ID = Q_ALBUM_T.Q_ALBUM_ID 
			where Q_ALBUM_SONG_T.Q_ALBUM_ID = @Q_ALBUM_ID
		order by
			Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID

END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_ALBUM_SONG_T_UPDATE_SP]
	( @Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID int = 0
	, @SONG_TITLE varchar(100) = null
	, @SONG_LYRICS varchar(4000) = null
	, @Q_ALBUM_ID int = null
	, @SONG_NOTES varchar(2000) = null
	, @Q_ARTIST_ID int = null
	, @IS_SINGLE int = null
	)
AS
BEGIN

	set nocount on

	declare @ReturnValue int
	set @ReturnValue = @Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID 

	if @Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID = 0 
	begin

		insert into Q_ALBUM_SONG_T
			( SONG_TITLE
			, SONG_LYRICS
			, Q_ALBUM_ID
			, SONG_NOTES
			, Q_ARTIST_ID
			, IS_SINGLE
			)
		values
			( @SONG_TITLE
			, @SONG_LYRICS
			, @Q_ALBUM_ID
			, @SONG_NOTES
			, @Q_ARTIST_ID
			, @IS_SINGLE
			)
	
		set @ReturnValue = scope_identity()

	end
	else
	begin
	
		update Q_ALBUM_SONG_T with (rowlock)
			set SONG_TITLE = @SONG_TITLE
			, SONG_LYRICS = @SONG_LYRICS
			, Q_ALBUM_ID = @Q_ALBUM_ID
			, SONG_NOTES = @SONG_NOTES
			, Q_ARTIST_ID = @Q_ARTIST_ID
			, IS_SINGLE = @IS_SINGLE
		where 
			Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID = @Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue
--	exec C:\webs_richard\components\UnifiedASPCodeGeneratorSourceVB.Net2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASP Code Generator Source VB.Net 2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASPCodeGenerator\outputQ_ALBUM_SONG_T_Get @ReturnValue

END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_ALBUM_T_UPDATE_SP]
	( @Q_ALBUM_ID int = 0
	, @ALBUM_NAME varchar(50) = null
	, @AMAZON varchar(100) = null
	, @ARTIST int = null
	, @RELEASE_DATE smalldatetime = null
	, @GENERAL_NOTES varchar(4000) = null
	, @THUMB_URL varchar(50) = null
	, @THUMB_HEIGHT int = null
	, @THUMB_WIDTH int = null
	, @PICTURE_URL varchar(50) = null
	, @PICTURE_HEIGHT int = null
	, @PICTURE_WIDTH int = null
	, @ACTIVE TINYINT
	)
AS
BEGIN

	set nocount on

	declare @ReturnValue int
	set @ReturnValue = @Q_ALBUM_ID 

	if @Q_ALBUM_ID = 0 
	begin

		insert into Q_ALBUM_T
			( ALBUM_NAME
			, AMAZON
			, ARTIST
			, RELEASE_DATE
			, GENERAL_NOTES
			, THUMB_URL
			, THUMB_HEIGHT
			, THUMB_WIDTH
			, PICTURE_URL
			, PICTURE_HEIGHT
			, PICTURE_WIDTH
			, ACTIVE
			)
		values
			( @ALBUM_NAME
			, @AMAZON
			, @ARTIST
			, @RELEASE_DATE
			, @GENERAL_NOTES
			, @THUMB_URL
			, @THUMB_HEIGHT
			, @THUMB_WIDTH
			, @PICTURE_URL
			, @PICTURE_HEIGHT
			, @PICTURE_WIDTH
			, @ACTIVE
			)
	
		set @ReturnValue = scope_identity()

	end
	else
	begin
	
		update Q_ALBUM_T with (rowlock)
			set ALBUM_NAME = @ALBUM_NAME
			, AMAZON = @AMAZON
			, ARTIST = @ARTIST
			, RELEASE_DATE = @RELEASE_DATE
			, GENERAL_NOTES = @GENERAL_NOTES
			, THUMB_URL = @THUMB_URL
			, THUMB_HEIGHT = @THUMB_HEIGHT
			, THUMB_WIDTH = @THUMB_WIDTH
			, PICTURE_URL = @PICTURE_URL
			, PICTURE_HEIGHT = @PICTURE_HEIGHT
			, PICTURE_WIDTH = @PICTURE_WIDTH
			, ACTIVE = @ACTIVE
		where 
			Q_ALBUM_ID = @Q_ALBUM_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue
--	exec C:\webs_richard\components\UnifiedASPCodeGeneratorSourceVB.Net2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASP Code Generator Source VB.Net 2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASPCodeGenerator\outputQ_ALBUM_T_Get @ReturnValue

END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_ARTICLE_ADD_SP]
@ARTICLE_NAME varchar(150),
@SOURCE varchar(150),
@ARTICLE_TEXT ntext,
@Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_ID tinyint,
@DISPLAY tinyint,
@USER_ID int,
@THEDATE varchar(60)
AS
INSERT INTO Q_ARTICLE_T
(
ARTICLE_NAME,
SOURCE,
ARTICLE_TEXT,
Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_ID,
DISPLAY,
USER_ID,
THEDATE
)
VALUES
(
@ARTICLE_NAME,
@SOURCE,
@ARTICLE_TEXT,
@Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_ID,
@DISPLAY,
@USER_ID,
@THEDATE
)

select @@identity
return @@identity
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_LIST_GROUP_SP] 
AS
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT dbo.Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_T.Q_ARTICLE_CAT_ID, dbo.Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_T.ARTICLE_CATEGORY, 
                      COUNT(dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.Q_ARTICLE_ID) AS thecount
FROM         dbo.Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T ON dbo.Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_T.Q_ARTICLE_CAT_ID = dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_ID
GROUP BY dbo.Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_T.Q_ARTICLE_CAT_ID, dbo.Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_T.ARTICLE_CATEGORY
ORDER BY dbo.Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_T.ARTICLE_CATEGORY
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_ARTICLE_LIST_BY_CATEGORY_SP]
@Q_ARTICLE_CAT_ID SMALLINT
AS
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT dbo.Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_T.ARTICLE_CATEGORY, dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.ARTICLE_NAME, dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.DISPLAY, dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.SOURCE,
                      dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.Q_ARTICLE_ID, THEDATE,  Q_ARTICLE_T.DATE_CREATED
FROM         dbo.Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T ON dbo.Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_T.Q_ARTICLE_CAT_ID = dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_ID
WHERE dbo.Q_ARTICLE_CATEGORY_T.Q_ARTICLE_CAT_ID = @Q_ARTICLE_CAT_ID AND DISPLAY = 1
ORDER BY dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.DISPLAY, DATE_CREATED DESC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_ARTICLE_LIST_SP]

                      dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.Q_ARTICLE_ID

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BIO_NEXT_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@IPAGE SMALLINT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
    


    SELECT  TOP 1 TITLE
FROM         Q_BIO_T
WHERE  DISPLAY_SEQUENCE > (SELECT DISPLAY_SEQUENCE FROM Q_BIO_T WHERE Q_BIO_ID = @IPAGE )
ORDER BY DISPLAY_SEQUENCE ASC



END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_BIO_T_PAGE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Q_BIO_T_PAGE_SP]
@PageSize int,  
@CurrentPage int,        
@ItemCount int output     
AS 
Declare @UpperBand int, @LowerBand int
-- Get The Count Of The Rows That They Meet the Criteria 
SET @ItemCount = (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM Q_BIO_T)    
-- Calculate the @LowerCount and @UpperCount    
SET @LowerBand  = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize    
SET @UpperBand  = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize) + 1   
-- -- create a temporaty table     
CREATE TABLE #AllRows(             
RowNumber int IDENTITY, 
	Q_BIO_ID smallint,
	TITLE varchar(50),
	SUMMARY varchar(400),
	BIO_TEXT ntext,
	DISPLAY_SEQUENCE tinyint,
	CREATE_DATE smalldatetime)
   -- INSERT ALL THE Rows that meets the Criteria 
	 INSERT INTO #AllRows ( 		[Q_BIO_ID],
		[TITLE],
		[SUMMARY],
		[BIO_TEXT],
		[DISPLAY_SEQUENCE],
		[CREATE_DATE])
	 select  			[Q_BIO_ID],
			[TITLE],
			[SUMMARY],
			[BIO_TEXT],
			[DISPLAY_SEQUENCE],
			[CREATE_DATE]
	From Q_BIO_T
	ORDER BY display_sequence ASC 
	  -- AND finally select and return desired -Paged- Rows  
	 SELECT RowNumber ,
		[Q_BIO_ID],
		[TITLE],
		[SUMMARY],
		[BIO_TEXT],
		[DISPLAY_SEQUENCE],
		[CREATE_DATE] FROM #AllRows WHERE Q_bio_id = @CurrentPage
		
		
		RETURN
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_BIO_UPDATE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BIO_UPDATE_SP]
@TITLE VARCHAR(50),
@SUMMARY VARCHAR(400),
@BIO_TEXT varchar(MAX),
@DISPLAY_SEQUENCE TINYINT,
@Q_BIO_ID SMALLINT
AS
IF @Q_BIO_ID = 0 
	BEGIN
		INSERT INTO Q_BIO_T
		(
		TITLE,
		SUMMARY,
		BIO_TEXT,
		DISPLAY_SEQUENCE
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@TITLE,
		@SUMMARY,
		@BIO_TEXT,
		@DISPLAY_SEQUENCE
		)
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		UPDATE Q_BIO_T
		SET
		TITLE = @TITLE,
		SUMMARY = @SUMMARY,
		BIO_TEXT = @BIO_TEXT,
		DISPLAY_SEQUENCE = @DISPLAY_SEQUENCE,
		CREATE_DATE = GETDATE()
		WHERE 
		Q_BIO_ID = @Q_BIO_ID
	END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_ACCESS_CHECK_SP] 
@USER_ID2 INT,
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID2 SMALLINT
AS

BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here

Declare @return tinyint
set @return = 0
	
if exists( SELECT     ISNULL(Q_BLOG_ACCESS_T.USER_ID, 0) AS THENUMBER, ISNULL(Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.USER_ID, 0) AS THENUMBER2 
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      Q_BLOG_ACCESS_T ON dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = Q_BLOG_ACCESS_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
WHERE     
((Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.USER_ID = @USER_ID2) AND (Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID2))
OR

((Q_BLOG_ACCESS_T.USER_ID = @USER_ID2) AND (Q_BLOG_ACCESS_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID2))
)
	begin
		
		set @return = 1
	
	end 

return @return

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_BLOG_ADD_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_ADD_SP] 
@BLOG_SUBJECT VARCHAR(150),
@BLOG_TEXT ntext,
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID SMALLINT,
@PUBLISH TINYINT,
@ALLOW_COMMENT tinyint,
@Q_BLOG_ID INT,
@USER_ID INT

AS

DECLARE	@RETURNVALUE INT
SET @RETURNVALUE = 0

DECLARE @RETURN INT 



EXEC	@RETURNVALUE = [Q_BLOG_ACCESS_CHECK_SP]
		@USER_ID2 = @USER_ID,
		@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID2 = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID

IF (@RETURNVALUE > 0)
	
BEGIN

IF @Q_BLOG_ID = 0 
	BEGIN


		PRINT('NEW BLOG POST')

		INSERT INTO Q_BLOG_T
		(
		BLOG_SUBJECT,
		BLOG_TEXT,	
		Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID,
		PUBLISH,
		ALLOW_COMMENT
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@BLOG_SUBJECT,
		@BLOG_TEXT,	
		@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID,
		@PUBLISH,
		@ALLOW_COMMENT
		)

	SELECT @@IDENTITY	
	SET @RETURN = @@IDENTITY	


	END
	


ELSE
	BEGIN
		UPDATE Q_BLOG_T
		SET
		BLOG_SUBJECT = @BLOG_SUBJECT,
		BLOG_TEXT = @BLOG_TEXT,
		PUBLISH = @PUBLISH,
		ALLOW_COMMENT = @ALLOW_COMMENT
		WHERE Q_BLOG_ID = @Q_BLOG_ID AND Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
		
		PRINT('OLD BLOG POST '  )
		PRINT(@Q_BLOG_ID)

		SET @RETURN = @Q_BLOG_ID

	END
	

	
	

END

PRINT('RETURNING')
--SELECT @RETURN
RETURN @RETURN
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_BLOG_ADD_WRITER_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_ADD_WRITER_SP] 
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure hereG
	@Q_BLOG_ID int,
@BLOG_SUBJECT VARCHAR(150),
@BLOG_TEXT ntext,
@PUBLISH TINYINT,
@USER_ID INT

AS
BEGIN

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	
	DECLARE	@RETURNVALUE INT
	SET @RETURNVALUE = 0

	DECLARE @RETURN INT 

	
	DECLARE	@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID SMALLINT
	
	SELECT TOP 1 @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID 
	FROM Q_BLOG_TITLE_T
	WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID
	

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
	
	IF @Q_BLOG_ID = 0 
		BEGIN
		
			INSERT INTO Q_BLOG_T
		(
		BLOG_SUBJECT,
		BLOG_TEXT,	
		Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID,
		PUBLISH,
		ALLOW_COMMENT
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@BLOG_SUBJECT,
		@BLOG_TEXT,	
		@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID,
		@PUBLISH,
		1
		)

		END
		
	ELSE
		
		BEGIN
		
		UPDATE Q_BLOG_T
		SET
		BLOG_SUBJECT = @BLOG_SUBJECT,
		BLOG_TEXT = @BLOG_TEXT,
		PUBLISH = @PUBLISH,
		ALLOW_COMMENT = 1
		WHERE Q_BLOG_ID = @Q_BLOG_ID AND Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
		
		PRINT('OLD BLOG POST '  )
		PRINT(@Q_BLOG_ID)

		SET @RETURN = @Q_BLOG_ID
		
		
		END
		
	END
	
	
	
	



PRINT('RETURNING')
--SELECT @RETURN
RETURN @RETURN
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_BLOG_ARCHIVE_LIST_BY_BLOG_TITLE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_ARCHIVE_LIST_BY_BLOG_TITLE_SP]
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID INT
AS
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT COUNT(Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID) AS THECOUNT, MONTH(CREATE_DATE) AS THEMONTH, YEAR(CREATE_DATE) AS THEYEAR, Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_T
WHERE      ((dbo.Q_BLOG_T.PUBLISH = 1) or (PUBLISH = 2)) AND Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
GROUP BY MONTH(CREATE_DATE), Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID, YEAR(CREATE_DATE)
ORDER BY YEAR(CREATE_DATE) desc, MONTH(CREATE_DATE) desc
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_BLOG_ARCHIVE_LIST_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_ARCHIVE_LIST_SP]
@Q_BLOG_ID INT
AS
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT COUNT(Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID) AS THECOUNT, MONTH(CREATE_DATE) AS THEMONTH, YEAR(CREATE_DATE) AS THEYEAR, Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_T
WHERE      ((dbo.Q_BLOG_T.PUBLISH = 1) or (PUBLISH = 2)) AND Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = (select Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID from q_blog_t where q_blog_id = @q_blog_id)
GROUP BY MONTH(CREATE_DATE), Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID, YEAR(CREATE_DATE)
ORDER BY YEAR(CREATE_DATE) desc, MONTH(CREATE_DATE) desc
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_BLOG_BY_USER_ID_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_BY_USER_ID_SP] 
@USER_ID  INT
AS
-- LOG THE BLOG VIEW

-- SELECT THE BLOG ENTRY
SELECT     TOP 10 Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_SUBJECT, Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_TEXT, Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE, Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID, 
                      Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V.COMMENT_COUNT, Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.USER_ID, Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID, Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.BLOG_TITLE
FROM         Q_BLOG_T INNER JOIN
                      Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V ON Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID = Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V.Q_BLOG_ID INNER JOIN
                      Q_BLOG_TITLE_T ON Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
WHERE     (Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.USER_ID = @USER_ID) AND (Q_BLOG_T.PUBLISH = 1)
ORDER BY Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE DESC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_COMMENT_LIST_SP]
@Q_BLOG_ID INT
AS
SELECT     ISNULL(USERS_T.USERNAME, '') AS username, Q_BLOG_COMMENT_T.DATE_CREATED, isnull(USERS_T.USER_ID, '') as USER_ID, 
                      ISNULL(Q_BLOG_COMMENT_T.NAME_OF_COMMENT, '') AS name_of_comment, Q_BLOG_COMMENT_T.BLOG_COMMENT, 
                      Q_BLOG_COMMENT_T.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_ID, USERS_T.USERNAME AS USERNAME2
FROM         Q_BLOG_COMMENT_T LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      USERS_T ON Q_BLOG_COMMENT_T.USER_ID = USERS_T.USER_ID
where Q_BLOG_ID =  @Q_BLOG_ID
order by Q_BLOG_COMMENT_T.date_created asc
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_DATE_ENTRY_SP]
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID SMALLINT,
@THEDATE SMALLDATETIME
AS
SELECT DISTINCT CONVERT(CHAR(11), CREATE_DATE, 10) AS Expr1
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_T
WHERE     (Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID) 
 AND PUBLISH = 1 AND 
(
MONTH(CREATE_DATE) = MONTH(@THEDATE)
AND 
YEAR(CREATE_DATE) = YEAR(@THEDATE)
)
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_DISPLAY_BY_USER_BY_DATE_SP]
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID  SMALLINT,
@THEDATE SMALLDATETIME
AS
-- LOG THE BLOG VIEW
INSERT INTO Q_BLOG_LOG_T
(
Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
)
VALUES
(
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
)
-- SELECT THE BLOG ENTRY
SELECT     TOP 10 dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_SUBJECT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_TEXT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID, 
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V.COMMENT_COUNT
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V ON dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V.Q_BLOG_ID
WHERE dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID AND PUBLISH = 1
 AND 
(
MONTH(CREATE_DATE) = MONTH(@THEDATE)
AND
YEAR(CREATE_DATE) = YEAR(@THEDATE)
AND
DAY(CREATE_DATE) =DAY(@THEDATE)
)
ORDER BY 
CREATE_DATE DESC
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_BLOG_ENTRY_COUNT_BY_MONTH_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_ENTRY_COUNT_BY_MONTH_SP]
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID INT
AS
SELECT     COUNT(Q_BLOG_ID) AS ENTRY_NUMBER, { fn MONTHNAME(MONTH(CREATE_DATE)) } AS MONTHNAME, MONTH(CREATE_DATE) AS MONTH, 
                      YEAR(CREATE_DATE) AS THEYEAR
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_T
WHERE     (Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID) AND  PUBLISH = 1
GROUP BY { fn MONTHNAME(MONTH(CREATE_DATE)) }, MONTH(CREATE_DATE), YEAR(CREATE_DATE)
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_FEATURED_ADD_SP]
	
	@TITLE varchar(70),
	@FEATURED_TEXT varchar(4000),
	@DISPLAY tinyint,
	@IMAGE_URL varchar(70),
	@IMAGE_WIDTH smallint,
	@IMAGE_HEIGHT smallint,
	@LINK_URL varchar(100),
@BYLINE VARCHAR(100),
@Q_BLOG_FEATURED_ID smallint
As


IF @Q_BLOG_FEATURED_ID = 0 

Begin
	Insert Into Q_BLOG_FEATURED_T
		([TITLE],[FEATURED_TEXT],[DISPLAY],[IMAGE_URL],[IMAGE_WIDTH],[IMAGE_HEIGHT],[LINK_URL], [BYLINE])
	Values
		(@TITLE,@FEATURED_TEXT,@DISPLAY,@IMAGE_URL,@IMAGE_WIDTH,@IMAGE_HEIGHT,@LINK_URL, @BYLINE)

End

ELSE

BEGIN

	IF @IMAGE_URL <> '' 
		BEGIN
Update Q_BLOG_FEATURED_T
	Set
		
		[TITLE] = @TITLE,
		[FEATURED_TEXT] = @FEATURED_TEXT,
		[DISPLAY] = @DISPLAY,
		[IMAGE_URL] = @IMAGE_URL,
		[IMAGE_WIDTH] = @IMAGE_WIDTH,
		[IMAGE_HEIGHT] = @IMAGE_HEIGHT,
		[LINK_URL] = @LINK_URL,
		[BYLINE] = @BYLINE
	Where [Q_BLOG_FEATURED_ID] = @Q_BLOG_FEATURED_ID	



		END
ELSE
		BEGIN

Update Q_BLOG_FEATURED_T
	Set
		
		[TITLE] = @TITLE,
		[FEATURED_TEXT] = @FEATURED_TEXT,
		[DISPLAY] = @DISPLAY,

		[LINK_URL] = @LINK_URL,
[BYLINE] = @BYLINE
	Where [Q_BLOG_FEATURED_ID] = @Q_BLOG_FEATURED_ID	
		END

	


END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_LIST_BY_DATE_SP] 
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID SMALLINT,
@MONTH TINYINT,
@YEAR SMALLINT
AS
SELECT     TOP 100 dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_SUBJECT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_TEXT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID, 
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V.COMMENT_COUNT, byline
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V ON dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V.Q_BLOG_ID
WHERE     (dbo.Q_BLOG_T.PUBLISH = 1) AND  (MONTH(CREATE_DATE) = @MONTH AND YEAR(CREATE_DATE) = @YEAR) AND Q_blog_t.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID  = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID 
ORDER BY CREATE_DATE DESC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_LIST_BY_TAG_SP]
@Q_BLOG_TAG_ID SMALLINT,
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID SMALLINT
 AS
SELECT     TOP 100 dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_SUBJECT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_TEXT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID, 
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V.COMMENT_COUNT, byline
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V ON dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V.Q_BLOG_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T ON dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_ID
where publish = 1 and Q_BLOG_T.q_blog_title_id = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID  and q_blog_tag_id = @Q_BLOG_TAG_ID
ORDER BY dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE DESC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_LIST_DISPLAY_BY_MONTH_SP] 
@YEAR SMALLINT,
@MONTH TINYINT,
@USER_ID INT, 
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID SMALLINT
AS
SELECT BLOG_SUBJECT, Q_BLOG_ID, PUBLISH, CREATE_DATE
FROM Q_BLOG_T
WHERE  (MONTH(CREATE_DATE) = @MONTH AND YEAR(CREATE_DATE) = @YEAR) AND Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID  = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID 
ORDER BY CREATE_DATE DESC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_LIST_LAST_POSTS_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
	@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID SMALLINT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT     TOP 10 dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_SUBJECT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_TEXT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID, 
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V.COMMENT_COUNT, byline
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V ON dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_COMMENT_COUNT_V.Q_BLOG_ID
WHERE      Q_blog_t.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID  = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID 
ORDER BY CREATE_DATE DESC

END
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Q_BLOG_PAGE_V_PAGE_SP]
@PageSize int,  
@CurrentPage int,  
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID SMALLINT,      
@ItemCount int output     
AS 
Declare @UpperBand int, @LowerBand int
-- Get The Count Of The Rows That They Meet the Criteria 
SET @ItemCount = (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM Q_BLOG_PAGE_V where q_blog_title_id = @q_blog_title_id)    
-- Calculate the @LowerCount and @UpperCount    
SET @LowerBand  = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize    
SET @UpperBand  = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize) + 1   
-- -- create a temporaty table     
CREATE TABLE #AllRows(             
RowNumber int IDENTITY, 
	BLOG_SUBJECT varchar(50),
	BLOG_TEXT VARCHAR(500),
	CREATE_DATE smalldatetime,
	Q_BLOG_ID int,
	COMMENT_COUNT int)
   -- INSERT ALL THE Rows that meets the Criteria 
	 INSERT INTO #AllRows ( 		[BLOG_SUBJECT],
		[BLOG_TEXT],
		[CREATE_DATE],
		[Q_BLOG_ID],
		[COMMENT_COUNT])
	 select 			[BLOG_SUBJECT],
			SUBSTRING([BLOG_TEXT], 1, 500) AS BLOG_TEXT,
			[CREATE_DATE],
			[Q_BLOG_ID],
			[COMMENT_COUNT]
	From Q_BLOG_PAGE_V
	WHERE Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
	ORDER BY [CREATE_DATE] DESC 
	  -- AND finally select and return desired -Paged- Rows  
	 SELECT RowNumber ,
		[BLOG_SUBJECT],
		[BLOG_TEXT],
		[CREATE_DATE],
		[Q_BLOG_ID],
		[COMMENT_COUNT] FROM #AllRows WHERE RowNumber > @LowerBand AND RowNumber < @UpperBand RETURN
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_BLOG_POPULAR_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_POPULAR_SP]
AS
SELECT     TOP 15  COUNT(dbo.Q_BLOG_LOG_T.Q_BLOG_LOG_ID) AS THECOUNT, dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.BLOG_TITLE, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, 
                      dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.BLOG_URL
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_LOG_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.USER_ID ON 
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_LOG_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
WHERE     (dbo.Q_BLOG_LOG_T.LOG_DATE >= GETDATE() - 7)
GROUP BY dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.BLOG_TITLE, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.BLOG_URL
ORDER BY THECOUNT DESC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_RECENTLY_UPDATED_SP] 
AS
SELECT     TOP 20 dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.BLOG_TITLE, dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.BLOG_URL, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, 
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_SUBJECT AS blog_subject, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE, [Q_BLOG_MAX_DATE_V].[Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID]
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.USER_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_T ON dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_MAX_DATE_V ON dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE = dbo.Q_BLOG_MAX_DATE_V.maxdate
WHERE     (dbo.Q_BLOG_T.PUBLISH = 1)
ORDER BY dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE DESC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_RSS_BY_POST_SP]
@Q_BLOG_ID SMALLINT
AS
SELECT     TOP 10 dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_SUBJECT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.BLOG_TEXT, dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE, 
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_ATTACH_T.FILE_NAME, dbo.Q_BLOG_ATTACH_T.FILE_SIZE
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_T LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_ATTACH_T ON dbo.Q_BLOG_T.Q_BLOG_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_ATTACH_T.Q_BLOG_ID
WHERE Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = (select Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID from q_blog_id where q_blog_id = @q_blog_id) and publish = 1
ORDER BY dbo.Q_BLOG_T.CREATE_DATE DESC
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_BLOG_SETTINGS_UPDATE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_SETTINGS_UPDATE_SP] 
@BLOG_TITLE VARCHAR(50),
@BLOG_URL VARCHAR(25),
@USER_ID INT,
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID SMALLINT,
@BLOG_DESCRIPTION varchar(200),
@BLOG_COUNTER varchar(600),
@ANONYMOUS TINYINT
AS
DECLARE @RETURN TINYINT
IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT USER_ID FROM Q_BLOG_TITLE_T WHERE BLOG_URL = @BLOG_URL and USER_ID <> @USER_ID)
	BEGIN
		IF @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = 0 
			BEGIN
				INSERT INTO
				Q_BLOG_TITLE_T
				(
				BLOG_TITLE,
				BLOG_URL,
				USER_ID,
				BLOG_DESCRIPTION,
				BLOG_COUNTER,
				ANONYMOUS
				)
				VALUES
				(
				@BLOG_TITLE,
				@BLOG_URL,
				@USER_ID,
				@BLOG_DESCRIPTION,
				@BLOG_COUNTER,
@ANONYMOUS
				)
				SET @RETURN = 1
			END
		ELSE
			BEGIN
				UPDATE Q_BLOG_TITLE_T
				SET
				BLOG_TITLE = @BLOG_TITLE,
				BLOG_URL = @BLOG_URL,
				BLOG_DESCRIPTION = @BLOG_DESCRIPTION ,
				BLOG_COUNTER = @BLOG_COUNTER,
				ANONYMOUS = @ANONYMOUS
				WHERE
				Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
				SET @RETURN = 1
			END
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		SET @RETURN = 0
	END
SELECT @RETURN
RETURN @RETURN
GO

GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_TAG_COUNT_FROM_BLOG_TITLE_SP]
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID SMALLINT
AS
SELECT     dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID, dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T.TAG_NAME, COUNT(dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID) AS thecount
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T RIGHT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T ON dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID
WHERE     dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
GROUP BY dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID, dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T.TAG_NAME
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_TAG_COUNT_SP]
@Q_BLOG_ID SMALLINT
AS
SELECT     dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID, dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T.TAG_NAME, COUNT(dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID) AS thecount
FROM         dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T RIGHT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T ON dbo.Q_BLOG_CONTENT_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID = dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID
WHERE     dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = (select q_blog_title_id from q_blog_t where q_blog_id = @Q_BLOG_ID)
GROUP BY dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T.Q_BLOG_TAG_ID, dbo.Q_BLOG_TAG_T.TAG_NAME
GO

CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Q_BLOG_TAG_LIST_SP]
@Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID INT
As
Begin
	Select 
		[Q_BLOG_TAG_ID],
		[TAG_NAME],
		[Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID],
		[TAG_TYPE]
	From Q_BLOG_TAG_T
WHERE Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = @Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID and tag_type = 0 
ORDER BY TAG_NAME ASC
End

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BLOG_USER_LIST_SP]
@USER_ID INT
AS
SELECT    Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID, Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.BLOG_TITLE, Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.BLOG_URL
FROM         Q_BLOG_TITLE_T LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      Q_BLOG_ACCESS_T ON Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID = Q_BLOG_ACCESS_T.Q_BLOG_TITLE_ID
WHERE dbo.Q_BLOG_TITLE_T.USER_ID = @USER_ID or  Q_BLOG_ACCESS_T.USER_ID = @USER_ID
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BUDDY_ADD_SP]
@USER_ID INT,
@BUDDY_ID INT
AS
IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT [USER_ID] FROM Q_BUDDY_T WHERE [USER_ID] = @USER_ID AND BUDDY_ID = @BUDDY_ID)
	BEGIN
		INSERT INTO Q_BUDDY_T
		(
		USER_ID,
		BUDDY_ID
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@USER_ID,
		@BUDDY_ID
		)
		
	END
GO

DELETE FROM

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BUDDY_LIST_PUBLIC_SP]
@USER_ID INT
AS
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.USERS_T.ONLINE_NOW, 
                      dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.USER_ID AS Expr1, dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.DISPLAY, 
                      dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.THUMB_WIDTH, dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.THUMB_HEIGHT, 
                      isnull(dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.THUMB, '') as thumb, ban
FROM         dbo.Q_BUDDY_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_BUDDY_T.BUDDY_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V ON dbo.Q_BUDDY_T.BUDDY_ID = dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.USER_ID
WHERE Q_BUDDY_T.USER_ID = @USER_ID AND BAN = 0
ORDER BY USERNAME ASC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_BUDDY_LIST_SP]
@USER_ID INT
AS
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.USERS_T.ONLINE_NOW, 
                      dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.USER_ID AS Expr1, dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.DISPLAY, 
                      dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.THUMB_WIDTH, dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.THUMB_HEIGHT, 
                      isnull(dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.THUMB, '') as thumb, ban
FROM         dbo.Q_BUDDY_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_BUDDY_T.BUDDY_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V ON dbo.Q_BUDDY_T.BUDDY_ID = dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.USER_ID
WHERE Q_BUDDY_T.USER_ID = @USER_ID
ORDER BY USERNAME ASC
GO

-- ==========================================================================================
-- Entity Name:	Q_COMMENT_T_ADD_SP
-- Author:	Richard Orchard
-- Create date:	6/21/2009 7:11:09 PM
-- Description:	This stored procedure is intended for inserting values to Q_COMMENT_T table
-- ==========================================================================================
Create Procedure [dbo].[Q_COMMENT_T_ADD_SP]
	@USER_ID int,
	@COMMENT varchar(2000),
	@COMMENT_PRIMARY_kEY int,
	@COMMENT_SECTION tinyint
	As
Begin
	Insert Into Q_COMMENT_T
		([USER_ID],[COMMENT],[COMMENT_PRIMARY_kEY],[COMMENT_SECTION])
	Values
		(@USER_ID,@COMMENT,@COMMENT_PRIMARY_kEY,@COMMENT_SECTION)

	Declare @ReferenceID int
	Select @ReferenceID = @@IDENTITY

	Return @ReferenceID

End
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_COMMENT_T_LIST_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

-- ==========================================================================================
-- Entity Name:	Q_COMMENT_T_LIST_SP
-- Author:	Richard Orchard
-- Create date:	6/21/2009 7:11:09 PM
-- Description:	This stored procedure is intended for selecting all rows from Q_COMMENT_T table
-- ==========================================================================================
CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Q_COMMENT_T_LIST_SP]
@COMMENT_PRIMARY_KEY INT,
@COMMENT_SECTION TINYINT
As
Begin
	SELECT     Q_COMMENT_T.Q_COMMENT_ID, Q_COMMENT_T.USER_ID, Q_COMMENT_T.COMMENT, Q_COMMENT_T.COMMENT_PRIMARY_kEY, 
                      Q_COMMENT_T.COMMENT_SECTION, Q_COMMENT_T.DATE_CREATED, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.USERS_T.ONLINE_NOW AS ONLINE
FROM         Q_COMMENT_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON Q_COMMENT_T.USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID
	WHERE COMMENT_PRIMARY_KEY = @COMMENT_PRIMARY_KEY AND COMMENT_SECTION = @COMMENT_SECTION
ORDER BY Q_COMMENT_T.DATE_CREATED ASC	
End
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FIND_MEMBER_ID_BY_EMAIL_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@EMAIL varchar(100)
AS

BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
SET NOCOUNT ON;

DECLARE @nLogin int 
 
set @nLogin = 0


if exists (SELECT  USER_ID
FROM         dbo.USERS_T where EMAIL = @EMAIL )
begin

set @nLogin = (SELECT  USER_ID
FROM         dbo.USERS_T where EMAIL = @EMAIL )

end 
	 
	 select @nLogin
	 RETURN @nLogin
	 
END

GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_DUPLICATE_TOPIC_SUBJECT_SP] 
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
--	<@Param1, sysname, @p1> <Datatype_For_Param1, , int> = <Default_Value_For_Param1, , 0>, 
--	<@Param2, sysname, @p2> <Datatype_For_Param2, , int> = <Default_Value_For_Param2, , 0>
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT topic_subject, COUNT(*) TotalCount
FROM q_forum_topic_t
where q_forum_topic_parent_id = 0
GROUP BY topic_subject
HAVING COUNT(topic_subject) > 1
ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC 

END
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_HOT_TOPICS_FRONT_SP] 
AS
SELECT     TOP 10 Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, TOPIC_SUBJECT
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
WHERE     (TOPIC_LAST_POST > { fn NOW() } - 2) AND (Q_FORUM_ID = 1 OR
                      Q_FORUM_ID = 4 OR Q_FORUM_ID = 9  OR Q_FORUM_ID = 10 ) and (topic_date > { fn NOW() } - 2) and DISCOGRAPHY <> 2
ORDER BY dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_REPLIES DESC
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FORUM_HOT_TOPICS_NEWSLETTER_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_HOT_TOPICS_NEWSLETTER_SP] 
AS
SELECT     TOP 6 Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, TOPIC_SUBJECT
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
WHERE     (TOPIC_LAST_POST > { fn NOW() } - 7) AND (Q_FORUM_ID = 1 OR
                      Q_FORUM_ID = 4 OR Q_FORUM_ID = 9  OR Q_FORUM_ID = 10 ) and (topic_date > { fn NOW() } - 7)
ORDER BY dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_REPLIES DESC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_MAIN_SP] AS
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT Q_FORUM_ID, Q_FORUM_NAME, Q_FORUM_DESCRIPTION, Q_FORUM_POST_COUNT, Q_FORUM_LAST_POST
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_T
GROUP BY Q_FORUM_ID, Q_FORUM_NAME, Q_FORUM_DESCRIPTION, FORUM_ORDER, Q_FORUM_NAME, Q_FORUM_DESCRIPTION, 
                      Q_FORUM_POST_COUNT, Q_FORUM_LAST_POST
ORDER BY FORUM_ORDER

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FORUM_PAGE_CACHE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_PAGE_CACHE_SP] 
@Q_FORUM_ID SMALLINT
AS
SELECT DISTINCT top 500
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.TOPIC_SUBJECT, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.TOPIC_LAST_POST, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.TOPIC_REPLIES AS NUMBEROFREPLIES, USERS_T_1.USERNAME AS LAST_POST_USERNAME,
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.STICKY
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.USER_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T USERS_T_1 ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.LAST_USER_ID = USERS_T_1.USER_ID
WHERE Q_FORUM_ID = @Q_FORUM_ID and users_t.validated = 1 
order by STICKY DESC, topic_last_post desc
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_POST_EDIT_SP]
@USER_ID INT,
@TOPIC_SUBJECT NVARCHAR(75), 
@TOPIC_MESSAGE VARCHAR(8000), 
@POST_IP NVARCHAR(20),
@Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID INT,
@STICKY SMALLINT,
@Parent_id int
 AS
UPDATE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
SET
TOPIC_SUBJECT = @TOPIC_SUBJECT,
TOPIC_MESSAGE = @TOPIC_MESSAGE,
POST_IP = @POST_IP,
STICKY = @STICKY,
TOPIC_EDIT_DATE = GETDATE()
WHERE
Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID
And USER_ID = @USER_ID

SELECT 1, Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, [Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T].[TOPIC_SUBJECT] from Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T 
WHERE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @parent_Id
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FORUM_POST_REPLY_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_POST_REPLY_SP] 
@USER_ID INT,
@TOPIC_MESSAGE VARCHAR(8000),
@POST_IP_ADDRESS NVARCHAR(20),
@Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID INT,
@STICKY SMALLINT,
@ATTACHMENT VARCHAR(120),
@FILESIZE char(12)
AS

DECLARE @Q_FORUM_ID TINYINT

IF EXISTS (SELECT USER_ID FROM USERS_T WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID AND VALIDATED = 1)
BEGIN

SELECT @Q_FORUM_ID = Q_FORUM_ID 
FROM Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
WHERE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID

print(@Q_FORUM_ID)

INSERT INTO Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T 
(
USER_ID,
TOPIC_MESSAGE, 
POST_IP, 
Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID, 
TOPIC_SUBJECT, 
Q_FORUM_ID,
STICKY,
ATTACHMENT,
FILESIZE 
) 
VALUES
 (
@USER_ID,
@TOPIC_MESSAGE,
@POST_IP_ADDRESS,
@Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID,
' ',
@Q_FORUM_ID,
@STICKY,
@ATTACHMENT,
@FILESIZE 
)

Declare @CurrentPostId int
Set @CurrentPostId = @@Identity


DECLARE @THEDATE SMALLDATETIME
SET @THEDATE =  GETDATE()

print(@thedate)

UPDATE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
SET TOPIC_LAST_POST =@THEDATE,
TOPIC_REPLIES = (TOPIC_REPLIES + 1),
LAST_USER_ID = @USER_ID
WHERE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID 


UPDATE Q_FORUM_T
SET 
Q_FORUM_LAST_POST = @THEDATE,
Q_FORUM_POST_COUNT = (Q_FORUM_POST_COUNT + 1)
WHERE Q_FORUM_ID = @Q_FORUM_ID 
UPDATE USERS_T
SET
NUMBER_OF_POSTS = (NUMBER_OF_POSTS + 1)
WHERE
USER_ID = @USER_ID


SELECT [Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T].[TOPIC_REPLIES], @CurrentPostId, TOPIC_SUBJECT
FROM
Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
WHERE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID 


END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FORUM_POST_TOPIC_NEWS_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_POST_TOPIC_NEWS_SP] 
@Q_FORUM_ID INT, 
@USER_ID INT,
@TOPIC_SUBJECT NVARCHAR(75), 
@TOPIC_MESSAGE VARCHAR(8000), 
@POST_IP NVARCHAR(20),
@STICKY SMALLINT,
@ATTACHMENT VARCHAR(120),
@FILESIZE char(12),
@NEWS_ID SMALLINT
AS
Set Nocount on 

DECLARE @THEDATE SMALLDATETIME
DECLARE @THEINT INT
DECLARE @RETURNVALUE INT

SET @THEDATE =  GETDATE()

print('at the sp')

IF EXISTS (SELECT USER_ID  FROM USERS_T WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID AND VALIDATED = 1)

print('validated user')

	BEGIN

IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID FROM Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T WHERE NEWS_ID = @NEWS_ID)
BEGIN

print('news id check is passed')

insert into 
Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
(
Q_FORUM_ID, 
USER_ID, 
TOPIC_SUBJECT, 
TOPIC_MESSAGE, 
TOPIC_LAST_POST, 
POST_IP,
STICKY,
ATTACHMENT,
FILESIZE,
LAST_USER_ID,
TOPIC_STARTER,
NEWS_ID
) 
values 
(
@Q_FORUM_ID, 
@USER_ID, 
@TOPIC_SUBJECT, 
@TOPIC_MESSAGE, 
@THEDATE, 
@POST_IP,
@STICKY,
@ATTACHMENT,
@FILESIZE,
@USER_ID,
1,
@NEWS_ID
)

print('added record to forums db')

UPDATE Q_FORUM_T
SET 
Q_FORUM_LAST_POST = @THEDATE,
Q_FORUM_POST_COUNT = (Q_FORUM_POST_COUNT + 1)
WHERE Q_FORUM_ID = @Q_FORUM_ID 
UPDATE USERS_T
SET
NUMBER_OF_POSTS = (NUMBER_OF_POSTS + 1)
WHERE
USER_ID = @USER_ID
-- SELECT @THEINT = @@IDENTITY
-- UPDATE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
-- SET Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = @THEINT
-- WHERE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @THEINT
-- RETURN @RETURNVALUE
UPDATE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
SET Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = @@IDENTITY 
WHERE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @@IDENTITY 


select @@identity
return @@identity


END 

END

set nocount off
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FORUM_POST_TOPIC_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_POST_TOPIC_SP] 
@Q_FORUM_ID INT, 
@USER_ID INT,
@TOPIC_SUBJECT NVARCHAR(75), 
@TOPIC_MESSAGE VARCHAR(8000), 
@POST_IP NVARCHAR(20),
@STICKY SMALLINT,
@ATTACHMENT VARCHAR(120),
@FILESIZE char(12),
@DISCOGRAPHY TINYINT
AS
Set Nocount on 
DECLARE @THEDATE SMALLDATETIME
DECLARE @THEINT INT
DECLARE @RETURNVALUE INT
SET @THEDATE =  GETDATE()

Declare @find varchar(100) 
set @find = 'ccv'


Declare @subject nvarchar(75)
select @subject = lower(@TOPIC_SUBJECT)


Declare @findBuy varchar(100) 
set @findBuy = 'buy'

Declare @findICQ varchar(100) 
set @findICQ = 'icq'

if (charindex(@find, @subject) > 0)
    return 

if (charindex(@findBuy, @subject) > 0)
    return 

if (charindex(@findICQ, @subject) > 0)
    return 


IF EXISTS (SELECT user_id  FROM USERS_T WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID AND VALIDATED = 1)
	BEGIN
insert into 
Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
(
Q_FORUM_ID, 
USER_ID, 
TOPIC_SUBJECT, 
TOPIC_MESSAGE, 
TOPIC_LAST_POST, 
POST_IP,
STICKY,
ATTACHMENT,
FILESIZE,
LAST_USER_ID,
TOPIC_STARTER,
DISCOGRAPHY
) 
values 
(
@Q_FORUM_ID, 
@USER_ID, 
@TOPIC_SUBJECT, 
@TOPIC_MESSAGE, 
@THEDATE, 
@POST_IP,
@STICKY,
@ATTACHMENT,
@FILESIZE,
@USER_ID,
1,
@DISCOGRAPHY
)

UPDATE Q_FORUM_T
SET 
Q_FORUM_LAST_POST = @THEDATE,
Q_FORUM_POST_COUNT = (Q_FORUM_POST_COUNT + 1)
WHERE Q_FORUM_ID = @Q_FORUM_ID 
UPDATE USERS_T
SET
NUMBER_OF_POSTS = (NUMBER_OF_POSTS + 1)
WHERE
USER_ID = @USER_ID
-- SELECT @THEINT = @@IDENTITY
-- UPDATE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
-- SET Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = @THEINT
-- WHERE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @THEINT
-- RETURN @RETURNVALUE


UPDATE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
SET Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = @@IDENTITY 
WHERE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @@IDENTITY 
END

SELECT  @@IDENTITY
SET  @RETURNVALUE = @@IDENTITY

RETURN @RETURNVALUE
set nocount off
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_QUOTE_SP] 
@Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID int
AS
SELECT     dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_MESSAGE
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.USER_ID
WHERE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FORUM_RSS_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_RSS_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@Q_FORUM_ID TINYINT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here


	SELECT     TOP 20 dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_DATE, '<p>Posted by ' +  dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME + '</p> ' + dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_MESSAGE as topic_message, 
                      Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1.TOPIC_SUBJECT
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T AS Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1 ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID
WHERE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_ID = @Q_FORUM_ID
ORDER BY dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_DATE DESC

END
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS OFF

SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_SEARCH_SP] 
@SEARCHSTUFF VARCHAR(400),
@USERNAME VARCHAR(50),
@Q_FORUM_ID tinyint
AS
DECLARE @STEST varchar(1000)
DECLARE @KEYWORDS VARCHAR(400)
DECLARE @SUSER varchar(35)
DECLARE @USER_ID INT
SET @USER_ID = 0 
		
		print(@searchstuff)
		SET @STEST = 'select distinct q_forum_topic_parent_id from q_forum_topic_t where '
		print(@STEST)
		
		IF @SEARCHSTUFF <> '' 
		--SET @KEYWORDS =  replace(@SEARCHSTUFF, "'", "''")
			BEGIN 
				SET @KEYWORDS =  'contains(*, ''' + convert(varchar,  replace(@SEARCHSTUFF, "'", "''")) + ''')'
				 print @KEYWORDS
			END 
		
		IF @USERNAME <> ''
			BEGIN
				SELECT TOP 1 @USER_ID = USER_ID FROM USERS_T WHERE USERNAME = @USERNAME
				
				IF @USER_ID > 1 					
					BEGIN
						SET @SUSER = ' USER_ID = ''' + convert(varchar, @USER_ID) + ''''
						print('yes')
					END 
			END 	
		IF @SEARCHSTUFF <> '' AND @USER_ID > 0 
			BEGIN
				SET @STEST = @STEST +  @KEYWORDS + ' AND ' + @SUSER
			END 
		ELSE IF @SEARCHSTUFF <> '' AND @USER_ID = 0
			BEGIN
				
				SET @STEST = @STEST +  @KEYWORDS
			END 
		ELSE IF @SEARCHSTUFF = '' AND @USER_ID > 0
			BEGIN
				SET @STEST = @STEST +  @SUSER
			END
		ELSE
			begin
				print('what')
			end
			
		IF @Q_FORUM_ID > 0	
			BEGIN  
			SET @STEST = @STEST + ' AND Q_FORUM_ID = ' + convert(varchar, @Q_FORUM_ID)
			END	
			
		SET @STEST = 'SELECT     dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.TOPIC_SUBJECT, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.TOPIC_LAST_POST, dbo.Q_FORUM_T.Q_FORUM_NAME, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.Q_FORUM_ID, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.LAST_USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_T ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.Q_FORUM_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_T.Q_FORUM_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.LAST_USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID where q_forum_topic_id in (' + @STEST + ') ORDER BY topic_last_post desc'		
		print @STEST
		EXEC(@STEST)
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FORUM_SEARCH_USER_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_SEARCH_USER_SP] 
@USERNAME VARCHAR(100)
AS
DECLARE @USER_ID INT
SELECT @USER_ID = USER_ID FROM USERS_T WHERE USERNAME = @USERNAME
select  Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, TOPIC_SUBJECT, TOPIC_LAST_POST  
from Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V 
where q_forum_topic_id in (SELECT DISTINCT Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID
FROM
Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID)
order by topic_last_post desc
GO

	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_MAIL_SUBSCRIBE_SP]
@USER_ID INT,
@Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID INT
AS
IF NOT EXISTS 
	(SELECT * FROM Q_FORUM_MAIL_T
	WHERE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID AND @USER_ID = @USER_ID)
		BEGIN
			INSERT INTO  Q_FORUM_MAIL_T
		(
		Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID,
		USER_ID
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID,
		@USER_ID
		)
		END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NEW_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NEW_SP]
	(
	@CurrentPage As int,
	@PageSize As int,
	 @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID int,
	@USER_ID int,
	 @TotalRecords int OUTPUT,
	@SUBSCRIBED INT OUTPUT,
	@forum_name VARCHAR(30) OUTPUT,
	@SUBJECT VARCHAR(75) OUTPUT,
	@Q_FORUM_ID INT OUTPUT,
@DISCO TINYINT OUTPUT
	)
AS
SET NOCOUNT ON
Declare @FirstRec int
Declare @LastRec int
-- Initialize variables.
Set @FirstRec = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize
Set @LastRec = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize + 1)
--Create a temporary table
DECLARE @TempTable Table
(	
	
	ID int IDENTITY,
	TOPIC_MESSAGE varchar(8000),
	TOPIC_DATE smalldatetime,
	USER_ID int,
	USERNAME char(40),
	SIGNATURE varchar(200),
	NUMBER_OF_POSTS smallint,
	DATE_CREATED smalldatetime,
	Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID int,
ATTACHMENT varchar(120),
FILESIZE char(12),
ATTACH_COUNT SMALLINT,
ONLINE TINYINT,
AVATAR VARCHAR(50),
DISPLAY_MESSAGE varchar(30),
DISCO TINYINT
)
-- 10
-- Insert the rows from tblItems into the temp.table
INSERT INTO 
@TempTable
( 
TOPIC_MESSAGE, 
TOPIC_DATE, 
USER_ID, 
USERNAME, 
SIGNATURE, 
NUMBER_OF_POSTS, 
DATE_CREATED, 
Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID,
ATTACHMENT,
FILESIZE,
ATTACH_COUNT,
ONLINE,
AVATAR,
DISPLAY_MESSAGE,
DISCO
)
SELECT distinct      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_MESSAGE, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_DATE, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, 
                     isnull( dbo.USERS_T.SIGNATURE, '') as SIGNATURE, dbo.USERS_T.NUMBER_OF_POSTS, dbo.USERS_T.DATE_CREATED, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.ATTACHMENT, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.FILESIZE, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.ATTACH_COUNT, dbo.USERS_T.ONLINE_NOW, dbo.Q_USERS_AVATAR_V.AVATAR, DISPLAY_MESSAGE, DISCOGRAPHY
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.USER_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_USERS_AVATAR_V ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_USERS_AVATAR_V.USER_ID
where (Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID  or Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID )
AND DISCOGRAPHY <> 2 
and users_t.validated = 1
ORDER BY TOPIC_DATE ASC
-- Now, return the set of paged records, plus, an indiciation of we
-- have more records or not!
SELECT 

isnull(TOPIC_MESSAGE, '') as TOPIC_MESSAGE ,
	TOPIC_DATE ,
	USER_ID,
	USERNAME,
	SIGNATURE,
	NUMBER_OF_POSTS,
	DATE_CREATED,
	Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID,
ATTACHMENT,
FILESIZE,
ATTACH_COUNT,
ONLINE,
AVATAR,
DISPLAY_MESSAGE,
DISCO


FROM @TempTable
WHERE ID > @FirstRec AND ID < @LastRec
order by TOPIC_DATE  asc
--Return the total number of records available as an output parameter
Select
@TotalRecords = Count(*)
From 
Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T 
WHERE
Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID  or Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID


SELECT 
@SUBSCRIBED = COUNT(Q_FORUM_MAIL_ID)
FROM Q_FORUM_MAIL_T
WHERE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID AND USER_ID = @USER_ID

SELECT    @Q_FORUM_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_ID, @forum_name = dbo.Q_FORUM_T.Q_FORUM_NAME, @SUBJECT = dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_SUBJECT,
@DISCO = DISCOGRAPHY
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T ON dbo.Q_FORUM_T.Q_FORUM_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_ID
WHERE   dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID
SET NOCOUNT OFF
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_LIST_BY_FORUM_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_LIST_BY_FORUM_SP]
@Q_FORUM_ID TINYINT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT     TOPIC_SUBJECT, Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, ISNULL(TOPIC_LAST_POST, '') AS TOPIC_DATE
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
WHERE     (TOPIC_STARTER = 1) AND Q_FORUM_ID = @Q_FORUM_ID
ORDER BY Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID DESC
END
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_LIST_SP]

AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT     TOPIC_SUBJECT, Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, ISNULL(TOPIC_LAST_POST, '') AS TOPIC_DATE
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
WHERE     (TOPIC_STARTER = 1)
ORDER BY Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID DESC
END

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_QUICK_VIEW_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID INT

AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

SELECT distinct      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_MESSAGE, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_DATE, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, 
                      dbo.USERS_T.SIGNATURE, dbo.USERS_T.NUMBER_OF_POSTS, dbo.USERS_T.DATE_CREATED, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.ATTACHMENT, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.FILESIZE, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.ATTACH_COUNT, dbo.USERS_T.ONLINE_NOW AS ONLINE, dbo.Q_USERS_AVATAR_V.AVATAR, DISPLAY_MESSAGE, DISCOGRAPHY
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.USER_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_USERS_AVATAR_V ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_USERS_AVATAR_V.USER_ID
where (Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID  or Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID )
AND DISCOGRAPHY <> 2 and users_t.validated = 1
ORDER BY TOPIC_DATE ASC


    -- Insert statements for procedure here
END
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_RSS_SP]
	@Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID INT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME as topic_subject, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_MESSAGE, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_DATE 
                      
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.USER_ID
                      where Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.q_forum_topic_id = @q_forum_topic_id or q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID
ORDER BY dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID DESC
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_SUBSCRIBE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_SUBSCRIBE_SP]
(
  @USER_ID int, 
  @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID int
)
AS
IF EXISTS(SELECT 'True' FROM Q_FORUM_MAIL_T WHERE Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID AND USER_ID = @USER_ID)
BEGIN
  --This means it exists, return it to ASP and tell us
  SELECT 'This record already exists!'
END
ELSE
BEGIN
  --This means the record isn't in there already, let's go ahead and add it
  SELECT 'Record Added'
  INSERT into Q_FORUM_MAIL_T(USER_ID, Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID) VALUES(@USER_ID, @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID)
END
GO
