CREATE PROCEDURE  [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TOPIC_VIEW_SP]
@Q_FORUM_ID INT
AS
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_SUBJECT, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_LAST_POST, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_REPLY_COUNT_V.NUMBEROFREPLIES, dbo.Q_FORUM_T.Q_FORUM_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_T.Q_FORUM_NAME
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_T ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_T.Q_FORUM_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_REPLY_COUNT_V ON 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_REPLY_COUNT_V.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID
WHERE     (dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID IS NULL) OR
                      (dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = 0) AND (dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_ID = @Q_FORUM_ID) AND (DISCOGRAPHY <> 2)
                      
ORDER BY dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_LAST_POST DESC
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TORRENT_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_TORRENT_SP] 
AS
SELECT DISTINCT top 500
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.TOPIC_SUBJECT, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.TOPIC_LAST_POST, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.TOPIC_REPLIES AS NUMBEROFREPLIES, USERS_T_1.USERNAME AS LAST_POST_USERNAME,
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.STICKY
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.USER_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T USERS_T_1 ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.LAST_USER_ID = USERS_T_1.USER_ID
WHERE 
TOPIC_STARTER = 1 AND ATTACHMENT LIKE '%.torrent'
and Q_forum_id = 4
order by STICKY DESC, topic_last_post desc
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_VIEW_PAGE_ALL_SP]
	 
	@Q_FORUM_ID INT
	
	As
-- Turn off count return.
-- Set NoCount On
SELECT DISTINCT 
                      TOP 100 PERCENT dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_SUBJECT, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_LAST_POST, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_REPLIES, USERS_T_1.USERNAME AS LAST_POST_USERNAME, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.STICKY
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1 ON 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_LAST_POST = Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1.TOPIC_LAST_POST INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T USERS_T_1 ON Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1.USER_ID = USERS_T_1.USER_ID
WHERE     (dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID > '' AND dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID < '' OR
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = 0) AND (dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_ID = @Q_FORUM_ID)
ORDER BY dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.STICKY DESC, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_LAST_POST DESC
--Return the total number of records available as an output parameter
--RETURN @TotalRecords
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FORUM_VIEW_PAGE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FORUM_VIEW_PAGE_SP]
@CurrentPage As int,
@PageSize As int,
@Q_FORUM_ID TINYINT,
 @TotalRecords int OUTPUT
 AS

SET NOCOUNT ON

Declare @FirstRec int
Declare @LastRec int

-- Initialize variables.

Set @FirstRec = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize
Set @LastRec = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize + 1)
--Create a temporary table

DECLARE @TempTable Table
(	
ID int IDENTITY,
Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID INT,
TOPIC_SUBJECT VARCHAR (150),
TOPIC_LAST_POST SMALLDATETIME,
USER_ID INT,
USERNAME VARCHAR(100),
NUMBEROFREPLIES SMALLINT,
LAST_POST_USERNAME VARCHAR(100),
STICKY TINYINT
)

INSERT INTO @TempTable
(
Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID ,
TOPIC_SUBJECT,
TOPIC_LAST_POST,
USER_ID,
USERNAME ,
NUMBEROFREPLIES,
LAST_POST_USERNAME,
STICKY

)
SELECT DISTINCT
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, 
dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.TOPIC_SUBJECT, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.TOPIC_LAST_POST, 
dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.TOPIC_REPLIES AS NUMBEROFREPLIES,
 USERS_T_1.USERNAME AS LAST_POST_USERNAME,
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.STICKY
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.USER_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T USERS_T_1 ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V.
LAST_USER_ID = USERS_T_1.USER_ID
WHERE Q_FORUM_ID = @Q_FORUM_ID and users_t.validated = 1 
order by STICKY DESC, TOPIC_LAST_POST desc



SELECT 
id,
Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID ,
TOPIC_SUBJECT,
TOPIC_LAST_POST,
USER_ID,
USERNAME ,
NUMBEROFREPLIES,
LAST_POST_USERNAME,
STICKY
FROM @TempTable
WHERE ID > @FirstRec AND ID < @LastRec
order by STICKY DESC, TOPIC_LAST_POST desc




SELECT @TotalRecords = Count(*)
FROM       dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
WHERE topic_starter = 1 AND Q_FORUM_ID = @Q_FORUM_ID
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FORUM_VIEW_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

AS
SELECT Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, TOPIC_SUBJECT, TOPIC_REPLIES, TOPIC_LAST_POST, USERNAME FROM FORUM_VIEW_V WHERE Q_FORUM_ID = @FORUM_ID  and 
TOPIC_LAST_POST >= @oldDate order by TOPIC_LAST_POST desc
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_FREDDIE_PAGE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Q_FREDDIE_PAGE_SP]
-- Declare parameters.
@CurrentPage As int,
@PageSize As int,
@TotalRecords int OUTPUT
As
-- Turn off count return.
Set NoCount On
-- Declare variables.
Declare @FirstRec int
Declare @LastRec int
-- Initialize variables.
Set @FirstRec = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize
Set @LastRec = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize + 1)
-- Create a temp table to hold the current page of data
-- Add an ID column to count the records
Create Table #TempTable
(
ID int IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
Name Nvarchar(200),
Thought VARCHAR(3500),
COUNTRY nvarchar(150),
FREDDIE_DATE nvarchar(50),
DISPLAY SMALLINT,
FREDDIE_ID INT
)
--Fill the temp table with the reminders
Insert Into #TempTable 
(
Name,
THOUGHT, 
COUNTRY, 
FREDDIE_DATE,
FREDDIE_ID
)
Select top 2500
NAME,
THOUGHT,
COUNTRY,
FREDDIE_DATE,
ID
From 
FREDDIE_T
WHERE DISPLAY = 1
Order By 
ID DESC
--Select one page of data based on the record numbers above
Select 
Name,
THOUGHT,
COUNTRY,
FREDDIE_DATE,
FREDDIE_ID
From 
#TempTable
Where 
Id > @FirstRec 
And Id < @LastRec
DROP TABLE #TempTable
--Return the total number of records available as an output parameter
Select
@TotalRecords = Count(*)
From 
FREDDIE_T
--RETURN @TotalRecords
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_FREDDIE_POST_SP]
@NAME varchar(200),
@EMAIL VARCHAR(60),
@COUNTRY VARCHAR(150),
@THOUGHT VARCHAR(3500),
@nsubscribe tinyint
AS
INSERT INTO FREDDIE_T
(
NAME,
EMAIL,
COUNTRY,
THOUGHT
)
VALUES
(
@NAME,
@EMAIL,
@COUNTRY,
@THOUGHT
)
if @nsubscribe = 1
	begin
		exec Q_NEWSLETTER_SP @EMAIL, 1
	end
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_GENERAL_RATING_DISPLAY_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_GENERAL_RATING_DISPLAY_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@RATING_SECTION smallint,
@RATING_PRIMARY_KEY int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here

	SELECT     COUNT(Q_RATING_ID) AS NUMBER_OF_VOTES, SUM(RATING) / COUNT(Q_RATING_ID) AS AVERAGE_VOTES
FROM         Q_GENERAL_RATING_T
WHERE RATING_SECTION = @RATING_SECTION AND RATING_PRIMARY_KEY = @RATING_PRIMARY_KEY

END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_GENERAL_RATING_HAS_VOTED_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@USER_ID int,
@RATING_SECTION SMALLINT,
@RATING_PRIMARY_KEY INT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT  count(   USER_ID)
FROM         Q_GENERAL_RATING_T
WHERE     (USER_ID = @user_id) AND (RATING_SECTION = @rating_section) AND (RATING_PRIMARY_KEY = @rating_primary_key)
	

END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_JOIN_RETURN_ID_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_JOIN_RETURN_ID_SP]
@USERNAME varchar(40),
@PASSWORD varchar(20),
@EMAIL varchar(100),
@COUNTRY_ID int,
@SIGNATURE varchar(200),
@nSubscribe tinyint,
@HOMEPAGE varchar(150),
@IP_ADDRESS varchar(50)
AS 
DECLARE @RETURNTHIS INT
IF EXISTS(SELECT USER_ID FROM USERS_T WHERE USERNAME = @USERNAME)
	SET @RETURNTHIS = 0
ELSE IF EXISTS(SELECT USER_ID FROM USERS_T WHERE EMAIL = @EMAIL)
	SET @RETURNTHIS = 2
ELSE
	BEGIN
		INSERT INTO USERS_T
		(
		USERNAME,
		PASSWORD,
		EMAIL,
		COUNTRY,
		SIGNATURE,
		HOMEPAGE,
		LAST_IP
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@USERNAME,
		@PASSWORD,
		@EMAIL,
		@COUNTRY_ID,
		@SIGNATURE,
		@HOMEPAGE,
		@IP_ADDRESS
		)
		select @@IDENTITY
		SET @RETURNTHIS = @@IDENTITY
		
		IF @nSubscribe = 1 
			BEGIN
				EXEC Q_NEWSLETTER_SP @EMAIL, 1
			END
		
	END
--	SELECT @RETURNTHIS
RETURN @RETURNTHIS
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_JOIN_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_JOIN_SP]
@USERNAME varchar(40),
@PASSWORD varchar(20),
@EMAIL varchar(100),
@COUNTRY_ID int,
@SIGNATURE varchar(200),
@nSubscribe tinyint,
@HOMEPAGE varchar(150),
@IP_ADDRESS varchar(50)
AS 
DECLARE @RETURNTHIS TINYINT
IF EXISTS(SELECT USER_ID FROM USERS_T WHERE USERNAME = @USERNAME)
	SET @RETURNTHIS = 0
ELSE IF EXISTS(SELECT USER_ID FROM USERS_T WHERE EMAIL = @EMAIL)
	SET @RETURNTHIS = 2
ELSE
	BEGIN
		INSERT INTO USERS_T
		(
		USERNAME,
		PASSWORD,
		EMAIL,
		COUNTRY,
		SIGNATURE,
		HOMEPAGE,
		LAST_IP
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@USERNAME,
		@PASSWORD,
		@EMAIL,
		@COUNTRY_ID,
		@SIGNATURE,
		@HOMEPAGE,
		@IP_ADDRESS
		)
		SET @RETURNTHIS = 1
		
		IF @nSubscribe = 1 
			BEGIN
				EXEC Q_NEWSLETTER_SP @EMAIL, 1
			END
		
	END
SELECT @RETURNTHIS
RETURN @RETURNTHIS
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ADD_SP]
@CATEGORY_NAME VARCHAR(50),
@Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID SMALLINT
 AS
IF @Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID = 0 
	BEGIN
		INSERT INTO
		Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T
		(
		CATEGORY_NAME
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@CATEGORY_NAME
		)
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		UPDATE
			Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T
			SET
			CATEGORY_NAME = @CATEGORY_NAME
			WHERE
			Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID = @Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID
	END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_LIST_COUNT_SP] AS
SELECT     dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID, dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T.CATEGORY_NAME, 
                      COUNT(dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID) AS theCount
FROM         dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T ON 
                      dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID = dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID
GROUP BY dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID, dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T.CATEGORY_NAME
ORDER BY dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T.CATEGORY_NAME ASC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_DISPLAY_SP]
@Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID INT
AS
SELECT     dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.TITLE_OF_ARTICLE, dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.ANSWER, 
                      dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID, dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID, 
                      dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T.CATEGORY_NAME, dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.DATE_ADDED, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, 
                      dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.DISPLAY
FROM         dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T ON 
                      dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID = dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID WHERE Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID = @Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_NEW_SP]
 AS
SELECT     dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID, dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.TITLE_OF_ARTICLE, 
                      dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_T.CATEGORY_NAME, dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.DATE_ADDED, 
                      dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID, dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.ANSWER

                      dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T ON

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_UPDATE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_UPDATE_SP]
@TITLE_OF_ARTICLE NVARCHAR(100),
@ANSWER VARCHAR(8000),
@Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID SMALLINT,
@Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID INT,
@USER_ID INT,
@DISPLAY TINYINT
AS

declare @return INT

IF @Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID = 0 
	BEGIN
		
INSERT INTO Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T
(
TITLE_OF_ARTICLE,
ANSWER,
Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID,
USER_ID,
DISPLAY
)
VALUES
(
@TITLE_OF_ARTICLE,
@ANSWER,
@Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID,
@USER_ID,
@DISPLAY 
)

SELECT @RETURN = @@IDENTITY 


	END
ELSE
	BEGIN


IF @USER_ID = 0 
	BEGIN
	UPDATE  Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T
SET
TITLE_OF_ARTICLE = @TITLE_OF_ARTICLE,
ANSWER = @ANSWER,
Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID = @Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID,
DISPLAY = @DISPLAY
WHERE Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID = @Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID
	
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
	
	UPDATE  Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T
SET
TITLE_OF_ARTICLE = @TITLE_OF_ARTICLE,
ANSWER = @ANSWER,
Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID = @Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_CATEGORY_ID,
USER_ID = @USER_ID,
DISPLAY = @DISPLAY
WHERE Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID = @Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID
	
	SET @RETURN = @Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID
	
	END



END

RETURN @RETURN
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_LOGIN_ROLES_SP] 
@EMAIL varchar(100),
@PASSWORD varchar(100)
AS
SELECT  USER_ID, USERNAME, ACCESS
FROM         dbo.USERS_T
where EMAIL = @EMAIL and PASSWORD = @PASSWORD
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_LOGIN_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_LOGIN_SP] 
@EMAIL varchar(100),
@PASSWORD varchar(100)
AS
DECLARE @nLogin int  
if exists(SELECT  USER_ID
FROM         dbo.USERS_T
where EMAIL = @EMAIL and PASSWORD = @PASSWORD and VALIDATED = 1)
	begin
		set @nLogin = 1
	end
ELSE
	
		IF exists(SELECT  USER_ID
FROM         dbo.USERS_T
where EMAIL = @EMAIL and PASSWORD = @PASSWORD and VALIDATED = 0)
		BEGIN
		set @nLogin = 2
		END
	
ELSE	
	
	
		IF not exists(SELECT  USER_ID
FROM         dbo.USERS_T
where EMAIL = @EMAIL)
		BEGIN
			set @nLogin = 3
		END 
	
ELSE
	BEGIN
		set @nLogin = 4
	END
select @nLogin
return @nLogin
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_LOGIN2_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_LOGIN2_SP] 
@EMAIL varchar(100),
@PASSWORD varchar(100)
AS
DECLARE @nLogin int  



if exists(SELECT  USER_ID
FROM         dbo.USERS_T
where EMAIL = @EMAIL and PASSWORD = @PASSWORD and VALIDATED = 1)
	begin
		set @nLogin = 1
	end
ELSE
	
		IF exists(SELECT  USER_ID
FROM         dbo.USERS_T
where EMAIL = @EMAIL and PASSWORD = @PASSWORD and VALIDATED = 0)
		BEGIN
		set @nLogin = 2
		END
	
ELSE	
	
	
		IF not exists(SELECT  USER_ID
FROM         dbo.USERS_T
where EMAIL = @EMAIL)
		BEGIN
			set @nLogin = 3
		END 
	
ELSE
	BEGIN
		set @nLogin = 4
	END

IF @nLogin = 1 
	BEGIN
		 SELECT  top 1 USER_ID, USERNAME, ACCESS, display_avatar
		FROM USERS_T
		WHERE EMAIL = @EMAIL and PASSWORD = @PASSWORD and validated = 1 
		order by user_id desc
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		select @nLogin
		return @nLogin
	END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_MEMBER_FAV_BAND_MEMBER_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_MEMBER_FAV_BAND_MEMBER_SP]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
	
	SELECT     dbo.Q_MEMBER_T.MEMBER_NAME, COUNT(dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID) AS THENUMBER
FROM         dbo.Q_MEMBER_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_MEMBER_T.Q_MEMBER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.Q_MEMBER_ID
GROUP BY dbo.Q_MEMBER_T.MEMBER_NAME
	
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_MEMBER_SHOW_EMAIL_SP] 
@USER_ID INT,
@FRIEND INT
AS
IF @FRIEND = 0 
	BEGIN
		SELECT USERNAME, EMAIL 
		FROM 
		USERS_T
		WHERE
		USER_ID = @USER_ID AND EMAIL_YES = 1
	END 
ELSE
	BEGIN
		SELECT USERNAME, Q_FRIENDS_EMAIL
		FROM 
		USERS_T
		WHERE
		USER_ID = @USER_ID
	END
GO

-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_MEMBER_STATS_FAV_ALBUM_SP]

AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

SELECT     dbo.Q_ALBUM_T.ALBUM_NAME, COUNT(dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID) AS THECOUNT
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_ALBUM_T ON dbo.USERS_T.Q_ALBUM_ID = dbo.Q_ALBUM_T.Q_ALBUM_ID
GROUP BY dbo.Q_ALBUM_T.ALBUM_NAME

END

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_MEMBER_VIEW_SP] 
@USER_ID INT
AS
SELECT     dbo.GENERAL_COUNTRY_T.COUNTRY_NAME, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.USERS_T.HOMEPAGE, dbo.USERS_T.PICTURE, 
                      dbo.USERS_T.PICTURE_TEXT, dbo.USERS_T.NUMBER_OF_POSTS, dbo.USERS_T.DATE_CREATED, dbo.Q_GENDER_T.GENDER, 
                      dbo.Q_MEMBER_T.MEMBER_NAME, dbo.Q_ALBUM_T.ALBUM_NAME, dbo.USERS_T.OCCUPATION_JOB, dbo.USERS_T.HOBBIES, 
                      dbo.USERS_T.GENERAL_INFORMATION, dbo.USERS_T.QUEEN_FAN_SINCE, DATE_OF_BIRTH, ADDITIONAL_LOCATION_INFORMATION, Q_FRIEND_ID, PEN_PAL, REAL_PAL,
UPLOADED, DOWNLOADED, display_message
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.GENERAL_COUNTRY_T ON dbo.USERS_T.COUNTRY = dbo.GENERAL_COUNTRY_T.GENERAL_COUNTRY_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_ALBUM_T ON dbo.USERS_T.Q_ALBUM_ID = dbo.Q_ALBUM_T.Q_ALBUM_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_GENDER_T ON dbo.USERS_T.Q_GENDER_ID = dbo.Q_GENDER_T.Q_GENDER_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_MEMBER_T ON dbo.USERS_T.Q_MEMBER_ID = dbo.Q_MEMBER_T.Q_MEMBER_ID
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID
GO

	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here

	-- interfering with SELECT statements.

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_MUSIC_CHART_T_ALBUM_LIST_SP]
@Q_ALBUM_ID smallint
AS
BEGIN

set nocount on

SELECT     Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.Q_MUSIC_CHART_ID, Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.Q_ALBUM_ID, Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.CHART_POSITION, Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.Q_AWARD_ID, 
                      Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.COUNTRY_ID, Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.USER_ID, Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.CREATE_DATE, Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.DISPLAY, 
                      Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.ADDITIONAL_NOTES, GENERAL_COUNTRY_T.COUNTRY_NAME, USERS_T.USERNAME, Q_AWARD_T.AWARD_NAME
FROM         Q_MUSIC_CHART_T INNER JOIN
                      USERS_T ON Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.USER_ID = USERS_T.USER_ID INNER JOIN
                      GENERAL_COUNTRY_T ON Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.COUNTRY_ID = GENERAL_COUNTRY_T.GENERAL_COUNTRY_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      Q_AWARD_T ON Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.Q_AWARD_ID = Q_AWARD_T.Q_AWARD_ID  
			where Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.q_album_id = @Q_ALBUM_ID
			and Q_MUSIC_CHART_T.q_album_song_id = 0
		order by
			Q_MUSIC_CHART_ID

END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_MUSIC_CHART_T_UPDATE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO



CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_MUSIC_CHART_T_UPDATE_SP]
	( @Q_MUSIC_CHART_ID int = 0
	, @Q_ALBUM_ID int = null
	, @CHART_POSITION int = null
	, @Q_AWARD_ID int = null
	, @COUNTRY_ID int = null
	, @USER_ID int = null
	, @DISPLAY int = null
	, @ADDITIONAL_NOTES varchar(500) = null
	, @Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID smallint = 0
	)
AS
BEGIN

	set nocount on

	declare @ReturnValue int
	set @ReturnValue = @Q_MUSIC_CHART_ID 

	if @Q_MUSIC_CHART_ID = 0 
	begin

		insert into Q_MUSIC_CHART_T
			( Q_ALBUM_ID
			, CHART_POSITION
			, Q_AWARD_ID
			, COUNTRY_ID
			, USER_ID
			, DISPLAY
			, ADDITIONAL_NOTES
			, Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID
			)
		values
			( @Q_ALBUM_ID
			, @CHART_POSITION
			, @Q_AWARD_ID
			, @COUNTRY_ID
			, @USER_ID
			, @DISPLAY
			, @ADDITIONAL_NOTES
			, @Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID
			)
	
		set @ReturnValue = scope_identity()

	end
	else
	begin
	
		update Q_MUSIC_CHART_T with (rowlock)
			set Q_ALBUM_ID = @Q_ALBUM_ID
			, CHART_POSITION = @CHART_POSITION
			, Q_AWARD_ID = @Q_AWARD_ID
			, COUNTRY_ID = @COUNTRY_ID
			, USER_ID = @USER_ID
			, DISPLAY = @DISPLAY
			, ADDITIONAL_NOTES = @ADDITIONAL_NOTES
			, Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID = @Q_ALBUM_SONG_ID
		where 
			Q_MUSIC_CHART_ID = @Q_MUSIC_CHART_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue
--	exec C:\webs_richard\components\UnifiedASPCodeGeneratorSourceVB.Net2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASP Code Generator Source VB.Net 2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASPCodeGenerator\outputQ_MUSIC_CHART_T_Get @ReturnValue

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_NEWS_ADD_OTHER_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWS_ADD_OTHER_SP] 
@TITLE VARCHAR(150),
@ARTICLE varchar(MAX),
@USER_ID INT,
@ACCESS TINYINT,
@QUEEN_ONLINE TINYINT,
@SOURCE_URL VARCHAR(75),
@THEDATE SMALLDATETIME
AS

IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT NEWS_ID FROM NEWS_T WHERE SOURCE_URL = @SOURCE_URL OR TITLE = @TITLE )	
	BEGIN
		INSERT INTO NEWS_T
		(
		TITLE,
		ARTICLE,
		USER_ID,
		DISPLAY,
		QUEEN_ONLINE,
		SOURCE_URL,
	 	[DATE]
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@TITLE,
		@ARTICLE,
		@USER_ID,
		@ACCESS,
		@QUEEN_ONLINE,
		@SOURCE_URL,
		@THEDATE
		)
	
SELECT @@identity
RETURN @@identity
end

else

return 0
GO

SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWS_ADD_SP] 
@TITLE VARCHAR(150),
@EXCERPT VARCHAR(800),
@ARTICLE varchar(MAX),
@USER_ID INT,
@ACCESS TINYINT,
@QUEEN_ONLINE TINYINT
AS

	
		INSERT INTO NEWS_T
		(
		TITLE,
		EXCERPT,
		ARTICLE,
		USER_ID,
		DISPLAY,
		QUEEN_ONLINE
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@TITLE,
		@EXCERPT,
		@ARTICLE,
		@USER_ID,
		@ACCESS,
		0
		)
	
SELECT @@identity
RETURN @@identity
GO

GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWS_BY_YEAR_AND_MONTH_SP]
@THEYEAR SMALLINT
  AS
SELECT DISTINCT TOP 100 PERCENT YEAR([DATE]) AS THEYEAR, MONTH([DATE]) AS THEMONTH
FROM         dbo.NEWS_T
WHERE YEAR([DATE]) = @THEYEAR
GROUP BY YEAR([DATE]), MONTH([DATE])
ORDER BY THEMONTH asc
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS OFF

GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWS_BY_YEAR_MONTH_SP] 
AS
SELECT DISTINCT TOP 100 PERCENT YEAR([DATE]) AS THEYEAR, MONTH([DATE]) AS THEMONTH
FROM         dbo.NEWS_T
GROUP BY YEAR([DATE]), MONTH([DATE])
ORDER BY THEYEAR DESC, THEMONTH DESC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWS_BY_YEAR_SP]
  AS
SELECT DISTINCT TOP 100 PERCENT YEAR([DATE]) AS THEYEAR
FROM         dbo.NEWS_T
GROUP BY YEAR([DATE])
ORDER BY THEYEAR DESC

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_NEWS_EXISTS_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWS_EXISTS_SP]
@URL VARCHAR(75)
 AS
Declare 	@RETURNVALUE TINYINT

IF EXISTS(SELECT NEWS_ID FROM NEWS_T WHERE SOURCE_URL = @URL)
	BEGIN
		SET @RETURNVALUE = 1
	--	PRINT('EXISTS')
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		SET @RETURNVALUE = 0
	--	PRINT('DOES NOT EXIST')
	END

SELECT @RETURNVALUE
RETURN @RETURNVALUE
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_NEWS_FORUM_TALK_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWS_FORUM_TALK_SP]
@NEWS_ID INT
 AS

DECLARE @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID INT

SELECT @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID =  dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID
FROM       dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T 
WHERE NEWS_ID = @NEWS_ID

SELECT     dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.USER_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_DATE, 
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_MESSAGE, dbo.USERS_T.ONLINE_NOW AS ONLINE, dbo.USERS_T.DISPLAY_MESSAGE, 
                      dbo.Q_USERS_AVATAR_V.AVATAR, NUMBER_OF_POSTS
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.USER_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_USERS_AVATAR_V ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_USERS_AVATAR_V.USER_ID
WHERE 
--Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID OR 
Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID AND TOPIC_STARTER = 0
ORDER BY Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID ASC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWS_LIST_UNVALIDATED_SP]
 AS
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT dbo.NEWS_T.TITLE, dbo.NEWS_T.NEWS_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.NEWS_T.EXCERPT, dbo.NEWS_T.ARTICLE, 
                      dbo.NEWS_T.USER_ID AS Expr1, dbo.NEWS_T.[DATE], dbo.NEWS_T.DISPLAY

                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.NEWS_T.USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID

GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWS_MONTH_AND_YEAR_BIO_SP]
@THEMONTH SMALLINT,
@THEYEAR SMALLINT
 AS


SELECT     NEWS_ID, TITLE, [DATE], EXCERPT
FROM         dbo.NEWS_T
where display = 1 and (MONTH([DATE]) = @THEMONTH) AND  ((YEAR([DATE]) = @THEYEAR))
ORDER BY [DATE] ASC
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_NEWS_RSS_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWS_RSS_SP]
 AS
SELECT  TOP 25   dbo.NEWS_T.TITLE, SUBSTRING(dbo.NEWS_T.ARTICLE, 1, 400) + ' [Read More at Queenzone.com ] '  AS ARTICLE_TRIM, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.NEWS_T.NEWS_ID, [DATE], TITLE + '.aspx' AS rsslinkTitle
FROM         dbo.NEWS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.NEWS_T.USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID
WHERE DISPLAY = 1
ORDER BY NEWS_ID DESC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWS_UPDATE_SP]
	
	(
	@TITLE VARCHAR(150),
	@ARTICLE varchar(MAX),
	@NEWS_ID INT
	)
	
AS

	/* SET NOCOUNT ON */
	
	UPDATE NEWS_T
	SET
	TITLE = @TITLE,
	ARTICLE = @ARTICLE,
	DISPLAY = 1
	WHERE NEWS_ID = @NEWS_ID
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWS_UPDATE_TITLE_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@id int

AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here

update NEWS_T
set TITLE = TITLE + ' ' + cast(@id as varchar(5))

--print(TITLE + ' ' + cast(@id as varchar(5)))

where NEWS_ID = cast(@id as int)


select title from NEWS_T where NEWS_ID = @id
END

GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWS_VIEW_PAGE_SP]
	@CurrentPage As int,
	@PageSize As int,	 
	@TotalRecords int OUTPUT
	As
-- Turn off count return.
Set NoCount On
-- Declare variables.
Declare @FirstRec int
Declare @LastRec int
-- Initialize variables.
Set @FirstRec = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize
Set @LastRec = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize + 1)
-- Create a temp table to hold the current page of data
-- Add an ID column to count the records
DECLARE @TempTable Table
(
ID int IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
NEWS_ID int,
TITLE VARCHAR(150),
EXCERPT VARCHAR(800),
thedate smalldatetime
)
--Fill the temp table with the reminders
Insert Into @TempTable 
(
NEWS_ID,
TITLE,
EXCERPT,
thedate
)
SELECT NEWS_ID, TITLE, substring(dbo.RemoveHTML(article), 1, 300) as EXCERPT, [date]
FROM         NEWS_T
WHERE DISPLAY = 1
ORDER BY news_id DESC
--Select one page of data based on the record numbers above
Select 
NEWS_ID, TITLE, EXCERPT, thedate
FROM
@TempTable
Where 
Id > @FirstRec 
And Id < @LastRec
ORDER BY news_id DESC
--Return the total number of records available as an output parameter
Select
@TotalRecords = Count(*)
From 
NEWS_T
RETURN @TotalRecords
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_NEWSLETTER_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_NEWSLETTER_SP]
@EMAIL VARCHAR(100),
@SUBSCRIBE TINYINT
AS
IF @SUBSCRIBE = 1
	BEGIN
		IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT SUBSCRIBER_ID FROM MAIL_SUBSCRIBERS_T where E_ADDRESS = @EMAIL)
			BEGIN
				INSERT INTO
				MAIL_SUBSCRIBERS_T
				(
				 E_ADDRESS
				)
				VALUES
				(
				@EMAIL
				)
			END 
	END  
ELSE
	BEGIN
		DELETE FROM MAIL_SUBSCRIBERS_T where E_ADDRESS = @EMAIL
	END
GO

CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Q_ONLINE_COUNTRY_ADD_SP]

BEGIN
	Insert Into Q_ONLINE_COUNTRY_T
		([COUNTRY_NAME], FLAG_URL)
	Values
		(@COUNTRY_NAME, @FLAG_URL)
END

SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PIC_CAT_PAGE_SP]
	
	@CurrentPage As int,
	@PageSize As int,	 
	@CAT_ID INT,
	@TotalRecords int OUTPUT
	As
-- Turn off count return.
Set NoCount On
-- Declare variables.
Declare @FirstRec int
Declare @LastRec int
-- Initialize variables.
Set @FirstRec = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize
Set @LastRec = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize + 1)
-- Create a temp table to hold the current page of data
-- Add an ID column to count the records
DECLARE @TempTable Table
(
ID int IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
NAME VARCHAR(150),
DATE_TIME DATETIME,
URL VARCHAR(255),
THUMB_URL VARCHAR(255),
T_HEIGHT SMALLINT,
T_WIDTH SMALLINT,
USER_ID INT,
USERNAME varchar(65),
pic_id int
)
--Fill the temp table with the reminders
Insert Into @TempTable 
(
NAME,
DATE_TIME,
URL,
THUMB_URL,
T_HEIGHT,
T_WIDTH,
USER_ID,
USERNAME,
PIC_ID
)
SELECT PIC_FILES_T.Name, PIC_FILES_T.Date_time, PIC_FILES_T.Url, PIC_FILES_T.Thumb_URL, PIC_FILES_T.t_height, PIC_FILES_T.t_width, USERS_T.USER_ID, USERS_T.USERNAME, pic_id 
FROM USERS_T INNER JOIN PIC_FILES_T ON USERS_T.USER_ID = PIC_FILES_T.user_id 
where Cat_Id= @CAT_ID AND DISPLAY=1 order by date_time Desc
--Select one page of data based on the record numbers above
Select 
NAME,
DATE_TIME,
URL,
THUMB_URL,
T_HEIGHT,
T_WIDTH,
USER_ID,
USERNAME,
pic_id
FROM
@TempTable
Where 
ID > @FirstRec 
And ID < @LastRec
 ORDER BY ID ASC
--Return the total number of records available as an output parameter
Select
@TotalRecords = Count(*)
From 
PIC_FILES_T
where Cat_Id= @CAT_ID AND DISPLAY=1
RETURN @TotalRecords
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PIC_CAT_PAGE2_SP]
	@CurrentPage As int,
	@PageSize As int,	 
	@CAT_ID INT,
	@TotalRecords int OUTPUT,
	@CATEGORY_NAME VARCHAR(50) OUTPUT
	As
-- Turn off count return.
Set NoCount On
-- Declare variables.
Declare @FirstRec int
Declare @LastRec int
-- Initialize variables.
Set @FirstRec = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize
Set @LastRec = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize + 1)
-- Create a temp table to hold the current page of data
-- Add an ID column to count the records
DECLARE @TempTable Table
(
ID int IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,
NAME VARCHAR(150),
DATE_TIME DATETIME,
URL VARCHAR(255),
THUMB_URL VARCHAR(255),
T_HEIGHT SMALLINT,
T_WIDTH SMALLINT,
USER_ID INT,
USERNAME varchar(65),
pic_id int,
category_name varchar(50)
)
--Fill the temp table with the reminders
Insert Into @TempTable 
(
NAME,
DATE_TIME,
URL,
THUMB_URL,
T_HEIGHT,
T_WIDTH,
USER_ID,
USERNAME,
PIC_ID,
category_name
)
SELECT distinct    dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Name, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Date_time, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Url, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Thumb_URL, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.t_height, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.t_width, 
                      dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.PIC_ID, dbo.PIC_CAT_T.Name AS category_name
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.PIC_FILES_T ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.PIC_FILES_T.user_id INNER JOIN
                      dbo.PIC_CAT_T ON dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Cat_ID = dbo.PIC_CAT_T.Cat_ID
WHERE     (dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Cat_ID = @CAT_ID) AND (dbo.PIC_FILES_T.DISPLAY = 1)
ORDER BY dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Date_time DESC
--Select one page of data based on the record numbers above
Select 
distinct
NAME,
DATE_TIME,
URL,
THUMB_URL,
T_HEIGHT,
T_WIDTH,
USER_ID,
USERNAME,
pic_id,
category_name
FROM
@TempTable
Where 
ID > @FirstRec 
And ID < @LastRec
 ORDER BY pic_ID ASC
--Return the total number of records available as an output parameter
Select
@TotalRecords = Count(*)
FROM         dbo.PIC_FILES_T
where .PIC_FILES_T.Cat_Id= @CAT_ID AND DISPLAY=1

Select @CATEGORY_NAME = [name]
from pic_cat_t
where cat_id = @cat_id


RETURN @TotalRecords

Return @CATEGORY_NAME
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_PIC_SHOW_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PIC_SHOW_SP] 
@PIC_ID INT
AS
SELECT  distinct   TOP 1 USERS_T.USER_ID, USERS_T.USERNAME, PIC_FILES_T.Name, PIC_FILES_T.Url, PIC_CAT_T.Name AS CATEGORY_NAME, PIC_FILES_T.Cat_ID, 
                      COUNT(Q_PIC_RATING_T.Q_PIC_ID) AS RATING_COUNT, ISNULL(SUM(Q_PIC_RATING_T.Q_PIC_RATING) / COUNT(Q_PIC_RATING_T.Q_PIC_ID), '0') AS RATING, 
                      PIC_FILES_T.Thumb_URL, PIC_FILES_T.t_height, PIC_FILES_T.t_width, PIC_FILES_T.PIC_HEIGHT, PIC_FILES_T.PIC_WIDTH
FROM         PIC_FILES_T INNER JOIN
                      USERS_T ON PIC_FILES_T.user_id = USERS_T.USER_ID INNER JOIN
                      PIC_CAT_T ON PIC_FILES_T.Cat_ID = PIC_CAT_T.Cat_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      Q_PIC_RATING_T ON PIC_FILES_T.PIC_ID = Q_PIC_RATING_T.Q_PIC_ID
WHERE     (dbo.PIC_FILES_T.PIC_ID = @PIC_ID)
GROUP BY dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Name, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Url, dbo.PIC_CAT_T.Name, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Cat_ID, 
                      dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Thumb_URL, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.t_height, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.t_width, PIC_FILES_T.PIC_HEIGHT, PIC_FILES_T.PIC_WIDTH
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_PIC_VALIDATE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PIC_VALIDATE_SP]
@THUMBHEIGHT SMALLINT,
@THUMBWIDTH SMALLINT,
@THUMBNAME VARCHAR(100),
@BIGHEIGHT SMALLINT,
@BIGWIDTH SMALLINT,
@BIGNAME VARCHAR(100),
@PIC_ID SMALLINT,
@DESCRIPTION VARCHAR(150),
@CAT_ID TINYINT
AS
UPDATE PIC_FILES_T
SET
T_HEIGHT = @THUMBHEIGHT,
T_WIDTH = @THUMBWIDTH,
THUMB_URL = @THUMBNAME,
URL = @BIGNAME,
DISPLAY = 1,
CAT_ID = @CAT_ID,
[NAME] = @DESCRIPTION
WHERE PIC_ID = @PIC_ID

select @pic_id
Return @pic_id


--SELECT @@IDENTITY
--RETURN @@IDENTITY
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_PICS_VALIDATE_DISPLAY_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PICS_VALIDATE_DISPLAY_SP]
AS
SELECT  distinct   dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Name, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.PIC_ID, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Url, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Cat_ID, 
                      dbo.PIC_CAT_T.Name AS CATEGORY_NAME, date_time
FROM         dbo.PIC_FILES_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.PIC_FILES_T.user_id = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.PIC_CAT_T ON dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Cat_ID = dbo.PIC_CAT_T.Cat_ID
WHERE     (dbo.PIC_FILES_T.DISPLAY = 0) order by date_time asc
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_PICTURE_CAT_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PICTURE_CAT_SP] AS
SELECT PIC_CAT_T.Cat_ID, PIC_CAT_T.name, PIC_CAT_T.THEDATE, Count(PIC_FILES_T.PIC_ID) AS [Sum Of PIC_ID]
FROM PIC_FILES_T INNER JOIN PIC_CAT_T ON PIC_FILES_T.Cat_ID = PIC_CAT_T.Cat_ID
GROUP BY PIC_CAT_T.Cat_ID, PIC_CAT_T.THEDATE, PIC_CAT_T.name
ORDER BY PIC_CAT_T.name;
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PICTURE_CATEGORY_SP]

select distinct cat_id, name from pic_cat_t
order by name asc

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO

GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PICTURE_RANDOM_BY_CAT_SP] 
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@PIC_CAT_ID TINYINT

AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT     TOP 3 PIC_ID, Name, Url, Thumb_URL, t_height, t_width
FROM         PIC_FILES_T
WHERE     (DISPLAY = 1) AND (Cat_ID = @PIC_CAT_ID)
ORDER BY NEWID()

END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PICTURES_FRONT_SP] 
AS
SELECT  distinct   TOP 4 PIC_FILES_T.Name, PIC_FILES_T.PIC_ID, PIC_FILES_T.Thumb_URL, PIC_FILES_T.t_height, PIC_FILES_T.t_width, PIC_FILES_T.Url, USERS_T.USER_ID, PIC_FILES_T.Date_time,
                      USERS_T.USERNAME, PIC_CAT_T.Name AS CATEGORY_NAME
FROM         PIC_FILES_T INNER JOIN
                      USERS_T ON PIC_FILES_T.user_id = USERS_T.USER_ID INNER JOIN
                      PIC_CAT_T ON PIC_FILES_T.Cat_ID = PIC_CAT_T.Cat_ID
WHERE     (PIC_FILES_T.DISPLAY = 1)
ORDER BY PIC_FILES_T.Date_time DESC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PM_ADD_SP]
@TO_ID varchar(25),
@FROM_ID INT,
@SUBJECT VARCHAR(80),
@MESSAGE VARCHAR(2000)
--@Q_PM_ID INT
AS
DECLARE @@USER_ID INT
DECLARE @@RETURNVALUE INT
SET @@RETURNVALUE = 0
SET  @@USER_ID = (SELECT USER_ID FROM
USERS_T
WHERE USERNAME = @TO_ID)
IF @@USER_ID <> 0 
	BEGIN
INSERT INTO Q_PM_T
(
TO_ID,
FROM_ID,
SUBJECT,
MESSAGE
)
VALUES
(
@@USER_ID,
@FROM_ID,
@SUBJECT,
@MESSAGE
)
SET @@RETURNVALUE = 1
END
SELECT @@RETURNVALUE
RETURN @@RETURNVALUE
GO

MESSAGE
)

(
@@USER_ID,
@FROM_ID,
@SUBJECT,
@MESSAGE
)

                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_PM_T.FROM_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T USERS_T_1 ON dbo.Q_PM_T.TO_ID = USERS_T_1.USER_ID

	--BEGIN


--	END

-- RETURN @@RETURNVALUE
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PM_LIST_SENT_SP]
@TO_ID INT
 AS
SELECT     dbo.Q_PM_T.Q_PM_ID, dbo.Q_PM_T.FROM_ID, dbo.Q_PM_T.TO_ID, dbo.Q_PM_T.SUBJECT, dbo.Q_PM_T.MESSAGE, dbo.Q_PM_T.DATE_SENT, 
                      dbo.Q_PM_T.ISREAD, USERS_T_2.USERNAME AS SENDER, USERS_T_1.USERNAME AS RECIPIENT
FROM         dbo.USERS_T USERS_T_2 INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_PM_T ON USERS_T_2.USER_ID = dbo.Q_PM_T.FROM_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T USERS_T_1 ON dbo.Q_PM_T.TO_ID = USERS_T_1.USER_ID
WHERE FROM_ID = @TO_ID and SENT_delete = 0
order by date_sent desc
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PM_LIST_SP]
@TO_ID INT
 AS
SELECT     dbo.Q_PM_T.Q_PM_ID, dbo.Q_PM_T.FROM_ID, dbo.Q_PM_T.TO_ID, dbo.Q_PM_T.SUBJECT, dbo.Q_PM_T.MESSAGE, dbo.Q_PM_T.DATE_SENT, 
                      dbo.Q_PM_T.ISREAD, USERS_T_2.USERNAME AS SENDER, USERS_T_1.USERNAME AS RECIPIENT
FROM         dbo.USERS_T USERS_T_2 INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_PM_T ON USERS_T_2.USER_ID = dbo.Q_PM_T.FROM_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T USERS_T_1 ON dbo.Q_PM_T.TO_ID = USERS_T_1.USER_ID
WHERE     (USERS_T_2.VALIDATED = 1) AND (USERS_T_1.VALIDATED = 1) and 
 TO_ID = @TO_ID and receieved_delete = 0
order by date_sent desc
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PM_UNREAD_COUNT_SP]
@USER_ID INT
AS

FROM Q_PM_T
WHERE ISREAD = 0 and RECEIEVED_DELETE = 0  
AND TO_ID = @USER_ID

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PM_VIEW_SP]
@Q_PM_ID INT,
@TO_ID INT
AS
UPDATE Q_PM_T SET ISREAD = 1 WHERE Q_PM_ID = @Q_PM_ID
SELECT     dbo.Q_PM_T.Q_PM_ID, dbo.Q_PM_T.FROM_ID, dbo.Q_PM_T.TO_ID, dbo.Q_PM_T.SUBJECT, dbo.Q_PM_T.MESSAGE, dbo.Q_PM_T.DATE_SENT, 
                      dbo.Q_PM_T.ISREAD, USERS_T_2.USERNAME AS SENDER, USERS_T_1.USERNAME AS TO_USERNAME
FROM         dbo.USERS_T USERS_T_2 INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_PM_T ON USERS_T_2.USER_ID = dbo.Q_PM_T.FROM_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T USERS_T_1 ON dbo.Q_PM_T.TO_ID = USERS_T_1.USER_ID
WHERE
 Q_PM_ID = @Q_PM_ID AND ( TO_ID = @TO_ID or FROM_ID = @TO_ID)
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_POLL_ADD_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_POLL_ADD_SP]
@Q_POLL_ID INT,
@DISPLAY_TEXT VARCHAR(500),
@USER_ID INT,
@POLL_TYPE SMALLINT
--@DISPLAY TINYINT
 AS
DECLARE @DISPLAY TINYINT
SET @DISPLAY = 1
DECLARE @RETURN INT

IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM  Q_POLL_T WHERE Q_POLL_ID = @Q_POLL_ID)
	BEGIN
		INSERT INTO Q_POLL_T
		(
		DISPLAY_TEXT,
		USER_ID,
		POLL_TYPE,
		DISPLAY
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@DISPLAY_TEXT,
		@USER_ID,
		@POLL_TYPE,
		@DISPLAY
		)
	
	SELECT @@IDENTITY 
	SET @RETURN = @@IDENTITY 

	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		UPDATE Q_POLL_T
		SET
		DISPLAY_TEXT = @DISPLAY_TEXT,
		DISPLAY = @DISPLAY
		WHERE Q_POLL_ID = @Q_POLL_ID 
		
		SELECT @Q_POLL_ID 
		SET @RETURN = @Q_POLL_ID 

	END
RETURN @RETURN
GO

	(

		)

		print(@sort_order)

		
		INSERT INTO 
		Q_POLL_ANSWER_T
		(
		Q_POLL_ID,
		DISPLAY_TEXT,
	SORT_ORDER		)
		VALUES
		(
		@Q_POLL_ID,
		@DISPLAY_TEXT,
		@SORT_ORDER		)



	END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_POLL_ANSWERS_SP] 
@Q_POLL_ID INT

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_POLL_VOTE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_POLL_VOTE_SP]
@Q_POLL_ANSWER_ID INT
AS
IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT Q_POLL_ANSWER_ID FROM Q_POLL_RESPONSE_T WHERE Q_POLL_ANSWER_ID = @Q_POLL_ANSWER_ID)
	BEGIN  -- ADD THE POLL ENTRY AND INCREMENT BY ONE
		INSERT INTO  Q_POLL_RESPONSE_T
		(
		Q_POLL_ANSWER_ID,
		POLL_RESPONSE
		)
		VALUES		
		(
		@Q_POLL_ANSWER_ID,
		1

		)

	END
ELSE
	BEGIN --  INCREMENT POLL ENTRY BY ONE
		UPDATE Q_POLL_RESPONSE_T
		SET POLL_RESPONSE = POLL_RESPONSE + 1
		WHERE 
		Q_POLL_ANSWER_ID = @Q_POLL_ANSWER_ID
	END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_PROFILE_BASIC_UPDATE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PROFILE_BASIC_UPDATE_SP] 
@USERNAME VARCHAR(65), 
@COUNTRY SMALLINT, 
@HOMEPAGE VARCHAR(150), 
@PASSWORD VARCHAR(50), 
@EMAIL VARCHAR(100), 
@Q_GENDER_ID SMALLINT, 
@OCCUPATION VARCHAR(60), 
@DATE_OF_BIRTH VARCHAR(10),
@ADDITIONAL_LOCATION_INFORMATION VARCHAR(150),
@USER_ID INT
AS
DECLARE @RETURNVALUE TINYINT
IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT USER_ID FROM USERS_T WHERE USERNAME =@USERNAME AND USER_ID <> @USER_ID)
	BEGIN
		UPDATE USERS_T
		SET
		USERNAME = @USERNAME, 
COUNTRY = @COUNTRY, 
HOMEPAGE = @HOMEPAGE, 
PASSWORD = @PASSWORD, 
EMAIL = @EMAIL, 
Q_GENDER_ID = @Q_GENDER_ID, 
OCCUPATION_JOB = @OCCUPATION, 
DATE_OF_BIRTH = @DATE_OF_BIRTH,
ADDITIONAL_LOCATION_INFORMATION = @ADDITIONAL_LOCATION_INFORMATION
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID
SET @RETURNVALUE = 0
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		SET @RETURNVALUE = 1 
	END
RETURN  @RETURNVALUE
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_PROFILE_PIC_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PROFILE_PIC_SP]
@PICTURE_TEXT VARCHAR(150),
@PICTURE VARCHAR(150),
@PICTURE_HEIGHT SMALLINT,
@PICTURE_WIDTH SMALLINT,
@USER_ID INT
AS
DECLARE @OLDPIC VARCHAR(150)
SELECT @OLDPIC = PICTURE  FROM USERS_T 
WHERE 
USER_ID = @USER_ID
-- print(@user_id + ' ' + @OLDPIC)
IF @PICTURE_HEIGHT = 0 
	BEGIN
		UPDATE USERS_T
		SET
		PICTURE_TEXT = @PICTURE_TEXT
		WHERE
		USER_ID = @USER_ID
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		UPDATE USERS_T
		SET
		PICTURE_TEXT = @PICTURE_TEXT,
		PICTURE = @PICTURE,
		PICTURE_WIDTH = @PICTURE_WIDTH,
		PICTURE_HEIGHT = @PICTURE_HEIGHT
		WHERE
		USER_ID = @USER_ID
	END 
SELECT @OLDPIC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PROFILE_UPDATE_SP] 
@USERNAME VARCHAR(65), 
@COUNTRY SMALLINT, 
@HOMEPAGE VARCHAR(150), 
@PASSWORD VARCHAR(50), 
@PICTURE_TEXT VARCHAR(150), 
@EMAIL VARCHAR(100), 
@SIGNATURE VARCHAR(200), 
@Q_GENDER_ID SMALLINT, 
@Q_ALBUM_ID SMALLINT, 
@Q_MEMBER_ID SMALLINT,
@OCCUPATION VARCHAR(60), 
@HOBBIES VARCHAR(2000), 
@GENERAL_INFORMATION VARCHAR(4000), 
@QUEEN_FAN_SINCE VARCHAR(100),
@EMAIL_YES smallint,
@DATE_OF_BIRTH VARCHAR(10),
@ADDITIONAL_LOCATION_INFORMATION VARCHAR(150),
@EMAIL_PM SMALLINT,
@USER_ID INT
AS
DECLARE @RETURNVALUE TINYINT
IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT USER_ID FROM USERS_T WHERE USERNAME =@USERNAME AND USER_ID <> @USER_ID)
	BEGIN
		UPDATE USERS_T
		SET
		USERNAME = @USERNAME, 
COUNTRY = @COUNTRY, 
HOMEPAGE = @HOMEPAGE, 
PASSWORD = @PASSWORD, 
PICTURE_TEXT = @PICTURE_TEXT, 
EMAIL = @EMAIL, 
SIGNATURE = @SIGNATURE, 
Q_GENDER_ID = @Q_GENDER_ID, 
Q_ALBUM_ID = @Q_ALBUM_ID, 
Q_MEMBER_ID = @Q_MEMBER_ID,
OCCUPATION_JOB = @OCCUPATION, 
HOBBIES = @HOBBIES, 
GENERAL_INFORMATION = @GENERAL_INFORMATION, 
QUEEN_FAN_SINCE = @QUEEN_FAN_SINCE,
EMAIL_YES = @EMAIL_YES,
DATE_OF_BIRTH = @DATE_OF_BIRTH,
ADDITIONAL_LOCATION_INFORMATION = @ADDITIONAL_LOCATION_INFORMATION,
EMAIL_PM = @EMAIL_PM
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID
SET @RETURNVALUE = 0
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		SET @RETURNVALUE = 1 
	END
RETURN  @RETURNVALUE
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_PUZZLE_PICTURE_RANDOM_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_PUZZLE_PICTURE_RANDOM_SP]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT top 1    PIC_FILES_T.Name, PIC_FILES_T.Url, PIC_FILES_T.PIC_HEIGHT, PIC_FILES_T.PIC_WIDTH, USERS_T.USERNAME
FROM         PIC_FILES_T INNER JOIN
                      USERS_T ON PIC_FILES_T.user_id = USERS_T.USER_ID
WHERE     (PIC_FILES_T.PIC_WIDTH > 300) AND (PIC_FILES_T.PIC_WIDTH < 1000) AND (PIC_FILES_T.DISPLAY = 1)
order by newid() 

END
GO

GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_QUESTION_CAT_SP] AS
SELECT Q_QUESTION_CAT_T.Q_QUESTION_CAT_ID, Q_QUESTION_CAT_T.CATEGORY_NAME, Count(*) AS [thecount]
FROM Q_QUESTION_CAT_T INNER JOIN QUESTION_T ON Q_QUESTION_CAT_T.Q_QUESTION_CAT_ID = QUESTION_T.Q_QUESTION_CAT_ID
GROUP BY Q_QUESTION_CAT_T.Q_QUESTION_CAT_ID, Q_QUESTION_CAT_T.CATEGORY_NAME;
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO

GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_QUIZ_ANSWER] 
@Q_QUIZ_ID int
AS
SELECT     dbo.Q_QUIZ_ANSWER_T.*
FROM         dbo.Q_QUIZ_ANSWER_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_T ON dbo.Q_QUIZ_ANSWER_T.Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_ID = dbo.Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_T.Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_QUIZ_T ON dbo.Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_T.Q_QUIZ_ID = dbo.Q_QUIZ_T.Q_QUIZ_ID
WHERE Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_T.Q_QUIZ_ID = @Q_QUIZ_ID
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_QUIZ_BY_USER_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@USER_ID INT,
@ADMIN TINYINT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here

		[Q_QUIZ_ID],
		[QUIZ_NAME],
		[DISPLAY],
		[NEW],
		[USER_ID],

END

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_QUIZ_QUESTIONS_BY_USER_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@USER_ID INT,
@ADMIN TINYINT,
@ASSIGNED TINYINT

AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
    
    if @assigned = 0
		begin
		
    
Select 
		[Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_ID],
		[QUESTION],
		[Q_QUIZ_ID],
		[ADMIN],
		[DISPLAY],
		[USER_ID]
	From Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_T
	WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID OR (@ADMIN = 1 AND ADMIN = @ADMIN)
	
	END
	ELSE
	BEGIN
	
	Select 
		[Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_ID],
		[QUESTION],
		[Q_QUIZ_ID],
		[ADMIN],
		[DISPLAY],
		[USER_ID]
	From Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_T
	WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID OR (@ADMIN = 1 AND ADMIN = @ADMIN)
	AND Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_ID NOT IN (Select 
		[Q_QUIZ_QUESTIONS_LIST_ID]
	From Q_QUIZ_QUESTIONS_LIST_T)
	
	END
	
	END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_QUIZ_T_ADD_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Q_QUIZ_T_ADD_SP]
	@QUIZ_NAME varchar(150),
	@DISPLAY tinyint,
	@USER_ID int,
	@ADMIN_QUIZ tinyint,
	@Q_QUIZ_ID SMALLINT
As
Begin

IF @Q_QUIZ_ID = 0 
	BEGIN
	
	Insert Into Q_QUIZ_T
		([QUIZ_NAME],[DISPLAY],[USER_ID],[ADMIN_QUIZ])
	Values
		(@QUIZ_NAME,@DISPLAY,@USER_ID,@ADMIN_QUIZ)
	
	SELECT @Q_QUIZ_ID = @@IDENTITY
	
	END
	ELSE
	BEGIN
		UPDATE Q_QUIZ_T
		SET
		[QUIZ_NAME] = @QUIZ_NAME
		,[DISPLAY] = @DISPLAY
		,[USER_ID] = @USER_ID
		,[ADMIN_QUIZ] = @ADMIN_QUIZ
		where 
		 [Q_QUIZ_ID] = @Q_QUIZ_ID
	
	
	END
--	Declare @ReferenceID int
--	Select @ReferenceID = @@IDENTITY

--	Return @ReferenceID
select @q_quiz_id
Return @Q_QUIZ_ID

End
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_QUIZ_VIEW_SP] 
@Q_QUIZ_ID smallint
AS
SELECT     Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_T.QUESTION, Q_QUIZ_QUESTIONS_LIST_T.Q_QUESTION_ID AS Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_ID
FROM         Q_QUIZ_QUESTIONS_LIST_T INNER JOIN
                      Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_T ON Q_QUIZ_QUESTIONS_LIST_T.Q_QUESTION_ID = Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_T.Q_QUIZ_QUESTION_ID
WHERE Q_QUIZ_QUESTIONS_LIST_T.Q_QUIZ_ID = @Q_QUIZ_ID

ORDER BY SORT
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_RANDOM_PIC_ADD_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_RANDOM_PIC_ADD_SP]
@DOCUMENT_NAME VARCHAR(100),
@URL VARCHAR(50),
@DOCUMENT_SIZE CHAR(10),
@HEIGHT SMALLINT,
@WIDTH SMALLINT,
@Q_RANDOM_PIC_ID INT
AS
IF @Q_RANDOM_PIC_ID = 0 
BEGIN
INSERT INTO Q_RANDOM_PIC_T
(
DOCUMENT_NAME,
URL,
DOCUMENT_SIZE,
HEIGHT,
WIDTH
)
VALUES
(
@DOCUMENT_NAME,
@URL,
@DOCUMENT_SIZE,
@HEIGHT,
@WIDTH
)
END
ELSE
IF @URL = "" 
BEGIN
UPDATE Q_RANDOM_PIC_T
SET
DOCUMENT_NAME = @DOCUMENT_NAME,
HEIGHT = @HEIGHT,
WIDTH = @WIDTH
WHERE
Q_RANDOM_PIC_ID = @Q_RANDOM_PIC_ID
END
ELSE
BEGIN
-- Get the old RANDOM_PIC name so we can delete it
SELECT  URL  FROM 
Q_RANDOM_PIC_T
WHERE 
Q_RANDOM_PIC_ID = @Q_RANDOM_PIC_ID
-- update the record
UPDATE Q_RANDOM_PIC_T
SET
DOCUMENT_NAME = @DOCUMENT_NAME,
URL = @URL,
DOCUMENT_SIZE = @DOCUMENT_SIZE,
UPLOAD_DATE = GETDATE(),
HEIGHT = @HEIGHT,
WIDTH = @WIDTH
WHERE
Q_RANDOM_PIC_ID = @Q_RANDOM_PIC_ID
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_RANDOM_PIC_DELETE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_RANDOM_PIC_DELETE_SP] 
@Q_RANDOM_PIC_ID INT
AS
SELECT URL 
FROM
Q_RANDOM_PIC_T
WHERE 
Q_RANDOM_PIC_ID = @Q_RANDOM_PIC_ID
DELETE 
FROM
Q_RANDOM_PIC_T
WHERE 
Q_RANDOM_PIC_ID = @Q_RANDOM_PIC_ID
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_SCREEN_SAVER_T_DELETE_SP]
	( @Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID int )
As
BEGIN
	set nocount on

	delete from Q_SCREEN_SAVER_T with (rowlock) where Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID = @Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_SCREEN_SAVER_T_PAGE_SP]
@CurrentPage As int,
@PageSize As int,
@TotalRecords int OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN

set nocount on

Declare @FirstRec int
Declare @LastRec int

-- Initialize variables.
Set @FirstRec = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize
Set @LastRec = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize + 1)

--Create a temporary table

DECLARE @TempTable Table
(	
ID int IDENTITY,
 Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID int
	, SCREEN_SAVER_TITLE varchar(50)
	, SCREEN_SAVER_DESCRIPTION varchar(500)
	, DATE_CREATED smalldatetime 
	, THUMB_URL varchar(50) 
	, THUMB_HEIGHT int  
	, THUMB_WIDTH int
	, UPLOAD_FILE varchar(30) 
	, UPLOAD_SIZE varchar(12) 

)


INSERT INTO 
@TempTable
( 

--- all paramaters
		 
			 Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID
			,  SCREEN_SAVER_TITLE
			,  SCREEN_SAVER_DESCRIPTION
			,  DATE_CREATED
			,  THUMB_URL
			,  THUMB_HEIGHT
			,  THUMB_WIDTH
			,  UPLOAD_FILE
			,  UPLOAD_SIZE


)
		select 
			 Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID
			,  SCREEN_SAVER_TITLE
			,  SCREEN_SAVER_DESCRIPTION
			,  DATE_CREATED
			,  THUMB_URL
			,  THUMB_HEIGHT
			,  THUMB_WIDTH
			,  UPLOAD_FILE
			,  UPLOAD_SIZE

from
Q_SCREEN_SAVER_T
order by Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID


		select 
			 Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID
			,  SCREEN_SAVER_TITLE
			,  SCREEN_SAVER_DESCRIPTION
			,  DATE_CREATED
			,  THUMB_URL
			,  THUMB_HEIGHT
			,  THUMB_WIDTH
			,  UPLOAD_FILE
			,  UPLOAD_SIZE

-- parameter list
FROM @TempTable
WHERE ID > @FirstRec AND ID < @LastRec
order by Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID  asc

--Return the total number of records available as an output parameter
Select
@TotalRecords = Count(Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID)
From 
Q_SCREEN_SAVER_T




END
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_SCREEN_SAVER_T_UPDATE_SP]
	( @Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID int = 0
	, @SCREEN_SAVER_TITLE varchar(50)
	, @SCREEN_SAVER_DESCRIPTION varchar(500)
	, @THUMB_URL varchar(50) = null
	, @THUMB_HEIGHT int = null
	, @THUMB_WIDTH int = null
	, @UPLOAD_FILE varchar(50) = null
	, @UPLOAD_SIZE varchar(12) = null
--	, @ReturnValue INT OUTPUT
	)
AS
BEGIN

	set nocount on
	declare @ReturnValue int
	set @ReturnValue = @Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID 

	if @Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID = 0 
	begin

		insert into Q_SCREEN_SAVER_T
			( SCREEN_SAVER_TITLE
			, SCREEN_SAVER_DESCRIPTION
			, THUMB_URL
			, THUMB_HEIGHT
			, THUMB_WIDTH
			, UPLOAD_FILE
			, UPLOAD_SIZE
			)
		values
			( @SCREEN_SAVER_TITLE
			, @SCREEN_SAVER_DESCRIPTION
			, @THUMB_URL
			, @THUMB_HEIGHT
			, @THUMB_WIDTH
			, @UPLOAD_FILE
			, @UPLOAD_SIZE
			)
	
		set @ReturnValue = scope_identity()

	end
	else
	begin
	
		update Q_SCREEN_SAVER_T with (rowlock)
			set SCREEN_SAVER_TITLE = @SCREEN_SAVER_TITLE
			, SCREEN_SAVER_DESCRIPTION = @SCREEN_SAVER_DESCRIPTION
			, THUMB_URL = @THUMB_URL
			, THUMB_HEIGHT = @THUMB_HEIGHT
			, THUMB_WIDTH = @THUMB_WIDTH
			, UPLOAD_FILE = @UPLOAD_FILE
			, UPLOAD_SIZE = @UPLOAD_SIZE
		where 
			Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID = @Q_SCREEN_SAVER_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue
--	exec C:\webs_richard\components\UnifiedASPCodeGeneratorSourceVB.Net2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASP Code Generator Source VB.Net 2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASPCodeGenerator\outputQ_SCREEN_SAVER_T_Get @ReturnValue

END

AS

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_STAGE_ADD_SP]
@TITLE VARCHAR(100),
@PERFORMED_BY VARCHAR(100),
@URL VARCHAR(200),
@THESIZE VARCHAR(50),
@DISPLAY TINYINT,
@CONTACT varchar(300),
@Q_STAGE_ID SMALLINT
AS
IF @Q_STAGE_ID = 0 
	BEGIN
		INSERT INTO Q_STAGE_T
		(
		TITLE,
		PERFORMED_BY,
		URL,
		THESIZE,
		DISPLAY,
		CONTACT
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@TITLE,
		@PERFORMED_BY,
		@URL,
		@THESIZE,
		@DISPLAY,
		@CONTACT
		)
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		UPDATE Q_STAGE_T
		SET
		TITLE = @TITLE,
		PERFORMED_BY = @PERFORMED_BY,
		URL = @URL,
		THESIZE = @THESIZE,
		DISPLAY = @DISPLAY,
		CONTACT = @CONTACT
		WHERE
		Q_STAGE_ID = @Q_STAGE_ID
	END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_STAGE_T_PAGE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

-- ==========================================================================================
-- Entity Name:	Q_STAGE_T_PAGE_SP
-- Author:	Richard Orchard
-- Create date:	4/9/2010 5:27:02 PM
-- Description:	This stored procedure is intended for creating paged record sets for Q_STAGE_T table
-- ==========================================================================================
CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Q_STAGE_T_PAGE_SP]
@PageSize int,  
@CurrentPage int,        
@ItemCount int output     
AS 
Declare @UpperBand int, @LowerBand int
-- Get The Count Of The Rows That They Meet the Criteria 
SET @ItemCount = (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM Q_STAGE_T)    
-- Calculate the @LowerCount and @UpperCount    
SET @LowerBand  = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize    
SET @UpperBand  = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize) + 1   
-- -- create a temporaty table     
CREATE TABLE #AllRows(             
RowNumber int IDENTITY, 
	Q_STAGE_ID smallint,
	TITLE varchar(100),
	PERFORMED_BY varchar(100),
	DESCRIPTION varchar(1000),
	URL varchar(200),
	THESIZE varchar(50),
	DATE_ADDED smalldatetime,
	DISPLAY tinyint,
	CONTACT varchar(300),
	USER_ID int,
	ALLOW_RATING tinyint)
   -- INSERT ALL THE Rows that meets the Criteria 
	 INSERT INTO #AllRows ( 		[Q_STAGE_ID],
		[TITLE],
		[PERFORMED_BY],
		[DESCRIPTION],
		[URL],
		[THESIZE],
		[DATE_ADDED],
		[DISPLAY],
		[CONTACT],
		[USER_ID],
		[ALLOW_RATING])
	 select distinct  			[Q_STAGE_ID],
			[TITLE],
			[PERFORMED_BY],
			[DESCRIPTION],
			[URL],
			[THESIZE],
			[DATE_ADDED],
			[DISPLAY],
			[CONTACT],
			[USER_ID],
			[ALLOW_RATING]
	From Q_STAGE_T
	where DISPLAY = 1 
	ORDER BY Q_STAGE_ID desc 
	  -- AND finally select and return desired -Paged- Rows  
	 SELECT RowNumber ,
		[Q_STAGE_ID],
		[TITLE],
		[PERFORMED_BY],
		[DESCRIPTION],
		[URL],
		isnull([THESIZE], 0) as thesize,
		[DATE_ADDED],
		[DISPLAY],
		[CONTACT],
		[USER_ID],
		[ALLOW_RATING] FROM #AllRows WHERE RowNumber > @LowerBand AND RowNumber < @UpperBand 
		order by [DATE_ADDED] desc
	
		RETURN
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_STAGE_T_UPDATE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO



CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_STAGE_T_UPDATE_SP]
	( @Q_STAGE_ID int = 0
	, @TITLE varchar(100) = null
	, @PERFORMED_BY varchar(100) = null
	, @DESCRIPTION varchar(1000) = null
	, @URL varchar(200) = null
	, @THESIZE varchar(50) = null
	, @DISPLAY int = null
	, @CONTACT varchar(300) = null
	, @USER_ID int = null
	, @ALLOW_RATING int = null
	)
AS
BEGIN

	set nocount on

	declare @ReturnValue int
	set @ReturnValue = @Q_STAGE_ID 

	if @Q_STAGE_ID = 0 
	begin

		insert into Q_STAGE_T
			( TITLE
			, PERFORMED_BY
			, DESCRIPTION
			, URL
			, THESIZE
			, DISPLAY
			, CONTACT
			, USER_ID
			, ALLOW_RATING
			)
		values
			( @TITLE
			, @PERFORMED_BY
			, @DESCRIPTION
			, @URL
			, @THESIZE
			, @DISPLAY
			, @CONTACT
			, @USER_ID
			, @ALLOW_RATING
			)
	
		set @ReturnValue = scope_identity()

	end
	else
	begin
	
		update Q_STAGE_T with (rowlock)
			set TITLE = @TITLE
			, PERFORMED_BY = @PERFORMED_BY
			, DESCRIPTION = @DESCRIPTION
			, URL = @URL
			, THESIZE = @THESIZE
			, DISPLAY = @DISPLAY
			, CONTACT = @CONTACT
			, USER_ID = @USER_ID
			, ALLOW_RATING = @ALLOW_RATING
		where 
			Q_STAGE_ID = @Q_STAGE_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue
--	exec C:\webs_richard\components\UnifiedASPCodeGeneratorSourceVB.Net2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASP Code Generator Source VB.Net 2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASPCodeGenerator\outputQ_STAGE_T_Get @ReturnValue

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_STATS_MEMBERS_ARTICLES_BY_MONTH_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_STATS_MEMBERS_ARTICLES_BY_MONTH_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@MONTH tinyint,
@year smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT     COUNT(dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.Q_ARTICLE_ID) AS ARTICLE_COUNT, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME
FROM         dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_ARTICLE_T.USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID
where month(Q_ARTICLE_T.DATE_CREATED) = @month and year(Q_ARTICLE_T.DATE_CREATED) = @year AND DISPLAY = 1

GROUP BY dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME
ORDER BY ARTICLE_COUNT DESC

END
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_STATS_MEMBERS_FAQ_BY_MONTH_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@MONTH tinyint,
@year smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here

SELECT     COUNT(dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_ID) AS FAQ_COUNT, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME
                    
FROM         dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T.USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID
where month(DATE_ADDED) = @month and year(DATE_ADDED) = @year AND DISPLAY = 1

GROUP BY dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME
ORDER BY FAQ_COUNT DESC

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_STATS_MEMBERS_NEWS_BY_MONTH_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_STATS_MEMBERS_NEWS_BY_MONTH_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@MONTH tinyint,
@year smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here

SELECT     COUNT(dbo.NEWS_T.NEWS_ID) AS NEWS_COUNT, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.NEWS_T ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.NEWS_T.USER_ID
where month(DATE) = @month and year(DATE) = @year AND DISPLAY = 1 and dbo.NEWS_T.USER_ID <> 41402

GROUP BY dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME
ORDER BY NEWS_COUNT DESC

END

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_STATS_MEMBERS_PICS_BY_MONTH_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@MONTH tinyint,
@year smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
	SELECT     COUNT(dbo.PIC_FILES_T.PIC_ID) AS pic_count, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.PIC_FILES_T ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.PIC_FILES_T.user_id 
where month(dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Date_time) = @month and year(dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Date_time) = @year
and dbo.USERS_T.user_id <> 41402
GROUP BY USERS_T.USER_ID, USERS_T.USERNAME
ORDER BY PIC_COUNT DESC
END
GO

	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@MONTH TINYINT,
@YEAR SMALLINT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedu
    SELECT     COUNT(dbo.PIC_FILES_T.PIC_ID) AS picture_count, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.PIC_FILES_T.Date_time

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_TEST_SP] 
@SEARCHSTUFF VARCHAR(400),
@USERNAME VARCHAR(50)
AS
DECLARE @STEST varchar(1000)
DECLARE @KEYWORDS VARCHAR(400)
DECLARE @SUSER varchar(35)
DECLARE @USER_ID INT
SET @USER_ID = 0 
		
		print(@searchstuff)
		SET @STEST = 'select distinct q_forum_topic_parent_id from q_forum_topic_t where '
		print(@STEST)
		
		IF @SEARCHSTUFF <> '' 
		--SET @KEYWORDS =  replace(@SEARCHSTUFF, "'", "''")
			BEGIN 
				SET @KEYWORDS =  'contains(*, ''' + convert(varchar,  replace(@SEARCHSTUFF, "'", "''")) + ''')'
				 print @KEYWORDS
			END 
		
		IF @USERNAME <> ''
			BEGIN
				SELECT TOP 1 @USER_ID = USER_ID FROM USERS_T WHERE USERNAME = @USERNAME
				
				IF @USER_ID > 1 					
					BEGIN
						SET @SUSER = ' USER_ID = ''' + convert(varchar, @USER_ID) + ''''
						print('yes')
					END 
			END 	
		IF @SEARCHSTUFF <> '' AND @USER_ID > 0 
			BEGIN
				SET @STEST = @STEST +  @KEYWORDS + ' AND ' + @SUSER
			END 
		ELSE IF @SEARCHSTUFF <> '' AND @USER_ID = 0
			BEGIN
				
				SET @STEST = @STEST +  @KEYWORDS
			END 
		ELSE IF @SEARCHSTUFF = '' AND @USER_ID > 0
			BEGIN
				SET @STEST = @STEST +  @SUSER
			END
		ELSE
			begin
				print('what')
			end
		SET @STEST = 'select  Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, TOPIC_SUBJECT, TOPIC_LAST_POST  from Q_FORUM_TOPIC_NO_PARENT_V where q_forum_topic_id in (' + @STEST + ') ORDER BY topic_last_post desc'		
		print @STEST
		EXEC(@STEST)
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_TIMELINE_T_UPDATE_SP]
	( @Q_TIMELINE_ID int = 0
	, @START_DATE smalldatetime = null
	, @NAME_OF_EVENT varchar(80) = null
	, @DESCRIPTION_OF_EVENT varchar(2000) = null
	, @USER_ID int = null
	, @DISPLAY int = null
	, @THUMB_URL varchar(50) = null
	, @THUMB_WIDTH int = null
	, @THUMB_HEIGHT int = null
	)
AS
BEGIN

	set nocount on

	declare @ReturnValue int
	set @ReturnValue = @Q_TIMELINE_ID 

	if @Q_TIMELINE_ID = 0 
	begin

		insert into Q_TIMELINE_T
			( START_DATE
			, NAME_OF_EVENT
			, DESCRIPTION_OF_EVENT
			, USER_ID
			, DISPLAY
			, THUMB_URL
			, THUMB_WIDTH
			, THUMB_HEIGHT
			)
		values
			( @START_DATE
			, @NAME_OF_EVENT
			, @DESCRIPTION_OF_EVENT
			, @USER_ID
			, @DISPLAY
			, @THUMB_URL
			, @THUMB_WIDTH
			, @THUMB_HEIGHT
			)
	
		set @ReturnValue = scope_identity()

	end
	else
	begin
	
		update Q_TIMELINE_T with (rowlock)
			set START_DATE = @START_DATE
			, NAME_OF_EVENT = @NAME_OF_EVENT
			, DESCRIPTION_OF_EVENT = @DESCRIPTION_OF_EVENT
			, USER_ID = @USER_ID
			, DISPLAY = @DISPLAY
			, THUMB_URL = @THUMB_URL
			, THUMB_WIDTH = @THUMB_WIDTH
			, THUMB_HEIGHT = @THUMB_HEIGHT
		where 
			Q_TIMELINE_ID = @Q_TIMELINE_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue
--	exec C:\webs_richard\components\UnifiedASPCodeGeneratorSourceVB.Net2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASP Code Generator Source VB.Net 2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASPCodeGenerator\outputQ_TIMELINE_T_Get @ReturnValue

END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_TOUR_DATE_ADD_SP] 
	@THEDATE smalldatetime,
	@VENUE varchar(80),
	@CAPACITY varchar(50),
	@SETLIST varchar(4000),
	@FAN_GATHERING varchar(6000),
	@GENERAL_INFORMATION varchar(4000),
	@TICKET_URL varchar(150),
	@GENERAL_COUNTRY_ID smallint,
@Q_TOUR_DATE_ID SMALLINT
As
Begin

IF @Q_TOUR_DATE_ID = 0 
	BEGIN

	Insert Into Q_TOUR_DATE_T
		([THEDATE],[VENUE],[CAPACITY],[SETLIST],[FAN_GATHERING],[GENERAL_INFORMATION],[TICKET_URL],[GENERAL_COUNTRY_ID])
	Values
		(@THEDATE,@VENUE,@CAPACITY,@SETLIST,@FAN_GATHERING,@GENERAL_INFORMATION,@TICKET_URL,@GENERAL_COUNTRY_ID)

	END
ELSE
	BEGIN

			Update Q_TOUR_DATE_T
	Set
		[THEDATE] = @THEDATE,
		[VENUE] = @VENUE,
		[CAPACITY] = @CAPACITY,
		[SETLIST] = @SETLIST,
		[FAN_GATHERING] = @FAN_GATHERING,
		[GENERAL_INFORMATION] = @GENERAL_INFORMATION,
		[TICKET_URL] = @TICKET_URL,
		[GENERAL_COUNTRY_ID] = @GENERAL_COUNTRY_ID
	Where		
		[Q_TOUR_DATE_ID] = @Q_TOUR_DATE_ID




	END 


--	Declare @ReferenceID int
--	Select @ReferenceID = @@IDENTITY

--	Return @ReferenceID

End
GO

                      dbo.Q_TOUR_DATE_T.FAN_GATHERING, dbo.Q_TOUR_DATE_T.GENERAL_INFORMATION, dbo.Q_TOUR_DATE_T.TICKET_URL, 
                      dbo.Q_TOUR_DATE_T.GENERAL_COUNTRY_ID, dbo.GENERAL_COUNTRY_T.COUNTRY_NAME

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_TOUR_DATE_LIST_SP]
@theyear smallint
AS
SELECT     dbo.Q_TOUR_DATE_T.Q_TOUR_DATE_ID, dbo.Q_TOUR_DATE_T.THEDATE, dbo.Q_TOUR_DATE_T.VENUE, 
                      dbo.GENERAL_COUNTRY_T.COUNTRY_NAME, TICKET_URL
FROM         dbo.Q_TOUR_DATE_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.GENERAL_COUNTRY_T ON dbo.Q_TOUR_DATE_T.GENERAL_COUNTRY_ID = dbo.GENERAL_COUNTRY_T.GENERAL_COUNTRY_ID
where year(dbo.Q_TOUR_DATE_T.THEDATE) >= @theyear
ORDER BY dbo.Q_TOUR_DATE_T.THEDATE
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_ACTIVE_TORRENTS_BY_USER_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_ACTIVE_TORRENTS_BY_USER_SP]
@USER_ID INT,
@DISPLAY SMALLINT
 AS
	SELECT DISTINCT 
                      TOP 100 PERCENT Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1.TOPIC_SUBJECT, Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_DATE, 
                      COUNT(DISTINCT Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_ID) AS totalPeers, Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID, 
                      Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_T.INFOHASH, Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.INFOHASH AS Expr1, Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.UPLOADED, Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.DOWNLOADED, 
                      Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.USER_ID
FROM         Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T INNER JOIN
                      Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_T ON Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID INNER JOIN
                      Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T ON Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_T.INFOHASH = Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.INFOHASH INNER JOIN
                      Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T AS Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1 ON Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID
                      WHERE Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.USER_ID = @USER_ID AND Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.DISPLAY = @DISPLAY

GROUP BY dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_DATE, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID, 
                      Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1.TOPIC_SUBJECT, dbo.Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_T.INFOHASH, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.INFOHASH, Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.UPLOADED, Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.DOWNLOADED, Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.USER_ID
ORDER BY dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_DATE DESC
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_COUNT_ACTIVE_TORRENTS_BY_USER_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_COUNT_ACTIVE_TORRENTS_BY_USER_SP] 
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@USER_ID INT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

DECLARE @SEEDING TINYINT
DECLARE @DOWNLOADING TINYINT

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT  @SEEDING = COUNT(USER_ID) 
FROM         Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T
WHERE     (DISPLAY = 1) AND (IS_COMPLETE = 1) AND USER_ID = @USER_ID

SELECT  @DOWNLOADING =   COUNT(USER_ID) 
FROM         Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T
WHERE     (DISPLAY = 1) AND (IS_COMPLETE = 0) AND USER_ID = @USER_ID


SELECT @SEEDING AS SEEDING, @DOWNLOADING AS DOWNLOADING

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_PEERS_BY_TORRENT_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_PEERS_BY_TORRENT_SP]
	
	(
	@Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID INT

	)
	
AS
	/* SET NOCOUNT ON */
	
	SELECT DISTINCT 
	                      TOP 100 PERCENT COUNT(dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_ID) AS totalPeers, isnull(dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, '') as USERNAME, isnull(dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, 0) as user_id, 
	                      dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.UPLOADED, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.DOWNLOADED, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.IPADDRESS, 
	                      dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.CREATE_DATE, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.IS_COMPLETE, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.DOWNLOAD_SPEED, 
	                      dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.UPLOAD_SPEED, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.REMAINING
	FROM         dbo.Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_T INNER JOIN
	                      dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T ON dbo.Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_T.INFOHASH = dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.INFOHASH LEFT OUTER JOIN
	                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID
	WHERE     (dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.DISPLAY = 1) AND (dbo.Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = @Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID)
	GROUP BY dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.UPLOADED, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.DOWNLOADED, 
	                      dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.IPADDRESS, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.CREATE_DATE, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.IS_COMPLETE, 
	                      dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.DOWNLOAD_SPEED, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.UPLOAD_SPEED, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.REMAINING
	ORDER BY dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.IS_COMPLETE DESC, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.IPADDRESS
	
	RETURN
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_PEERS_CLEANUP_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_PEERS_CLEANUP_SP]
@HASH VARCHAR(50),
@IPADDRESS VARCHAR(25)
AS
DECLARE @@UPLOADED INT
DECLARE @@DOWNLOADED INT
DECLARE @@USER_ID INT
SELECT @@UPLOADED = UPLOADED, @@DOWNLOADED = DOWNLOADED, @@USER_ID = USER_ID
FROM Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T
WHERE
INFOHASH = @HASH AND IPADDRESS = @IPADDRESS
PRINT(@@USER_ID)
PRINT(@@UPLOADED)
PRINT(@@DOWNLOADED)
IF @@USER_ID > 0 
	print(@@user_id)
	BEGIN
		UPDATE USERS_T
		SET UPLOADED = (UPLOADED + @@UPLOADED),
		DOWNLOADED = (DOWNLOADED + @@DOWNLOADED)
		WHERE
		USER_ID=@@USER_ID
	DELETE FROM Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T WHERE INFOHASH = @HASH AND IPADDRESS = @IPADDRESS
	END

--select * from users_t where user_id = 6
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_PEERS_UPDATE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_PEERS_UPDATE_SP] 
@USER_ID INT,
@INFOHASH varchar(50),
@UPLOADED BIGINT,
@DOWNLOADED BIGINT,
@IPADDRESS VARCHAR(25)
AS
IF EXISTS (SELECT USER_ID FROM Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID AND INFOHASH = @INFOHASH)
	BEGIN
		
		print('does exist')
		UPDATE Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T
		SET
		UPLOADED = UPLOADED + @UPLOADED,
		DOWNLOADED = DOWNLOADED + @DOWNLOADED,
		IPADDRESS = @IPADDRESS
		WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID AND INFOHASH = @INFOHASH
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		INSERT INTO Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T
		(
		USER_ID,
		UPLOADED,
		DOWNLOADED,
		INFOHASH,
		IPADDRESS
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@USER_ID,
		@UPLOADED,
		@DOWNLOADED,
		@INFOHASH,
		@IPADDRESS
		)
	END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_REMOVE_PEERS_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_REMOVE_PEERS_SP]
	
	(
	@USER_ID int,
	@INFOHASH varchar(50),
	@IPADDRESS varchar(25),
	@UPLOADED BIGINT,
	@DOWNLOADED BIGINT,
	@IS_COMPLETE TINYINT
	)
	
AS
	/* SET NOCOUNT ON */
	
	UPDATE    dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T
	SET              
	DISPLAY = 0,
	UPLOADED = @UPLOADED,
	DOWNLOADED = @DOWNLOADED,
	IS_COMPLETE =  @IS_COMPLETE
	WHERE     ((([USER_ID] = @USER_ID) AND (USER_ID > 0)) OR (IPADDRESS = @IPADDRESS)) AND (INFOHASH = @INFOHASH)
	
	
	
	
	RETURN
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_ACTIVE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_ACTIVE_SP]
	/*
	(
	@parameter1 int = 5,
	@parameter2 datatype OUTPUT
	)
	*/
AS
	/* SET NOCOUNT ON */
	
	SELECT DISTINCT 
                      TOP 100 PERCENT Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1.TOPIC_SUBJECT, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_DATE, 
                      COUNT(DISTINCT dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_ID) AS totalPeers, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID, 
                       dbo.Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_T.INFOHASH, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.INFOHASH AS Expr1
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_T ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID = dbo.Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T ON dbo.Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_T.INFOHASH = dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.INFOHASH INNER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T AS Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1 ON dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID = Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID
WHERE     (dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.DISPLAY = 1)
GROUP BY dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_ID, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_DATE, dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_PARENT_ID, 
                      Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T_1.TOPIC_SUBJECT, dbo.Q_TRACKER_TORRENTS_T.INFOHASH, dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T.INFOHASH
ORDER BY dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T.TOPIC_DATE DESC
	
	RETURN
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_UPDATE_PEERS_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_TRACKER_UPDATE_PEERS_SP]
	(
	@USER_ID int,
	@UPLOADED bigint,
	@DOWNLOADED bigint,
	@INFOHASH varchar(50),
	@IPADDRESS varchar(25),
	@DISPLAY tinyint,
	@UPLOAD_SPEED int,
	@DOWNLOAD_SPEED int,
	@IS_COMPLETE tinyint,
	@REMAINING int
	)
AS

IF EXISTS (SELECT @DISPLAY FROM Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T WHERE (
((USER_ID = @USER_ID AND @USER_ID > 0) OR (IPADDRESS = @IPADDRESS)) AND 
(INFOHASH = @INFOHASH)) )
	BEGIN
	
	print('record exists, so updating record ')
	PRINT(@USER_ID)
	PRINT(@IPADDRESS)
	PRINT(@INFOHASH)
	
	
	UPDATE    dbo.Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T
	SET              USER_ID = @USER_ID, UPLOADED = @UPLOADED, DOWNLOADED = @DOWNLOADED, INFOHASH = @INFOHASH, IPADDRESS = @IPADDRESS, 
	                      CREATE_DATE = GETDATE(), DISPLAY = 1, UPLOAD_SPEED = @UPLOAD_SPEED, DOWNLOAD_SPEED = @DOWNLOAD_SPEED, 
	                      IS_COMPLETE = @IS_COMPLETE, 
	                      REMAINING = @REMAINING
	WHERE     (((USER_ID = @USER_ID) AND (@USER_ID > 0)) OR (IPADDRESS = @IPADDRESS)) AND (INFOHASH = @INFOHASH)
	
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
	
		print('this is a brand new record ')
	
		Insert Into Q_TRACKER_PEERS_T
		([USER_ID],[UPLOADED],[DOWNLOADED],[INFOHASH],[IPADDRESS],[CREATE_DATE],[DISPLAY],[UPLOAD_SPEED],[DOWNLOAD_SPEED],[IS_COMPLETE], REMAINING)
	Values
		(@USER_ID,@UPLOADED,@DOWNLOADED,@INFOHASH,@IPADDRESS,GETDATE(),1,@UPLOAD_SPEED,@DOWNLOAD_SPEED,@IS_COMPLETE, @REMAINING)

	
	
	END 

	/* SET NOCOUNT ON */
	RETURN
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Q_USER_PROFILE_LIST_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_USER_PROFILE_LIST_SP] 
@country_id smallint
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
	
SELECT DISTINCT 
                      dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.LAST_LOGIN, dbo.GENERAL_COUNTRY_T.COUNTRY_ABREVIATION, dbo.USERS_T.ONLINE_NOW, 
                      dbo.USERS_T.ADDITIONAL_LOCATION_INFORMATION
FROM         dbo.USERS_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.GENERAL_COUNTRY_T ON dbo.USERS_T.COUNTRY = dbo.GENERAL_COUNTRY_T.GENERAL_COUNTRY_ID
                      where users_t.country = @country_id and ISDATE(last_LOGIN) = 1
                      order by last_login desc
END
GO
