SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_USER_QZ_STATS_LIST_SP]
@USER_ID INT
 AS
DECLARE @TempTable Table
(	
	ID int IDENTITY,
	USER_ID INT,
	NUMBER_OF_POSTS  varchar(25),
	CREATE_DATE smalldatetime,
	NUMBER_OF_PICTURES SMALLINT,
	NUMBER_OF_NEWS SMALLINT,
	NUMBER_OF_ARTICLES SMALLINT,
NUMBER_OF_FAQ SMALLINT,
NUMBER_OF_TORRENTs SMALLINT,
FanSongs smallint
	)
-- 10
-- Insert the rows from tblItems into the temp.table
INSERT INTO 
@TempTable
( 
USER_ID, 
CREATE_DATE,
NUMBER_OF_POSTS
)
SELECT     USER_ID, DATE_CREATED, NUMBER_OF_POSTS 
FROM         USERS_T
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID

UPDATE
@TempTable
SET NUMBER_OF_NEWS = (SELECT COUNT(NEWS_ID)
FROM NEWS_T
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID)
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID


UPDATE
@TempTable
SET NUMBER_OF_ARTICLES = (SELECT COUNT(Q_ARTICLE_ID) FROM Q_ARTICLE_T
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID)
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID


UPDATE
@TempTable
SET NUMBER_OF_FAQ = (SELECT COUNT(user_id) FROM Q_KNOWLEDGE_BASE_T
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID and display = 1)
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID


UPDATE 
@TempTable

SET NUMBER_OF_PICTURES = (
SELECT COUNT(PIC_ID)
FROM PIC_FILES_T
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID)
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID

UPDATE 
@TEMPTABLE
set NUMBER_OF_TORRENTS
= (select count(q_forum_topic_id) from q_forum_topic_t where attachment like '%.torrent' and user_id = @user_id)



SELECT NUMBER_OF_PICTURES as [Number of pictures], CREATE_DATE as [Joined on], NUMBER_OF_POSTS AS [Number of forum posts], 
NUMBER_OF_ARTICLES as [Number of articles ],
NUMBER_OF_NEWS AS [Number of news stories],
NUMBER_OF_FAQ AS [Number of FAQs],
NUMBER_OF_TORRENTS as [Number of Torrents]
FROM @TEMPtABLE
order by CREATE_date desc
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_USER_SEARCH_SP]

 AS

FROM         dbo.USERS_T
WHERE USERNAME LIKE '%' + @SEARCHTEXT + '%' OR EMAIL LIKE '%' +  @SEARCHTEXT + '%'
order by user_id asc

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_USER_VALIDATE_SP]
	
	(
	@USER_ID INT,
	@email varchar(40)
	)
	
AS

Declare @return int
SET @return = 0

if exists (select USER_ID FROM USERS_T WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID and EMail = @email and NUMBER_OF_POSTS=0)
	
	BEGIN

	UPDATE USERS_T
	SET
	VALIDATED = 1
	WHERE USER_ID =  @USER_ID
	
	
	SET @return = @USER_ID 
	SELECT @RETURN 
	END 
	
	else
		begin
	SELECT @RETURN 
	
	end
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_USER_VIEW_SP]
@USER_ID INT
AS

SELECT     GENERAL_COUNTRY_T.COUNTRY_NAME, Q_GENDER_T.GENDER, Q_ALBUM_T.ALBUM_NAME, USERS_T.USER_ID, USERS_T.USERNAME, USERS_T.COUNTRY, 
                      USERS_T.HOMEPAGE, USERS_T.PASSWORD, USERS_T.ACCESS, USERS_T.EMAIL_YES, USERS_T.PICTURE, USERS_T.PICTURE_TEXT, USERS_T.EMAIL, 
                      USERS_T.SIGNATURE, USERS_T.NUMBER_OF_POSTS, USERS_T.DATE_CREATED, USERS_T.VALIDATED, USERS_T.Q_GENDER_ID, USERS_T.Q_ALBUM_ID, 
                      USERS_T.Q_MEMBER_ID, USERS_T.OCCUPATION_JOB, USERS_T.HOBBIES, USERS_T.GENERAL_INFORMATION, USERS_T.QUEEN_FAN_SINCE, 
                      USERS_T.PICTURE_HEIGHT, USERS_T.PICTURE_WIDTH, USERS_T.DATE_OF_BIRTH, USERS_T.Q_FRIEND_ID, USERS_T.Q_FRIENDS_EMAIL, 
                      USERS_T.ADDITIONAL_LOCATION_INFORMATION, USERS_T.PEN_PAL, USERS_T.REAL_PAL, USERS_T.QUEENZONE_POSITION, USERS_T.LAST_IP, 
                      USERS_T.LAST_LOGIN, USERS_T.UPLOADED, USERS_T.DOWNLOADED, USERS_T.ONLINE_NOW, USERS_T.EMAIL_PM, USERS_T.IP_ADDRESS, 
                      USERS_T.IM_MESSAGE, USERS_T.DISPLAY_MESSAGE, USERS_T.DISPLAY_AVATAR, USERS_T.BGCOLOR, USERS_T.HOW_QUEEN, USERS_T.FAVE_QUEEN_ITEM, 
                      Q_MEMBER_T.MEMBER_NAME
FROM         USERS_T LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      Q_MEMBER_T ON USERS_T.Q_MEMBER_ID = Q_MEMBER_T.Q_MEMBER_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      GENERAL_COUNTRY_T ON USERS_T.COUNTRY = GENERAL_COUNTRY_T.GENERAL_COUNTRY_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      Q_ALBUM_T ON USERS_T.Q_ALBUM_ID = Q_ALBUM_T.Q_ALBUM_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      Q_GENDER_T ON USERS_T.Q_GENDER_ID = Q_GENDER_T.Q_GENDER_ID
WHERE USERS_T.USER_ID = @USER_ID
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_USERNAME_AUTOCOMPLETE_SP]
@PRE VARCHAR(20)
 AS
SELECT     TOP 10 USERNAME
FROM         dbo.USERS_T
WHERE     (USERNAME LIKE @PRE + '%') and year(last_login) >= 2007 
ORDER BY username asc

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_USERS_HI_ADD_SP]
@HI_MESSAGE varchar(2000),
@USER_ID INT,
@HI_USER_ID int
AS

DECLARE @@RETURN TINYINT
SET @@RETURN = 0

IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT USER_ID FROM Q_BUDDY_T where buddy_id = @hi_user_id and ban = 1 )
BEGIN
	INSERT INTO Q_USERS_HI_T
	(
	 USER_ID, HI_USER_ID, HI_MESSAGE

	)
	VALUES
	(
	 @USER_ID, @HI_USER_ID, @HI_MESSAGE

	)

	SELECT @@RETURN = EMAIL_PM 
	FROM USERS_T
	WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID

END

RETURN @@RETURN
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS OFF

GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_USERS_HI_LIST_SP]
@USER_ID INT
 AS
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID, dbo.USERS_T.USERNAME, dbo.Q_USERS_HI_T.HI_MESSAGE, dbo.Q_USERS_HI_T.CREATE_DATE, 
                      dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.THUMB_WIDTH, dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.THUMB_HEIGHT, 
                      dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.THUMB
FROM         dbo.Q_USERS_HI_T INNER JOIN
                      dbo.USERS_T ON dbo.Q_USERS_HI_T.HI_USER_ID = dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_BUDDY_T ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_BUDDY_T.USER_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V ON dbo.USERS_T.USER_ID = dbo.Q_USERS_PICTURES_FRONT_DISPLAY_V.USER_ID
WHERE     (dbo.Q_BUDDY_T.BAN <> 1)  AND   (dbo.Q_USERS_HI_T.USER_ID = @USER_ID)
ORDER BY dbo.Q_USERS_HI_T.CREATE_DATE DESC
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_USERS_IP_ADDRESS_LIST_SP]
@USER_ID INT
 AS
DECLARE @TempTable Table
(	
	
	ID int IDENTITY,
	IP_ADDRESS varchar(25),
	TOPIC_DATE smalldatetime
	)
-- 10
-- Insert the rows from tblItems into the temp.table
INSERT INTO 
@TempTable
( 
IP_ADDRESS, 
TOPIC_DATE
)

SELECT     POST_IP, TOPIC_DATE
FROM         dbo.Q_FORUM_TOPIC_T
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID

SELECT * FROM @TEMPtABLE
order by topic_date desc
GO

CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Q_USERS_PERSONAL_INFO_ADD_SP]
	@ACTIVITIES varchar(2000),
	@INTERESTS varchar(2000),
	@FAVORITE_MUSIC varchar(2000),
	@FAVORITE_TV_SHOWS varchar(2000),
	@FAVORITE_MOVIES varchar(2000),
	@FAVORITE_BOOKS varchar(2000),
	@FAVORITE_QUOTES varchar(2000),
	@ABOUT_ME varchar(2000),
		@USER_ID int
As
--Begin

IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT Q_USER_PERSONAL_INFO_ID FROM Q_USERS_PERSONAL_INFO_T WHERE [USER_ID] = @USER_ID)  
	BEGIN

	PRINT('NEW LINE')

	Insert Into Q_USERS_PERSONAL_INFO_T
		([USER_ID],[ACTIVITIES],[INTERESTS],[FAVORITE_MUSIC],[FAVORITE_TV_SHOWS],[FAVORITE_MOVIES],[FAVORITE_BOOKS],[FAVORITE_QUOTES],[ABOUT_ME])
	Values
		(@USER_ID,@ACTIVITIES,@INTERESTS,@FAVORITE_MUSIC,@FAVORITE_TV_SHOWS,@FAVORITE_MOVIES,@FAVORITE_BOOKS,@FAVORITE_QUOTES,@ABOUT_ME)
		
		END
	ELSE
	 BEGIN
	 
	 PRINT('UPDATING')
	 
	 Update Q_USERS_PERSONAL_INFO_T
	Set
		[USER_ID] = @USER_ID,
		[ACTIVITIES] = @ACTIVITIES,
		[INTERESTS] = @INTERESTS,
		[FAVORITE_MUSIC] = @FAVORITE_MUSIC,
		[FAVORITE_TV_SHOWS] = @FAVORITE_TV_SHOWS,
		[FAVORITE_MOVIES] = @FAVORITE_MOVIES,
		[FAVORITE_BOOKS] = @FAVORITE_BOOKS,
		[FAVORITE_QUOTES] = @FAVORITE_QUOTES,
		[ABOUT_ME] = @ABOUT_ME
	Where		
		[USER_ID] = @USER_ID
	 
	 
	 END
	 
	 

--	Declare @ReferenceID int
--	Select @ReferenceID = @@IDENTITY

--	Return @ReferenceID

--End

--GO
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Q_VIDEO_RANDOM_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT TOP 2 [Q_YOUTUBE_ID]
      ,[VIDEOID]
      ,[VIDEO_TITLE]
      ,[DESCRIPTION]
      ,[OWNER]
      ,[THUMB_URL]
  FROM Q_YOUTUBE_T
  order by newid()
  
  
  END
GO

	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here

AS

	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

print(@SQL)

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
EXEC(@SQL)

END

CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Q_YOUTUBE_T_ADD_SP]
	@VIDEOID varchar(20),
	@VIDEO_TITLE varchar(200),
	@DESCRIPTION varchar(1000),
	@OWNER varchar(50),
	@THUMB_URL varchar(100)
	As
Begin

if not exists(select videoid from q_youtube_t where videoid = @videoid)
	begin

	Insert Into Q_YOUTUBE_T
		([VIDEOID],[VIDEO_TITLE],[DESCRIPTION],[OWNER],[THUMB_URL])
	Values
		(@VIDEOID,@VIDEO_TITLE,@DESCRIPTION,@OWNER,@THUMB_URL)

	Declare @ReferenceID int
	Select @ReferenceID = @@IDENTITY

	Return @ReferenceID
	end
	
End

SET ANSI_NULLS ON

GO
-- ==========================================================================================
-- Entity Name:	Q_YOUTUBE_T_PAGE_SP
-- Author:	Richard Orchard
-- Create date:	6/21/2009 7:24:52 AM
-- Description:	This stored procedure is intended for creating paged record sets for Q_YOUTUBE_T table
-- ==========================================================================================
CREATE Procedure [dbo].[Q_YOUTUBE_T_PAGE_SP]
@PageSize int,  
@CurrentPage int,        
@ItemCount int output     
AS 
Declare @UpperBand int, @LowerBand int
-- Get The Count Of The Rows That They Meet the Criteria 
SET @ItemCount = (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM Q_YOUTUBE_T)    
-- Calculate the @LowerCount and @UpperCount    
SET @LowerBand  = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize    
SET @UpperBand  = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize) + 1   
-- -- create a temporaty table     
CREATE TABLE #AllRows(             
RowNumber int IDENTITY, 
	Q_YOUTUBE_ID int,
	VIDEOID varchar(20),
	VIDEO_TITLE varchar(200),
	DESCRIPTION varchar(1000),
	OWNER varchar(50),
	THUMB_URL varchar(100))
   -- INSERT ALL THE Rows that meets the Criteria 
	 INSERT INTO #AllRows ( 		[Q_YOUTUBE_ID],
		[VIDEOID],
		[VIDEO_TITLE],
		[DESCRIPTION],
		[OWNER],
		[THUMB_URL])
	 select distinct  			[Q_YOUTUBE_ID],
			[VIDEOID],
			[VIDEO_TITLE],
			[DESCRIPTION],
			[OWNER],
			[THUMB_URL]
	From Q_YOUTUBE_T
	ORDER BY Q_YOUTUBE_ID ASC 
	  -- AND finally select and return desired -Paged- Rows  
	 SELECT RowNumber ,
		[Q_YOUTUBE_ID],
		[VIDEOID],
		[VIDEO_TITLE],
		[DESCRIPTION],
		[OWNER],
		[THUMB_URL] FROM #AllRows WHERE RowNumber > @LowerBand AND RowNumber < @UpperBand RETURN
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_T_UPDATE_SP]
	( @QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_ID int = 0
	, @QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_TITLE varchar(50)
	, @QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_URL varchar(100)
	, @SITE_COMMENT varchar(400)
	, @Q_LINK_CAT_ID int
	, @FEATURED_SITE int = null
	, @USER_ID int = null
	, @DISPLAY int = null
	)
AS
BEGIN

	set nocount on

	declare @ReturnValue int
	set @ReturnValue = @QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_ID 

	if @QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_ID = 0 
	begin

		insert into QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_T
			( QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_TITLE
			, QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_URL
			, SITE_COMMENT
			, Q_LINK_CAT_ID
			, FEATURED_SITE
			, USER_ID
			, DISPLAY
			)
		values
			( @QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_TITLE
			, @QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_URL
			, @SITE_COMMENT
			, @Q_LINK_CAT_ID
			, @FEATURED_SITE
			, @USER_ID
			, @DISPLAY
			)
	
		set @ReturnValue = scope_identity()

	end
	else
	begin
	
		update QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_T with (rowlock)
			set QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_TITLE = @QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_TITLE
			, QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_URL = @QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_URL
			, SITE_COMMENT = @SITE_COMMENT
			, Q_LINK_CAT_ID = @Q_LINK_CAT_ID
			, FEATURED_SITE = @FEATURED_SITE
			, USER_ID = @USER_ID
			, DISPLAY = @DISPLAY
		where 
			QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_ID = @QUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue
--	exec C:\webs_richard\components\UnifiedASPCodeGeneratorSourceVB.Net2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASP Code Generator Source VB.Net 2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASPCodeGenerator\outputQUEEN_FEATURED_SITE_T_Get @ReturnValue

END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[RemoveStringFinal]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO




Create Procedure [dbo].[RemoveStringFinal]
	@FIND  VARCHAR(500),
	@REPLACE  VARCHAR(500)

as

DECLARE @TABLE_NAME VARCHAR(500) 
DECLARE @COLUMN_NAME VARCHAR(500) 
DECLARE @DATA_TYPE VARCHAR(500) 


DECLARE db_cursor CURSOR FOR 
 	select  TABLE_NAME, COLUMN_NAME, DATA_TYPE FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.COLUMNS

OPEN db_cursor  
FETCH NEXT FROM db_cursor INTO @TABLE_NAME, @COLUMN_NAME, @DATA_TYPE

WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0  
BEGIN  
       if @DATA_TYPE = 'varchar' or @DATA_TYPE = 'text' or @DATA_TYPE = 'ntext' or @DATA_TYPE = 'nvarchar'
          begin

	    print @TABLE_NAME
            print @COLUMN_NAME
	    print @DATA_TYPE
		
           --EXEC FindReplace @TABLE_NAME,@COLUMN_NAME,'','<script src=http://www.en-us18.com/b.js></script>',' '
	     EXEC FindReplace @TABLE_NAME,@COLUMN_NAME,'',@FIND,@REPLACE	

          end
       

       FETCH NEXT FROM db_cursor INTO @TABLE_NAME, @COLUMN_NAME, @DATA_TYPE
END  

CLOSE db_cursor  
DEALLOCATE db_cursor
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SIREN_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SIREN_SP] AS
declare @nRecordCount int
declare @nRandNum int
-- Create a temporary table with the same structure of
-- the table we want to select a random record from
CREATE TABLE #TempTable
(
  FILENAME nvarchar(20),
  ALTERNATIVE_TEXT nvarchar(100),
  idNum int identity(1,1)
)
-- Dump the contents of the table to seach into the 
-- temp. table
INSERT INTO #TempTable
Select FILENAME, ALTERNATIVE_TEXT From SS_MAIN_PIC_T
-- Get the number of records in our temp table
Select @nRecordCount = count(*) From #TempTable
-- Select a random number between 1 and the number
-- of records in our table
Select @nRandNum = Round(((@nRecordCount - 2) * Rand() + 1), 0)
-- Select the record from the temp table with the
-- ID equal to the random number selected...
Select FILENAME, ALTERNATIVE_TEXT From #TempTable
Where idNum = @nRandNum
GO

	@TITLE varchar(75),

	@USER_ID int

		([TITLE],[MESSAGE],[CREATE_DATE],[USER_ID])
	Values

	Return @ReferenceID

End

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[test_tb_UPDATE_SP]
	( @TEST_ID int = 0, 
		@THUMB_FILE varchar(50) = null, 
		@THUMB_HEIGHT int = null,
		 @THUMB_WIDTH int = null,
		  @PICTURE_FILE varchar(50) = null,

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_T_PAGE_SP]
@CurrentPage As int,
@PageSize As int,
@TotalRecords int OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN

set nocount on

Declare @FirstRec int
Declare @LastRec int

-- Initialize variables.
Set @FirstRec = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize
Set @LastRec = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize + 1)

--Create a temporary table

DECLARE @TempTable Table
(	
ID int IDENTITY,
--- all paramaters
 TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID int 
	, TW_COURSE_ID int 
	, COURSE_CATEGORY varchar(50) 
	, DISPLAY_SEQUENCE int 

)


INSERT INTO 
@TempTable
( 

--- all paramaters
		 
			 TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID
			,  TW_COURSE_ID
			,  COURSE_CATEGORY
			,  DISPLAY_SEQUENCE


)
		select 
			 TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID
			,  TW_COURSE_ID
			,  COURSE_CATEGORY
			,  DISPLAY_SEQUENCE

from
TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_T
order by TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID


		select 
			 TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID
			,  TW_COURSE_ID
			,  COURSE_CATEGORY
			,  DISPLAY_SEQUENCE

-- parameter list
FROM @TempTable
WHERE ID > @FirstRec AND ID < @LastRec
order by TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID  asc

--Return the total number of records available as an output parameter
Select
@TotalRecords = Count(TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID)
From 
TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_T




END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_T_UPDATE_SP]
	( @TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID int = 0
	, @TW_COURSE_ID int = null
	, @COURSE_CATEGORY varchar(50) = null
	, @DISPLAY_SEQUENCE int = null
	)
AS
BEGIN

	set nocount on

	declare @ReturnValue int
	set @ReturnValue = @TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID 

	if @TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID = 0 
	begin

		insert into TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_T
			( TW_COURSE_ID
			, COURSE_CATEGORY
			, DISPLAY_SEQUENCE
			)
		values
			( @TW_COURSE_ID
			, @COURSE_CATEGORY
			, @DISPLAY_SEQUENCE
			)
	
		set @ReturnValue = scope_identity()

	end
	else
	begin
	
		update TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_T with (rowlock)
			set TW_COURSE_ID = @TW_COURSE_ID
			, COURSE_CATEGORY = @COURSE_CATEGORY
			, DISPLAY_SEQUENCE = @DISPLAY_SEQUENCE
		where 
			TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID = @TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[TW_LESSON_T_LIST_BY_COUSE_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@TW_COURSE_ID SMALLINT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	set nocount on

SELECT     TW_LESSON_T.TW_LESSON_ID, TW_LESSON_T.LESSON_TITLE, TW_LESSON_T.DESCRIPTION, TW_LESSON_T.VIDEO_FILE, TW_LESSON_T.VIDEO_FILE_SIZE, 
                      TW_LESSON_T.LESSON_FILES, TW_LESSON_T.LESSON_FILES_SIZE, TW_LESSON_T.DATE_CREATED, TW_LESSON_T.DISPLAY, 
                      TW_LESSON_T.DISPLAY_SEQUENCE, TW_LESSON_T.TW_COURSE_ID, TW_LESSON_T.LESSON_LENGTH, TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_T.COURSE_CATEGORY, 
                      TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_T.TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID
FROM         TW_LESSON_T WITH (nolock) INNER JOIN
                      TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_T ON TW_LESSON_T.TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID = TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_T.TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID
			WHERE 
			TW_LESSON_T.TW_COURSE_ID = @TW_COURSE_ID
		order by
			TW_LESSON_ID
			
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[TW_LESSON_T_PAGE_SP]
@TW_LESSON_ID smallint,
@TW_COURSE_ID smallint,
@CurrentPage As int,
@PageSize As int,
@TotalRecords int OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN

set nocount on

Declare @FirstRec int
Declare @LastRec int

-- Initialize variables.
Set @FirstRec = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize
Set @LastRec = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize + 1)

--Create a temporary table

DECLARE @TempTable Table
(	
ID int IDENTITY,
--- all paramaters
 TW_LESSON_ID int 
	, LESSON_TITLE varchar(100) 
	, DESCRIPTION varchar(500) 
	, VIDEO_FILE varchar(100) 
	, VIDEO_FILE_SIZE varchar(50) 
	, LESSON_FILES varchar(100) 
	, LESSON_FILES_SIZE varchar(50) 
	, DATE_CREATED smalldatetime 
	, DISPLAY int 
	, DISPLAY_SEQUENCE int 

)


INSERT INTO 
@TempTable
( 

--- all paramaters
		 
			 TW_LESSON_ID
			,  LESSON_TITLE
			,  DESCRIPTION
			,  VIDEO_FILE
			,  VIDEO_FILE_SIZE
			,  LESSON_FILES
			,  LESSON_FILES_SIZE
			,  DATE_CREATED
			,  DISPLAY
			,  DISPLAY_SEQUENCE


)
		select 
			 TW_LESSON_ID
			,  LESSON_TITLE
			,  DESCRIPTION
			,  VIDEO_FILE
			,  VIDEO_FILE_SIZE
			,  LESSON_FILES
			,  LESSON_FILES_SIZE
			,  DATE_CREATED
			,  DISPLAY
			,  DISPLAY_SEQUENCE

from
TW_LESSON_T
WHERE TW_COURSE_ID = @TW_COURSE_ID
order by TW_LESSON_ID


		select 
			 TW_LESSON_ID
			,  LESSON_TITLE
			,  DESCRIPTION
			,  VIDEO_FILE
			,  VIDEO_FILE_SIZE
			,  LESSON_FILES
			,  LESSON_FILES_SIZE
			,  DATE_CREATED
			,  DISPLAY
			,  DISPLAY_SEQUENCE

-- parameter list
FROM @TempTable
WHERE ID > @FirstRec AND ID < @LastRec
order by TW_LESSON_ID  asc

--Return the total number of records available as an output parameter
Select
@TotalRecords = Count(TW_LESSON_ID)
From 
TW_LESSON_T




END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[TW_LESSON_T_UPDATE_SP]
	( @TW_LESSON_ID smallint = 0
	, @LESSON_TITLE varchar(100) = null
	, @DESCRIPTION varchar(500) = null
	, @VIDEO_FILE varchar(100) = null
	, @VIDEO_FILE_SIZE varchar(50) = null
	, @LESSON_FILES varchar(100) = null
	, @LESSON_FILES_SIZE varchar(50) = null
	, @DISPLAY tinyint = null
	, @DISPLAY_SEQUENCE int = null
	, @TW_COURSE_ID SMALLINT
	, @LESSON_LENGTH char(5)
	, @LESSON_RESOURCES varchar(4000)
	, @TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID SMALLINT
	)
AS
BEGIN

	set nocount on

	declare @ReturnValue int
	set @ReturnValue = @TW_LESSON_ID 

	if @TW_LESSON_ID = 0 
	begin

		insert into TW_LESSON_T
			( LESSON_TITLE
			, DESCRIPTION
			, VIDEO_FILE
			, VIDEO_FILE_SIZE
			, LESSON_FILES
			, LESSON_FILES_SIZE
			, DISPLAY
			, DISPLAY_SEQUENCE
			, TW_COURSE_ID 
			, LESSON_LENGTH
			, LESSON_RESOURCES
			, TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID
			)
		values
			( @LESSON_TITLE
			, @DESCRIPTION
			, @VIDEO_FILE
			, @VIDEO_FILE_SIZE
			, @LESSON_FILES
			, @LESSON_FILES_SIZE
			, @DISPLAY
			, @DISPLAY_SEQUENCE
			, @TW_COURSE_ID
			, @LESSON_LENGTH
			, @LESSON_RESOURCES
			, @TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID
			)
	
		set @ReturnValue = scope_identity()

	end
	else
	begin
	
		update TW_LESSON_T with (rowlock)
			set LESSON_TITLE = @LESSON_TITLE
			, DESCRIPTION = @DESCRIPTION
			, VIDEO_FILE = @VIDEO_FILE
			, VIDEO_FILE_SIZE = @VIDEO_FILE_SIZE
			, LESSON_FILES = @LESSON_FILES
			, LESSON_FILES_SIZE = @LESSON_FILES_SIZE
			, DISPLAY = @DISPLAY
			, DISPLAY_SEQUENCE = @DISPLAY_SEQUENCE
			, TW_COURSE_ID = @TW_COURSE_ID
			, LESSON_LENGTH = @LESSON_LENGTH
			, LESSON_RESOURCES = @LESSON_RESOURCES
	, TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID = @TW_COURSE_CATEGORY_ID		
		where 
			TW_LESSON_ID = @TW_LESSON_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue


END
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[USER_UPDATE_USERNAME_DUPLICATE_FIX_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@USER_ID INT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

DECLARE @SOMEThING VARCHAR(100)

SET @SOMETHING = (SELECT USERNAME FROM USERS_T WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID)

PRINT('username ' + @SOMETHING)

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
UPDATE USERS_T
SET USERNAME = dbo.TRIM(USERNAME) + ' ' + cast(@user_id as varchar(5))
WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID

END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[USERS_EMAIL_T_UPDATE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO



CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[USERS_EMAIL_T_UPDATE_SP]
	( @USERS_EMAIL_ID int = 0
	, @USER_ID int = null
	, @SMTP_SERVER varchar(60)
	, @SMPT_PORT varchar(5)
	, @POP_SERVER varchar(60)
	, @POP_PORT varchar(5)
	, @USERNAME varchar(20)
	, @PASSWORD varchar(20)
	)
AS
BEGIN

	set nocount on

	declare @ReturnValue int
	set @ReturnValue = @USERS_EMAIL_ID 

	if not exists ( select user_id from users_email_t where user_id = @user_id )
	begin

		insert into USERS_EMAIL_T
			( USER_ID
			, SMTP_SERVER
			, SMPT_PORT
			, POP_SERVER
			, POP_PORT
			, USERNAME
			, PASSWORD
			)
		values
			( @USER_ID
			, @SMTP_SERVER
			, @SMPT_PORT
			, @POP_SERVER
			, @POP_PORT
			, @USERNAME
			, @PASSWORD
			)
	
		set @ReturnValue = scope_identity()

	end
	else
	begin
	
		update USERS_EMAIL_T with (rowlock)
			set USER_ID = @USER_ID
			, SMTP_SERVER = @SMTP_SERVER
			, SMPT_PORT = @SMPT_PORT
			, POP_SERVER = @POP_SERVER
			, POP_PORT = @POP_PORT
			, USERNAME = @USERNAME
			, PASSWORD = @PASSWORD
		where 
			USERS_EMAIL_ID = @USERS_EMAIL_ID

	end
	
RETURN @ReturnValue
--	exec C:\webs_richard\components\UnifiedASPCodeGeneratorSourceVB.Net2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASP Code Generator Source VB.Net 2009-04-18-01\UnifiedASPCodeGenerator\outputUSERS_EMAIL_T_Get @ReturnValue

END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[USERS_T_PAGE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[USERS_T_PAGE_SP]
@CurrentPage As int,
@PageSize As int,
@TotalRecords int OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN

set nocount on

Declare @FirstRec int
Declare @LastRec int

-- Initialize variables.
Set @FirstRec = (@CurrentPage - 1) * @PageSize
Set @LastRec = (@CurrentPage * @PageSize + 1)

--Create a temporary table

DECLARE @TempTable Table
(	
ID int IDENTITY,
--- all paramaters
 USER_ID int
	, USERNAME varchar(40) 
	, COUNTRY int 
	, HOMEPAGE varchar(150) 
	, PASSWORD varchar(50) 
	, ACCESS int
	, EMAIL_YES int
	, PICTURE varchar(150) 
	, PICTURE_TEXT varchar(150) 
	, EMAIL varchar(100) 
	, SIGNATURE varchar(200) 
	, NUMBER_OF_POSTS int
	, DATE_CREATED smalldatetime
	, VALIDATED int
	, Q_GENDER_ID int
	, Q_ALBUM_ID int
	, Q_MEMBER_ID int
	, OCCUPATION_JOB varchar(60) 
	, HOBBIES varchar(2000) 
	, GENERAL_INFORMATION varchar(4000) 
	, QUEEN_FAN_SINCE varchar(100) 
	, PICTURE_HEIGHT int 
	, PICTURE_WIDTH int 
	, DATE_OF_BIRTH varchar(10) 
	, Q_FRIEND_ID int
	, Q_FRIENDS_EMAIL varchar(80) 
	, ADDITIONAL_LOCATION_INFORMATION varchar(150) 
	, PEN_PAL int
	, REAL_PAL int
	, QUEENZONE_POSITION varchar(50) 
	, LAST_IP varchar(15) 
	, LAST_LOGIN smalldatetime 
	, UPLOADED int 
	, DOWNLOADED int 
	, ONLINE_NOW int
	, EMAIL_PM int
	, IP_ADDRESS varchar(25) 
	, IM_MESSAGE varchar(25) 
	, DISPLAY_MESSAGE varchar(130) 
	, DISPLAY_AVATAR int
	, BGCOLOR varchar(10) 
	, HOW_QUEEN varchar(1000) 
	, FAVE_QUEEN_ITEM varchar(1000) 
	, VIEW_ADS int 
	, APPLICATION_NAME varchar(5) 

)


INSERT INTO 
@TempTable
( 

--- all paramaters
		 
			 USER_ID
			,  USERNAME
			,  COUNTRY
			,  HOMEPAGE
			,  PASSWORD
			,  ACCESS
			,  EMAIL_YES
			,  PICTURE
			,  PICTURE_TEXT
			,  EMAIL
			,  SIGNATURE
			,  NUMBER_OF_POSTS
			,  DATE_CREATED
			,  VALIDATED
			,  Q_GENDER_ID
			,  Q_ALBUM_ID
			,  Q_MEMBER_ID
			,  OCCUPATION_JOB
			,  HOBBIES
			,  GENERAL_INFORMATION
			,  QUEEN_FAN_SINCE
			,  PICTURE_HEIGHT
			,  PICTURE_WIDTH
			,  DATE_OF_BIRTH
			,  Q_FRIEND_ID
			,  Q_FRIENDS_EMAIL
			,  ADDITIONAL_LOCATION_INFORMATION
			,  PEN_PAL
			,  REAL_PAL
			,  QUEENZONE_POSITION
			,  LAST_IP
			,  LAST_LOGIN
			,  UPLOADED
			,  DOWNLOADED
			,  ONLINE_NOW
			,  EMAIL_PM
			,  IP_ADDRESS
			,  IM_MESSAGE
			,  DISPLAY_MESSAGE
			,  DISPLAY_AVATAR
			,  BGCOLOR
			,  HOW_QUEEN
			,  FAVE_QUEEN_ITEM
			,  VIEW_ADS
			,  APPLICATION_NAME


)
		select 
			 USER_ID
			,  USERNAME
			,  COUNTRY
			,  HOMEPAGE
			,  PASSWORD
			,  ACCESS
			,  EMAIL_YES
			,  PICTURE
			,  PICTURE_TEXT
			,  EMAIL
			,  SIGNATURE
			,  NUMBER_OF_POSTS
			,  DATE_CREATED
			,  VALIDATED
			,  Q_GENDER_ID
			,  Q_ALBUM_ID
			,  Q_MEMBER_ID
			,  OCCUPATION_JOB
			,  HOBBIES
			,  GENERAL_INFORMATION
			,  QUEEN_FAN_SINCE
			,  PICTURE_HEIGHT
			,  PICTURE_WIDTH
			,  DATE_OF_BIRTH
			,  Q_FRIEND_ID
			,  Q_FRIENDS_EMAIL
			,  ADDITIONAL_LOCATION_INFORMATION
			,  PEN_PAL
			,  REAL_PAL
			,  QUEENZONE_POSITION
			,  LAST_IP
			,  LAST_LOGIN
			,  UPLOADED
			,  DOWNLOADED
			,  ONLINE_NOW
			,  EMAIL_PM
			,  IP_ADDRESS
			,  IM_MESSAGE
			,  DISPLAY_MESSAGE
			,  DISPLAY_AVATAR
			,  BGCOLOR
			,  HOW_QUEEN
			,  FAVE_QUEEN_ITEM
			,  VIEW_ADS
			,  APPLICATION_NAME

from
USERS_T
order by USER_ID


		select 
			 USER_ID
			,  USERNAME
			,  COUNTRY
			,  HOMEPAGE
			,  PASSWORD
			,  ACCESS
			,  EMAIL_YES
			,  PICTURE
			,  PICTURE_TEXT
			,  EMAIL
			,  SIGNATURE
			,  NUMBER_OF_POSTS
			,  DATE_CREATED
			,  VALIDATED
			,  Q_GENDER_ID
			,  Q_ALBUM_ID
			,  Q_MEMBER_ID
			,  OCCUPATION_JOB
			,  HOBBIES
			,  GENERAL_INFORMATION
			,  QUEEN_FAN_SINCE
			,  PICTURE_HEIGHT
			,  PICTURE_WIDTH
			,  DATE_OF_BIRTH
			,  Q_FRIEND_ID
			,  Q_FRIENDS_EMAIL
			,  ADDITIONAL_LOCATION_INFORMATION
			,  PEN_PAL
			,  REAL_PAL
			,  QUEENZONE_POSITION
			,  LAST_IP
			,  LAST_LOGIN
			,  UPLOADED
			,  DOWNLOADED
			,  ONLINE_NOW
			,  EMAIL_PM
			,  IP_ADDRESS
			,  IM_MESSAGE
			,  DISPLAY_MESSAGE
			,  DISPLAY_AVATAR
			,  BGCOLOR
			,  HOW_QUEEN
			,  FAVE_QUEEN_ITEM
			,  VIEW_ADS
			,  APPLICATION_NAME

-- parameter list
FROM @TempTable
WHERE ID > @FirstRec AND ID < @LastRec
order by USER_ID  asc

--Return the total number of records available as an output parameter
Select
@TotalRecords = Count(USER_ID)
From 
USERS_T




END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[USERS_USERNAME_BY_EMAIL_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[USERS_USERNAME_BY_EMAIL_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@EMAIL VARCHAR(120),
@APPLICATION_NAME CHAR(5)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
SELECT USERNAME 
FROM USERS_T
WHERE EMAIL = @EMAIL AND APPLICATION_NAME = @APPLICATION_NAME

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[usp_GetTableSizes]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create procedure [dbo].[usp_GetTableSizes] @sortby varchar(5)='rows',@updateusage varchar(5)='False'
as
/* 
** Date: August 17, 2000
** Author: Neil Mederich
** Purpose: Report row counts and data size of user tables
** Input Parameter: @sortby = column to sort results by ('rows' or 'data' or 'name') 
** Input Parameter: @updateusage = update statistics ('true' or 'false') 
*/
set nocount on
declare @dependency char(1)
if exists(select * from sysobjects where id=object_id('sp_spaceused2') and objectproperty(id,'isprocedure')=1)
    set @dependency='T'
else
    set @dependency='F'
if @updateusage='True'
  Begin 
    DBCC UPDATEUSAGE (0) with NO_INFOMSGS 
  End
create table #sdtt ([name] nvarchar(50),[rows] int,[reserved] varchar(18),
    [data] varchar(18),[index_size] varchar(18),[unused] varchar(18))
select convert(varchar(50),a.name) as tablename into #sdt
 from sysobjects a 
 where a.type='u' and objectproperty(a.id,'istable')=1
declare @x varchar(50), @y varchar(255)
declare cOne cursor for select distinct tablename from #sdt order by tablename
open cOne
fetch next from cOne into @x
While @@fetch_status=0
  begin
    if @dependency = 'T'
      set @y = 'exec sp_spaceused2 @objname=' + @x
    else 
      set @y = 'exec sp_spaceused @objname=' + @x
    set @y = 'insert #sdtt ' + @y 
     execute(@y)
    fetch next from cOne into @x
  end
close cOne
deallocate cOne
declare @z varchar(255)
if @sortby='name'
  set @z = 'select * from #sdtt order by ' + @sortby + ' asc'
else
  set @z = 'select * from #sdtt order by ' + @sortby + ' desc'
exec (@z)
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[W_USER_ACTIVE_PAGE_UPDATE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[W_USER_ACTIVE_PAGE_UPDATE_SP]
	-- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
@USER_ID INT,
@PAGE_TYPE TINYINT,
@PAGE_NUMBER TINYINT

AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here

IF EXISTS(SELECT USER_ID FROM W_USER_ACTIVE_PAGE_T WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID)
	BEGIN
		
		UPDATE W_USER_ACTIVE_PAGE_T
		SET
		PAGE_TYPE = @PAGE_TYPE,
		PAGE_NUMBER = @PAGE_NUMBER,
		ACCESS_DATE = GETDATE()
		WHERE
		USER_ID = @USER_ID
	
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		
		INSERT INTO W_USER_ACTIVE_PAGE_T
		(
		USER_ID,
		PAGE_TYPE,
		PAGE_NUMBER
		
		)
		VALUES
		(
		@USER_ID,
		@PAGE_TYPE,
		@PAGE_NUMBER
		
		
		)
		
	
	
	END

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[W_USER_DISPLAY_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[W_USER_DISPLAY_SP]
@USER_ID INT,
@PAGE_NUMBER TINYINT
 AS
SELECT W_STATE
FROM
W_USER_T
WHERE [USER_ID] = @USER_ID AND PAGE_NUMBER = @PAGE_NUMBER
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[W_USER_UPDATE_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[W_USER_UPDATE_SP]
@W_STATE VARCHAR(5000),
@USER_ID INT,
@PAGE_NUMBER TINYINT
 AS


IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT W_USER_ID FROM W_USER_T WHERE USER_ID = @USER_ID AND PAGE_NUMBER = @PAGE_NUMBER)
	BEGIN

		INSERT INTO
		W_USER_T
		(
W_STATE, 
[USER_ID],
PAGE_NUMBER
		)
		VALUES
		(
@W_STATE, 
@USER_ID,
@PAGE_NUMBER

		)



	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		UPDATE W_USER_T
		SET
W_STATE = @W_STATE,
CREATE_DATE = GETDATE(),
PAGE_NUMBER = @PAGE_NUMBER

		WHERE
		[USER_ID] = @USER_ID



	END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[W_WIDGET_CONFIG_ADD_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS OFF
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [dbo].[W_WIDGET_CONFIG_ADD_SP]
	@W_WIDGET_ID smallint,
	@CONFIGURATION varchar(1000),
	@USER_ID int,
	@PAGE_ID tinyint,
@CUSTOM_TITLE varchar(50),
	@UNIQUE_NAME varchar(100),
	@W_WIDGET_CONFIG_ID SMALLINT
As


DECLARE @RETURNVALUE SMALLINT

IF @W_WIDGET_CONFIG_ID = 0 

Begin

	
	Insert Into W_WIDGET_CONFIG_T
		([W_WIDGET_ID],[CONFIGURATION],[USER_ID],[PAGE_ID],custom_title, [UNIQUE_NAME])
	Values
		(@W_WIDGET_ID,@CONFIGURATION,@USER_ID,@PAGE_ID,@custom_title, @UNIQUE_NAME)

		

	-- Declare @ReferenceID int
	Select @@IDENTITY
	SET @RETURNVALUE = @@IDENTITY
--	Return @ReferenceID

End

ELSE
	BEGIN

	Update W_WIDGET_CONFIG_T
	Set
		[W_WIDGET_ID] = @W_WIDGET_ID,
		[CONFIGURATION] = @CONFIGURATION,
		[USER_ID] = @USER_ID,
		[PAGE_ID] = @PAGE_ID,
		[UNIQUE_NAME] = @UNIQUE_NAME,
		custom_title = @custom_title
	Where		
		[W_WIDGET_CONFIG_ID] = @W_WIDGET_CONFIG_ID


	select @W_WIDGET_CONFIG_ID
	SET @RETURNVALUE =  @W_WIDGET_CONFIG_ID

	END

	RETURN  @RETURNVALUE
GO

	Select 
	--	[W_WIDGET_CONFIG_ID],
	--	[W_WIDGET_ID],
		[CONFIGURATION]
	--	[USER_ID],
	--	[PAGE_ID],
	--	[CREATE_DATE],
	--	[UNIQUE_NAME]
	From W_WIDGET_CONFIG_T
	Where
		[UNIQUE_NAME]= @UNIQUE_NAME
End

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[W_WIDGET_CONFIG_DISPLAY2_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/

GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [dbo].[W_WIDGET_CONFIG_DISPLAY2_SP]
	@USER_ID int,
@UNIQUE_NAME VARCHAR(100),
@W_WIDGET_ID INT
As
Begin
	Select  top 1 
	--	[W_WIDGET_CONFIG_ID],
	--	[W_WIDGET_ID],
		[CONFIGURATION], 
CUSTOM_TITLE
	--	[USER_ID],
	--	[PAGE_ID],
	--	[CREATE_DATE],
	--	[UNIQUE_NAME]
	From W_WIDGET_CONFIG_T
	Where
		[UNIQUE_NAME] = @UNIQUE_NAME AND USER_ID = @USER_ID AND W_WIDGET_ID = @W_WIDGET_ID
End
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[W_WIDGET_HTML_ADD_SP]    Script Date: 22/06/2026 16:16:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[W_WIDGET_HTML_ADD_SP]
	
	(
	
	@HTML_TEXT varchar(2000),
	@W_WIDGET_HTML_ID int,
@USER_ID int
	)
	
AS

declare @return int

IF @W_WIDGET_HTML_ID = 0 
	BEGIN
			Insert Into W_WIDGET_HTML_T
		([USER_ID],[HTML_TEXT])
	Values
		(@USER_ID,@HTML_TEXT)
	
	Select  @@IDENTITY
	set @return = @@identity
	END
ELSE
	BEGIN
		Update W_WIDGET_HTML_T
	Set
		[USER_ID] = @USER_ID,
		[HTML_TEXT] = @HTML_TEXT,
		[CREATE_DATE] = getdate()
	Where		
		[W_WIDGET_HTML_ID] = @W_WIDGET_HTML_ID
	
Select @W_WIDGET_HTML_ID
set @return = @W_WIDGET_HTML_ID
	
	
	END



	/* SET NOCOUNT ON */
	RETURN @return
GO

As
Begin
	Select 
		
		HTML_Text
	From W_WIDGET_HTML_T
	Where
		[W_WIDGET_HTML_ID] = @W_WIDGET_HTML_ID
End
